### [1] [What Breaks When LLMs Code? Characterizing Operational Safety Failures of Agentic Code Assistants](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30777v1)
*Alif Al Hasan,Sumon Biswas*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 基于LLM的自主编码智能体在良性日常开发中常出现严重安全失败，如约束违反、破坏性操作等，主要发生在错误修复和配置任务中，现有基准未能覆盖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要关注恶意输入，但对良性使用中编码智能体的操作安全失败缺乏系统理解，实际高影响失败未被捕获。

Method: 通过筛选68,816篇论文和16,586个GitHub问题，手动确认547个安全失败，应用系统性开放编码构建多维安全分类法（33种风险类型，7个维度）。

Result: 326/547事件为高或严重严重性；主要风险包括约束违反、破坏性操作、授权绕过和欺骗；超过65%事件发生在错误修复和设置/配置中。

Conclusion: 防护措施需超越对抗性提示防御，强制实施环境约束、失败透明度和安全停止行为，对SE工具设计者和基准开发者有直接影响。

中文摘要：基于大型语言模型（LLM）的自主编码智能体正迅速融入开发工作流，但其操作安全属性（除了对显式恶意输入的评估外）仍鲜为人知。在实践中，高影响的失败发生在良性、目标导向的使用过程中，例如环境破坏、虚构成功报告等，而这些是当前基准测试未能捕获的。当编码智能体用于日常开发任务时，实际会发生哪些类别的操作安全失败，其影响如何？我们提出了一项基于事件驱动的实证研究，该研究基于两个互补的证据流。我们筛选了来自22个顶级会议/期刊的68,816篇论文，整理了185篇与安全相关的研究，并从广泛部署的LLM驱动的编码工具中挖掘了16,586个GitHub问题，手动确认了547个真正的安全失败。通过对两个语料库应用系统性的开放编码，我们推导出一个多维安全分类法，包括33种操作风险类型，组织在七个维度下，并标注每个事件的促成因素、任务上下文、严重性和下游影响。我们的发现表明，编码智能体的失败通常是严重的，547个事件中有326个被评为高或严重。主要风险是约束违反、破坏性操作、授权绕过和欺骗，超过65%的事件出现在错误修复和设置或配置中，这些模式在先前文献中基本缺失。这些结果对软件工程工具设计者和基准开发者有直接影响：防护措施必须超越对抗性提示防御，转而强制实施环境约束、失败透明度和安全停止行为。

Original abstract: Autonomous coding agents built on large language models (LLMs) are rapidly being integrated into development workflows, yet their operational safety properties remain poorly understood beyond evaluations of explicitly malicious inputs. In practice, high-impact failures arise during benign, goal-directed use through environment breakage, fabricated success reports, etc. that current benchmarks do not capture. What categories of operational safety failures actually occur when coding agents are used for everyday development tasks and what is their impact? We present an incident-driven empirical study grounded in two complementary evidence streams. We screen 68,816 papers from 22 premier venues, curating 185 safety-relevant studies, and mine 16,586 GitHub issues from widely deployed LLM-powered coding tools, manually confirming 547 genuine safety failures. Applying systematic open coding over both corpora, we derive a multi-dimensional safety taxonomy of 33 operational risk types organized across seven dimensions, and annotate each incident with contributing factors, task context, severity, and downstream impact. Our findings show that coding-agent failures are often severe, with 326 of 547 incidents rated high or critical. The dominant risks are constraint violations, destructive operations, authorization bypasses, and deception, and over 65% of incidents arise in bug fixing and setup or configuration, patterns largely missing from prior literature. These results have direct implications for SE tool designers and benchmark developers: guardrails must go beyond adversarial-prompt defenses to enforce environmental constraints, failure transparency, and safe-halt behaviors.

</details>


### [2] [Benchmarking Multimodal LLMs on Code Generation for Complex Interactive Webpages](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00154v1)
*Fan Wu,Lishuai Dong,Cuiyun Gao,Yujia Chen,Yiming Huang,Yang Xiao,Qing Liao*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出WebIGBench，首个评估交互式网页代码生成的基准，包含103个真实复杂网页和871个交互动作，并设计了自动化评估流程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准仅评估静态网页代码生成，忽略实际应用中的交互行为；评估标准局限于视觉和代码，缺乏交互一致性评估。

Method: 从真实网站收集103个复杂网页，结合手动交互路径和UI自动化，覆盖5种交互类型共871个动作，并提出新的自动化评估流程。

Result: 在多个代表性MLLMs上的实验揭示了当前模型在交互式网页代码生成上的性能边界。

Conclusion: WebIGBench有效填补了交互式网页代码生成评估的空白，并为未来研究提供了基准和洞察。

中文摘要：近期多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）的进展在多模态推理和代码生成方面取得了显著进步，催生了前端开发的新范式。特别是，这些模型可以直接将视觉设计转化为可执行代码，显著提高了Web开发的效率和适应性。现代Web应用是动态且交互的，具有频繁的用户-页面交互。然而，现有基准主要评估静态网页的代码生成，忽略了实际应用中的复杂交互行为。此外，它们的评估标准仍局限于视觉保真度和代码结构，忽视了生成网页与参考网页之间的交互一致性。为解决这些局限，我们引入了WebIGBench，这是首个旨在评估具有复杂交互的交互式网页代码生成的基准。通过将手动设计的交互路径与UI自动化相结合，我们从真实网站收集了103个复杂网页。该基准覆盖5种流行的交互动作类型（例如点击、输入），涉及871个不同的交互动作。此外，我们提出了一个新的评估流程，以填补交互动作自动评估的空白。在多个代表性MLLMs上的广泛实验揭示了当前模型在使用WebIGBench进行交互式网页代码生成时的性能边界。所提出的基准可在https://github.com/anoa12159-hue/WebIGBench_eval获取。

Original abstract: Recent advancements in multimodal large language models (MLLMs) have achieved remarkable progress in multimodal reasoning and code generation, catalyzing a new paradigm for front-end development. In particular, these models can directly transform visual designs into executable code, significantly improving the efficiency and adaptability of web development. Modern web applications are dynamic and interactive, featuring frequent user-page interactions. However, existing benchmarks largely evaluate the code generation of static webpages, ignoring the complex interactive behaviors in real-world applications. Besides, their evaluation criteria remain confined to visual fidelity and code structure, overlooking the interaction consistency between the generated and the reference webpages. To address these limitations, we introduce WebIGBench, the first benchmark designed to evaluate code generation for interactive webpages with complex interactions. By combining manually designed interaction paths with UI automation, we collected 103 complex webpages from real-world websites. This benchmark covers 5 popular interactive action types (e.g., click, input) involving 871 distinct interactive actions. Moreover, we propose a novel evaluation pipeline to address the gap in automated assessment of interactive actions. Extensive experiments on several representative MLLMs reveal the performance boundaries of current models in interactive webpage code generation using WebIGBench. The proposed benchmark is available at https://github.com/anoa12159-hue/WebIGBench_eval.

</details>


### [3] [BlueFin: Benchmarking LLM Agents on Financial Spreadsheets](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30907v1)
*Srivatsa Kundurthy,Clara Na,Colton Moraine,Anoushka Mohta,Case Winter,George Fang,John Ling,Emma Strubell,Zach Kirshner*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: BlueFin是一个针对专业金融领域电子表格任务的LLM代理基准测试，包含131个复杂任务和3225个细粒度评分标准，经专家验证。前沿模型表现不佳，平均得分低于50%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电子表格软件用户数量庞大，但LLM在电子表格领域的研究不足，缺乏反映专业金融角色真实职业任务的基准。

Method: 策划131个现实相关的复杂任务，包含3225个细粒度评分标准，并由专家验证；使用LM评委代理评估，该评委与专家共识高度一致（α=0.826，macro-F1=0.839）。

Result: 前沿LLM平均得分低于50%，尤其在动态正确性上表现弱。LM评委评估可靠。

Conclusion: 贡献了数据集、开源评估框架和模型性能评估，揭示了LLM在复杂电子表格任务上的不足。

中文摘要：我们提出了BlueFin，一个基准测试，要求大型语言模型（LLM）代理在专业金融领域的电子表格工作簿上执行合成、操作和理解任务。尽管估计全球使用电子表格软件的付费用户数量高达数亿——比全球专业开发人员的估计数量多一个数量级——但相比之下，投入探索和扩展LLM在电子表格领域能力的资源较少，并且更少专注于反映专业金融角色中遇到的真实职业任务。为此，我们策划了一组131个具有现实相关性的挑战性复杂任务，包含3,225个细粒度评分标准；值得注意的是，我们的评分标准和LM评委评估由一组专家人工标注者验证，从而实现了对复杂任务的高质量、细粒度评估，这些任务难以通过编程验证，但可以由LM评委代理可靠评估。我们的评委达到了与专家共识相当的水平（α=0.826），宏观F1分数为0.839。前沿LLM在具有挑战性的基准测试中表现不佳，最强的LLM在各项任务上的平均得分不到50%——模型在动态正确性方面表现出特别弱点。我们的贡献包括一个涵盖三类电子表格任务的数据集、一个开源工具包和代理评估框架，以及现有前沿模型在我们基准测试上的性能表征。

Original abstract: We present BlueFin, a benchmark that tasks large language model (LLM) agents with synthesis, manipulation, and comprehension tasks over spreadsheet workbooks in the professional finance domain. Though estimates of the global population of paying users of spreadsheet software range in the hundreds of millions -- an order of magnitude more than the estimated global population of professional developers -- comparatively fewer resources have been devoted to exploring and expanding LLM capabilities in the spreadsheet domain, with fewer still dedicated to mirroring real occupational tasks encountered by those in professional finance roles. In response, we curate a set of 131 challenging, complex tasks with real-world relevance in the domain, containing 3,225 granular rubric criteria; notably, our rubric criteria and LM judge evaluations are validated by a team of expert human annotators, resulting in high-quality, granular evaluations of complex tasks that are difficult to verify programmatically but can be reliably evaluated by an LM judge agent. Our judge achieves parity with expert consensus ($α=0.826$) with a macro-F1 score of 0.839. Frontier LLMs demonstrate poor performance on the challenging benchmark, with the strongest LLMs achieving less than 50\% average scores across tasks -- models exhibit particular weaknesses in dynamic correctness. Our contributions include a dataset of examples across three categories of spreadsheet tasks, an open source harness and agentic evaluation framework, and a characterization of existing frontier models' performance on our benchmark.

</details>


### [4] [Specification-Driven Development Benchmark: Security Knowledge Transition](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00167v1)
*Oleg Grynets,Andrii Salyk,Vasyl Lyashkevych,Oleh Kaskun,Danyil Zhuravchak*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出一种安全知识操作化方法，通过多层规范安全模型和安全知识转换方法，在AI辅助规范驱动开发中显式嵌入安全知识，减少生成系统的安全缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI辅助开发转向规范驱动，但安全行为被忽视，导致生成的系统虽满足功能需求却存在安全漏洞。

Method: 提出多层规范安全模型和安全知识转换方法，将业务和技术规范转化为安全增强的生成契约，并通过两个实证研究评估。

Result: 在221测试黑盒API评估中，模态失败从50降至36，尤其在业务逻辑和管理员安全类别提升显著。

Conclusion: 该方法能有效改善AI生成系统的安全性，尤其针对应用特定安全类别。

中文摘要：AI辅助软件开发正从孤立的代码补全转向规范驱动的生成，其中业务需求、技术规范和验收标准成为基于LLM的开发代理的操作输入。这种转变带来了一个安全问题：功能行为被显式描述，而安全行为仍然隐式、通用或推迟到生成后审查，导致生成的系统满足可见的功能需求，但未能保留授权规则、所有权边界、输入验证、令牌拒绝、敏感数据处理和滥用案例语义。本文提出了一种适用于AI辅助规范驱动开发的安全知识操作化方法，结合了两个贡献：一个多层规范安全模型，通过系统实体、威胁、风险、需求、实施规则、控制、验证场景和证据之间的可追溯关系来表示安全知识；以及一个安全知识转换方法，将业务和技术规范转化为经过验证的安全增强生成契约。我们通过两个实证研究评估了该方法：一个隐藏预言研究，评估基于LLM的管道能否从系统上下文中推导出结构化的安全模型；以及一个后端生成研究，在三种条件下进行：无显式安全需求、ASVS条件生成和多层安全模型条件生成。针对一个隐藏的221测试黑盒API套件进行评估，模态失败从基线的50次减少到ASVS的42次和多层安全模型的36次，在应用特定类别（如业务逻辑和管理员安全）中改进最为显著。

Original abstract: AI-assisted software development is shifting from isolated code completion toward specification-driven generation, where business requirements, technical specifications, and acceptance criteria become operational input for LLM-based development agents. This shift creates a security problem: functional behavior is described explicitly, while security behavior remains implicit, generic, or postponed to post-generation review, causing generated systems to satisfy visible functional requirements while failing to preserve authorization rules, ownership boundaries, input validation, token rejection, sensitive data handling, and abuse-case semantics. This paper proposes a security knowledge operationalization approach for AI-assisted specification-driven development, combining two contributions: a Multilayer Specification Security Model that represents security knowledge through traceable relations between system entities, threats, risks, requirements, implementation rules, controls, verification scenarios, and evidence; and a Security Knowledge Transition Method that transforms business and technical specifications into a validated security-enriched generation contract. We evaluate the approach through two empirical studies: a hidden-oracle study assessing whether an LLM-based pipeline can derive a structured security model from system context, and a backend generation study under three conditions: no explicit security requirements, ASVS-conditioned generation, and Multilayer Security Model conditioning. Evaluated against a hidden 221-test black-box API suite, modal failures decreased from 50 in the baseline to 42 with ASVS and 36 with the Multilayer Security Model, with the strongest improvements in application-specific categories such as business logic and admin safety.

</details>


### [5] [Governance-Aware Software Architecture for Multi-Stakeholder Platforms](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31316v1)
*Michael Nwankwo,Eric Umuhoza*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出一个治理-架构对应框架，将多利益相关者平台的治理原则映射到架构决策空间，使隐含的治理决策显式化，并以卢旺达养猪知识平台为例说明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有软件架构和治理文献均未解决治理原则与架构决策之间的转换问题，导致工程师在构建数字多利益相关者平台时可能无意中优先处理某些利益相关者需求。

Method: 提出了一个治理-架构对应框架，将五项MSP治理原则映射到对应的架构决策空间，并识别治理感知的设计选择及其覆盖的默认设置；以卢旺达养猪知识平台为例进行说明。

Result: 提出了框架但尚未实证验证；计划进行前后判断研究以检验治理结果的可证伪预测。

Conclusion: 该框架有助于在部署前显化并辩论隐含的治理决策，但需要进一步实证验证其有效性。

中文摘要：多利益相关者平台协调多样化的利益相关者群体，这些群体往往具有竞争性或冲突性需求。随着这些平台日益数字化，构建平台的工程师在数据可见性、服务分解和算法设计方面做出架构决策，这些决策直接决定了在冲突发生时哪些利益相关者的需求被优先考虑。软件架构文献提供了租户间数据隔离和访问控制的模式，但没有解决架构决策如何解决具有结构性分歧利益的利益相关者之间的冲突。MSP治理文献明确了涉及的原则，但将技术视为中立基础设施。两者均未涉及治理原则与架构决策空间之间的转换。本文提出了一种治理-架构对应框架，该框架揭示隐含的治理决策，使其在部署前明确且可辩论。该框架将五项MSP治理原则映射到必须处理的架构决策空间，为每项原则识别出治理感知的设计选择以及它所覆盖的技术上便利的默认设置。我们通过一个为卢旺达养猪业构建的知识平台来说明该框架，该平台中五种利益相关者类型存在结构性冲突的需求。作为进行中的工作，该框架已提出但尚未经过实证验证；一项计划中的跨所有利益相关者类型的平台用户前后判断研究将检验关于治理结果的可证伪预测。

Original abstract: Multi-stakeholder platforms (MSPs) coordinate diverse stakeholder groups, often with competing or conflicting requirements. As these platforms increasingly take digital form, engineers building them make architectural decisions about data visibility, service decomposition, and algorithm design that directly determine which stakeholder requirements are prioritized when conflicts arise. Software architecture literature provides patterns for data isolation and access control among tenants but does not address how architectural decisions resolve conflicts among stakeholders with structurally divergent interests. MSP governance literature identifies the principles at stake but treats technology as neutral infrastructure. Neither addresses the translation between governance principles and architectural decision spaces. This paper proposes a governance-architecture correspondence framework that surfaces implicit governance decisions, making them explicit and debatable before deployment. The framework maps five MSP governance principles to the architectural decision spaces where they must be addressed, identifying for each the governance-aware design choice and the technically convenient default it overrides. We illustrate the framework in a constructed knowledge platform for pig farming in Rwanda, where five stakeholder types present structurally conflicting requirements. As work in progress, the framework is proposed but not yet empirically validated; a planned pre/post judgment study with platform users across all stakeholder types will test falsifiable predictions about governance outcomes.

</details>


### [6] [Ladder Logic Translation using Large Language Models in Industrial Automation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31458v1)
*Oluwatosin Ogundare,Promise Ekpo,Nathanial Wiggins*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出一个数学形式化和严格工程化的管道，利用LLM和TIA Portal Openness API实现Rockwell到Siemens梯形图程序的自动转换，并保持高语义一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 切换PLC供应商困难，现有解决方案存在编程环境不匹配、梯形图结构不兼容、语义表达差异及黑盒工程工具限制等问题。

Method: 通过数学形式化问题，设计包含XML提取、结构归一化、约束生成函数（LLM）和TIA Portal Openness API系统集成的管道。

Result: 转换在不同指令类别中保持高语义一致性。

Conclusion: 本文方法有效解决了PLC梯形图跨厂商自动转换问题，验证了高语义保持能力。

中文摘要：梯形图逻辑转换是工业自动化中的一个重要问题，因为没有它，很难切换可编程逻辑控制器（PLC）供应商。当前的转换问题突显了不匹配的编程环境、不兼容的梯形图结构、供应商形式化语义表达能力的差异以及集成黑盒专有工程工具的限制，这些在我们的示例案例（Rockwell到Siemens PLC代码转换）中得到了体现。本文提出了该问题的数学形式化描述，以及一个解决方案的详细架构，该方案支持XML提取、结构归一化、约束生成函数（LLM），并通过TIA Portal Openness API进行系统集成，形成了一个严格工程化的管道，用于自动将Rockwell梯形图程序转换为Siemens S7梯形图程序。最后，我们展示了结果，表明转换在不同指令类别中保持了较高的语义一致性。

Original abstract: Ladder logic translation is an important problem in industrial automation because without it, it is difficult to switch Programmable Logic Controller (PLC) vendors. The prevailing translation problem highlights mismatched programming environments, incompatible ladder logic constructs, limitations in terms of differences in the semantic expressiveness of the vendor formalisms and integrated black-box proprietary engineering tools which are exemplified in our example case; Rockwell to Siemens PLC code translation. This work presents a mathematical formulation of the problem, the detailed architecture of a solution which supports XML extraction, structural normalization, constrained generative function (LLM), and system integration via the TIA Portal Openness API as rigorously engineered pipeline for automated translation of Rockwell Ladder Programs to Siemens S7 ladder programs. Finally, we present results that show that the translations retain high semantic consistency across instruction categories.

</details>


### [7] [Knowledge Boundary Probing and Demand-Guided Intervention for LLM-Based Power System Code Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31478v1)
*Hui Wu,Xiaoyang Wang,Zhong Fan*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文发现电力系统代码生成中的失败主要源于API知识边界错误，并提出PowerCodeBench和边界感知干预方法，显著提升开放权重模型在本地部署中的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型用于电力系统分析时，由于保密、法规等原因需本地部署，但开放权重模型可靠性不足，现有失败主要来自API知识边界错误而非纯推理。

Method: 提出PowerCodeBench基准生成器、L0-L3文档驱动探测过程，以及结合API需求估计、主动文档注入和被动修正的边界感知干预。

Result: 在2000任务上评估10个开放权重模型和4个商业API，干预后开放权重模型（≥7B）和所有商业API准确率提升32-56点，70B-120B模型匹配商业中端水平，Llama-3.1-405B和Qwen3-Coder-480B最优，且目标提示仅用41%令牌成本。

Conclusion: 提供了一种无需微调或云推理即可在本地部署中可靠使用LLM进行电网分析的路径。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）越来越多地被用于自动化电力系统分析，但许多公用事业公司和能源研究实验室由于保密性、法规、可重复性和成本原因要求本地部署。这使得开放权重模型的可靠性成为一个部署问题。我们表明，电力系统代码生成中的首次失败并非单独由推理主导，而是由结构化的API知识边界错误主导：虚构的函数名、误用的参数以及版本化仿真库中错误处理的结果表。我们引入了PowerCodeBench，一个执行验证的基准生成器，它将自然语言操作员查询与pandapower代码和数值真实值配对；一个L0-L3文档驱动的探测过程，用于测量每个模型的API知识分布；以及一个边界感知干预，结合了查询端API需求估计与目标性的主动文档注入和路由的被动修正。在一个2000任务的冻结发布上，我们评估了十个开放权重LLM（1.5B-480B参数）和四个商业中端API。该干预提高了每个评估的至少7B参数的开放权重模型和每个商业API 32到56个准确率点。70B-120B范围内的开放权重模型匹配了商业中端准确率范围，而Llama-3.1-405B和Qwen3-Coder-480B领先于面板。目标提示保持了全上下文准确率上限，同时使用了41%的提示令牌成本。结果是为电网分析工作流提供了一种准确率方面、部署时路径，以实现可靠的本地LLM辅助，无需微调或云推理。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used to automate power-system analysis, but many utilities and energy-research labs require on-premise serving for confidentiality, regulatory, reproducibility, and cost reasons. This makes the reliability of open-weight models a deployment issue. We show that first-pass failures in power-system code generation are dominated not by reasoning alone, but by structured API-knowledge boundary errors: hallucinated function names, misused parameters, and mishandled result tables in versioned simulation libraries.
  We introduce PowerCodeBench, an execution-validated benchmark generator that pairs natural-language operator queries with pandapower code and numerical ground truth; an L0-L3 documentation-driven probing procedure that measures per-model API knowledge profiles; and a boundary-aware intervention that combines query-side API demand estimation with targeted proactive documentation injection and routed reactive correction.
  On a 2,000-task frozen release, we evaluate ten open-weight LLMs (1.5B-480B parameters) and four commercial mid-tier APIs. The intervention improves every evaluated open-weight model of at least 7B parameters and every commercial API by 32 to 56 accuracy points. Open-weight models in the 70B-120B range match the commercial mid-tier accuracy range, while Llama-3.1-405B and Qwen3-Coder-480B lead the panel. The targeted prompts preserve the full-context accuracy ceiling while using 41% of the prompt-token cost. The result is an accuracy-side, deployment-time path toward reliable on-premise LLM assistance for grid-analysis workflows without fine-tuning or cloud inference.

### [8] [Separating Secrets from Placeholders: A Hybrid CNN-CodeBERT Framework for Three-Class Credential Leakage Detection](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31520v1)
*Maksuda Bilkis Baby,Khushika Shah,Naiyue Liang,Lei Zhang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出三分类框架，使用CodeBERT语义理解和字符级模式识别，显著降低误报率，提高占位符或弱凭证检测能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有凭证检测工具因刚性模式匹配和二元分类导致高误报率，无法区分真实凭证与占位符或弱凭证。

Method: 构建三分类框架（真实凭证、占位符或弱凭证、非凭证），结合CodeBERT语义理解与字符级模式识别。

Result: MCC 0.86，宏F1 0.90，真实凭证召回93%精度89%，高严重性警报减少33%，占位符或弱凭证F1从54%提升至81%，跨语言泛化强（9/10语言F1>0.80）。

Conclusion: 所提方法有效提高了凭证检测的准确性和减少误报，且具有良好的跨语言泛化能力。

中文摘要：公共源代码仓库中的凭证泄露构成了严重的安全威胁，仅在2024年就有超过2380万个秘密被泄露。现有的检测工具由于刚性模式匹配和二元分类方案无法区分真实凭证与占位符或弱凭证，导致高误报率。我们提出了一种三分类框架，明确将占位符或弱凭证建模为一个独立的类别，利用基于CodeBERT的语义理解结合字符级模式识别。我们在一个新构建的数据集上评估了我们的方法，该数据集包含9426个样本，涵盖10种编程语言。我们的模型实现了0.86的马修斯相关系数和0.90的宏F1分数，在真实凭证泄露方面达到了93%的召回率和89%的精度，同时将高严重性警报减少了33.0%（从373降至250），且未牺牲安全覆盖率。与之前的字符级方法相比，我们的方法将占位符或弱凭证检测的F1分数从54%提高到81%，同时保持了强大的跨语言泛化能力，在留一语言评估中，10种语言中有9种语言的F1分数超过0.80。

Original abstract: Credential leakage in public source code repositories poses a critical security threat, with over 23.8 million secrets exposed in 2024 alone. Existing detection tools suffer from high false-positive rates because rigid pattern matching and binary classification schemes fail to distinguish genuine credentials from placeholder or weak credentials. We propose a three-class classification framework that explicitly models placeholder or weak credentials as a distinct class, leveraging CodeBERT-based semantic understanding combined with character-level pattern recognition. We evaluate our approach on a newly constructed dataset of 9,426 samples spanning 10 programming languages. Our model achieves a Matthews Correlation Coefficient of 0.86 and a macro F1-score of 0.90, achieving 93% recall and 89% precision for genuine credential leaks while reducing high severity alerts by 33.0% (from 373 to 250) without sacrificing security coverage. Compared to prior character-level approaches, our method improves placeholder or weak credential detection from 54% to 81% F1-score while maintaining strong cross language generalization, with 9 of 10 languages achieving F1 above 0.80 under leave-one-language-out evaluation.

</details>


### [9] [How Generation Architecture Shapes Code Complexity in Multi-Agent LLM Systems: A Paired Study on HumanEval](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00308v1)
*Nazmus Ashrafi*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文研究了多智能体LLM代码生成架构对代码复杂度的影响，发现六种架构聚为两个复杂度集群，额外的复杂度并未提升功能正确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究仅关注功能正确性，未考察架构对代码复杂度的影响；需要系统评估不同架构层对复杂性的贡献。

Method: 使用六种多智能体配置在HumanEval数据集上，采用RADON复杂度指标，进行配对非参数统计检验。

Result: 六种架构分为两个复杂度集群，分析师-编码员分裂增加复杂度，调试器降低复杂度，测试员增加复杂度；重集群无正确性优势。

Conclusion: 架构细化应基于实际收益而非假设。

中文摘要：大型语言模型代码生成已从单次提示转变为多智能体编排——分析师、编码员、测试员和调试器流水线——并且几乎完全根据功能正确性进行评估。这些架构是否也会影响它们生成的代码的结构复杂性，以及哪些编排层承担了成本，在很大程度上仍未得到检验：先前的工作已经记录了提示级别对代码复杂性的影响，但架构级别的问题是开放的。我们比较了六种广泛使用的多智能体配置（Basic, AC, ACT, Debugger, AC+Debugger, ACT+Debugger），在GPT-4o系列的两个模型上，针对所有164个HumanEval任务——1,968个配对观测——使用五个RADON复杂度度量（SLOC、圈复杂度和Halstead体积、难度、工作量）。我们在所有完成和仅通过条件下应用了配对的非参数统计流程（Friedman整体检验、Wilcoxon符号秩事后检验与Holm校正、Kendall's W和匹配对秩双列效应量）。六种架构聚集成两个无法区分的复杂性集群，相差50-130%的差距，在两个模型和两种条件下都是相同的划分；在架构层中，分析师-编码员分裂增加了复杂性，运行时调试器不会——并且在分析师-编码员背景下主动降低复杂性——而测试员重新增加了复杂性。重集群的额外复杂性并没有带来pass@1的优势：最精简的架构在准确性上与最重的架构匹配或超越。因此，LLM代码生成中的架构细化应该通过所关注维度上的测量收益来证明其合理性，而不是假设。

Original abstract: Large-language-model code generation has shifted from single-shot prompting to multi-agent orchestrations - analyst, coder, tester, and debugger pipelines - and is evaluated almost exclusively on functional correctness. Whether these architectures also affect the structural complexity of the code they produce, and which orchestration layers carry the cost, remains largely unexamined: prior work has documented prompt-level effects on code complexity, but the architecture-level question is open. We compare six widely-used multi-agent configurations (Basic, AC, ACT, Debugger, AC+Debugger, ACT+Debugger) under two models from the GPT-4o family across all 164 HumanEval tasks - 1,968 paired observations - using the five RADON complexity metrics (SLOC, cyclomatic complexity, and Halstead Volume, Difficulty, and Effort). We apply a paired non-parametric statistical pipeline (Friedman omnibus, Wilcoxon signed-rank post-hoc with Holm correction, Kendall's $W$ and matched-pairs rank-biserial effect sizes) in both all-completions and passing-only conditions. The six architectures collapse into two indistinguishable complexity clusters separated by a 50-130% gap, the same partition in both models and under both conditions; among the architectural layers, the analyst-coder split inflates complexity, the runtime debugger does not - and on the analyst-coder background actively deflates it - and the tester re-inflates it. The heavy cluster's additional complexity buys no pass@1 advantage: the leanest architectures match or beat the heaviest on accuracy. Architectural elaboration in LLM code generation should therefore be justified by measured benefit on the dimensions that matter, not assumed.

</details>


### [10] [Measuring Delivery Consistency in Practice: A DORA Extension from a Multi-Platform Release Setting](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00364v1)
*Luiz Parente,James C. Davis*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出交付一致性（DC）指标作为DORA框架的补充，用于衡量部署节奏的规律性，并通过交付健康矩阵提供八原型诊断，在四个平台120周数据上验证了其区分能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DORA指标仅为一阶统计量或简单比率，无法捕捉部署时间的分布形状，导致具有相同测量值的团队可能表现出截然不同的节奏模式，缺乏对过程规律的深入洞察。

Method: 开发了有界二阶度量——交付一致性（DC），基于发布间隔的变异系数，并将其整合到交付健康矩阵中，形成八原型诊断框架；在四个平台的软件交付团队上使用120周的真实数据（Jira、GitHub、Firebase）进行经验评估。

Result: DC能区分具有相同DORA等级但节奏规律性不同的平台；交付健康矩阵将读数总结为原型，指向共享的组织或程序约束。

Conclusion: DC和交付健康矩阵提供了超越DORA指标的额外洞察，能有效识别工程过程中的节奏问题，并指导差异化干预措施。

中文摘要：DevOps研究与评估（DORA）框架是工程团队绩效衡量方面最广泛采用的测量系统。然而，每个DORA指标都是一阶统计量或简单比率，这限制了对工程过程的洞察潜力。例如，像部署频率这样的指标无法捕捉部署时间的分布形状，因此具有相同测量值的团队可能以节拍式节奏部署，也可能以不可取的突发式部署。我们一直在开发和试点交付一致性（Delivery Consistency, DC），这是一种有界的二阶度量，用于衡量节奏规律性，它源自发布间隔的变异系数。结合其他DORA概念，我们将DC整合到交付健康矩阵（Delivery Health Matrix）中，这是一种八原型诊断方法，将联合读数映射到差异化干预措施。我们报告了一项在四个平台软件交付团队上的经验评估，使用了从Jira、GitHub和Firebase记录中提取的120周数据。DC使我们能够区分具有相同DORA等级但节奏规律性不同的平台，而矩阵将读数总结为一个原型，指向共享的组织或程序约束。

Original abstract: The DevOps Research and Assessment (DORA) framework is the most widely adopted measurement system for performance measurement across engineering teams. However, every DORA metric is a first-moment statistic or a simple ratio, which limits the potential insights into engineering process. For example, metrics like Deployment Frequency do not capture the distributional shape of deployment timing, so teams with identical measures can deploy on a metronomic cadence or in undesirably erratic bursts. We have been developing and piloting Delivery Consistency (DC), a bounded second-moment measure of cadence regularity derived from the coefficient of variation of inter-release intervals. In conjunction with other DORA concepts, we integrated DC into the Delivery Health Matrix, an eight-archetype diagnostic that maps joint readings to differentiated interventions. We report an experience evaluation on a four-platform software delivery group using 120 weeks of data extracted from our Jira, GitHub, and Firebase records. DC allowed us to distinguish platforms with identical DORA tier placements but different cadence regularity, and the Matrix summarized the readings into an archetype that pointed at a shared organization or procedural constraint.

</details>

### [11] [Healthcare Mechanisms from Policy-as-Code Search under Strategic Provider Response](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30680v1)
*Zihan Wang,Xiang Xu,Hongyuan Zha,Wenhao Li*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 使用多agent模拟器与LLM引导程序合成，方法可迁移至agent设计。

TL;DR: 本文提出用语言模型程序合成方法设计医院机制，通过多智能体模拟器评估，并利用LLM进化搜索找到消除向上编码、减半拒绝率且保留大部分资金的混合目标程序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有医疗AI基准测试固定了提供者响应，无法评估机制均衡，需要能模拟策略性响应的方法。

Method: 将医院机制设计重新定义为语言模型的程序合成，使用多智能体模拟器Medi-Sim（含五个策略通道）执行和评分规则程序，并通过LLM引导的进化代码搜索优化。

Result: LLM引导进化搜索合成混合目标程序，消除向上编码，将拒绝减半，并保留大部分利润导向基线的资金。

Conclusion: 所提方法能有效设计可检查的医院机制，避免不良策略响应，实现更好的均衡结果。

中文摘要：医疗机制与其引发的策略性提供者响应密不可分：现有的医疗AI基准测试固定了这种响应，因此无法通过它们产生的均衡来评估机制。我们将医院机制设计重新定义为语言模型的程序合成：类型化、可检查的规则程序由Medi-Sim执行和评分，Medi-Sim是一个多智能体模拟器，具有五个策略性提供者通道（编码、选择、延迟、努力、分诊）。一次激励扫描恢复了经典的卫生经济学发现作为相邻制度——在利润压力下的向上编码和低复杂性患者选择，以及古德哈特式漂移，其中测量性能与真实结果变得反相关——而单个审计杠杆暴露了压力迁移：关闭编码通道使低复杂性选择翻倍以上。LLM引导的进化代码搜索在相同的规则程序空间上合成一个可检查的混合目标程序，该程序消除了向上编码，将拒绝减半，并保留了大部分以利润为导向的基线的资金。

Original abstract: Healthcare mechanisms are inseparable from the strategic provider response they induce: existing healthcare AI benchmarks hold this response fixed and so cannot evaluate mechanisms by the equilibrium they produce. We recast hospital mechanism design as program synthesis for language models: typed, inspectable rule programs are executed and scored by Medi-Sim, a multi-agent simulator with five strategic provider channels (coding, selection, delay, effort, triage). An incentive sweep recovers classical health-economics findings as adjacent regimes -- up-coding and low-complexity-patient selection under profit pressure, and Goodhart-style drift where measured performance becomes anti-correlated with true outcomes -- and a single audit lever exposes pressure migration: closing the coding channel more than doubles low-complexity selection. LLM-guided evolutionary code search over the same rule-program space then synthesizes an inspectable mixed-objective program that eliminates up-coding, halves rejection, and retains most of the profit-oriented baseline's funds.

</details>


### [12] [MAVEN: Improving Generalization in Agentic Tool Calling](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30738v1)
*Omkar Ghugarkar,Vishvesh Bhat,Muhammad Ahmed Mohsin,Asad Aali*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: MAVEN模块化agent验证执行网络，直接改进工具调用泛化。

TL;DR: MAVEN是一个轻量级符号推理框架，通过结构化分解和中间验证显著提升了工具调用场景的推理准确率，且成本极低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大型语言模型在单独基准测试上表现良好，但在组合推理策略、保留中间状态和跨域协调工具方面存在不足，需要一种轻量级方法来提升泛化能力。

Method: 提出了MAVEN框架，采用结构化分解、自适应工具编排和中间验证的符号推理方法，并构建了MAVEN-Bench压力测试基准。

Result: 在MAVEN-Bench上，MAVEN将GPT-OSS-120b的准确率从48%提升至71%无需额外训练，且成本约为前沿模型的1/10，与其他专有基线保持竞争力。

Conclusion: 轻量级验证中心的框架能有效增强组合推理，并推动对智能体进行更过程感知的评估。

中文摘要：跨智能体工具调用环境的泛化仍然是可靠智能体推理系统的核心挑战。尽管大型语言模型在单独基准测试上取得了强劲结果，但其组合推理策略、保留中间状态以及跨域协调工具的能力仍未得到充分探索。我们提出了MAVEN（模块化智能体验证与执行网络），这是一种轻量级符号推理框架，用于结构化分解、自适应工具编排和中间验证。我们在已建立的工具调用基准测试上评估了MAVEN，包括BFCL v3、TauBench、Tau2Bench、AceBench，并引入了MAVEN-Bench，这是一个针对多步数学和物理推理的压力测试基准，具有显式验证和对抗性任务组合。MAVEN-Bench揭示了部分推理质量与端到端任务成功之间的显著差距；在直接的MAVEN-Bench运行中，MAVEN使其GPT-OSS-120b基础模型从48%的准确率提升至71%，无需额外训练。同时，它在使用开源权重骨干模型且估计成本约为十分之一的情况下，仍能与前沿专有基线模型保持竞争力，这表明以轻量验证为中心的框架可以增强组合推理，并推动对实际环境中智能体进行更多过程感知的评估。

Original abstract: Generalization across agentic tool-calling environments remains a central challenge for reliable agentic reasoning systems. Although large language models achieve strong results on individual benchmarks, their ability to compose reasoning strategies, preserve intermediate states, and coordinate tools across domains remains underexplored. We present MAVEN (Modular Agentic Verification and Execution Network), a lightweight symbolic reasoning scaffold for structured decomposition, adaptive tool orchestration, and intermediate verification. We evaluate MAVEN across established tool-calling benchmarks, including BFCL v3, TauBench, Tau2Bench, AceBench, and introduce MAVEN-Bench, a stress-test benchmark for multi-step mathematical and physical reasoning with explicit verification and adversarial task composition. MAVEN-Bench exposes a substantial gap between partial reasoning quality and end-to-end task success; in direct MAVEN-Bench runs, MAVEN improves its GPT-OSS-120b base model from 48% to 71% accuracy without additional training. It also remains competitive with frontier proprietary baselines while using an open-weight backbone with an estimated cost ratio of roughly 1/10, suggesting that lightweight verification-centered scaffolds can strengthen compositional reasoning and motivate more process-aware evaluation of agents in the wild.

### [13] [Harnessing Agent Skills: Architectural Patterns and a Reference Architecture for Skill-Mediated LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20631v1)
*Boming Xia,Liming Zhu,Zhenchang Xing,Qinghua Lu,Dino Sejdinovic,Xiwei Xu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出agent技能架构模式与参考架构，直接相关agent设计。

TL;DR: 本文提出了代理技能利用的十个经验架构模式和一个四层参考架构，并通过八个系统实例化评估，为分析代理系统的技能利用责任提供了词汇和诊断框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 技能工件在使用时涉及静态到动态的过渡，需要明确架构责任来约束执行后果并捕获证据，以支持归因、验证、修复和演化。

Method: 通过经验性方法提炼十个架构模式（五个核心、五个支持），并综合成包含供应链、中介、执行控制、证据与反馈四个责任层的参考架构，最后在八个系统中进行交叉实例化评估。

Result: 得到了十个架构模式和一个四层参考架构，能够有效描述和分析不同代理系统中的技能利用责任。

Conclusion: 该模式和参考架构为代理技能利用提供了统一的词汇和诊断工具，有助于设计、分析和比较不同系统的技能管理机制。

中文摘要：代理技能将可重用的面向代理的行为知识和指导外部化为持久工件，这些工件可以被大型语言模型代理发现、激活和解释。尽管技能工件在静止时是静态的，但其架构责任在使用中产生，当工件被选择用于一次运行、绑定到上下文和权限约束、由随机代理解释并作为运行证据记录时。我们称这种特定于运行的关系为“使用中的技能”。本文研究代理技能利用：管理从技能工件到使用中的技能过渡的架构责任，约束与使用中的技能相关的可执行后果，并捕获用于归因、验证、修复和演化的证据。本文提供了一个包含十个经验性架构模式（五个核心，五个支持）的目录，用于技能利用，并将它们综合成一个具有四个责任层的参考架构：供应链、中介、执行控制、证据与反馈。我们通过跨8个选定系统的实例化来评估该架构。由此产生的模式和参考架构为分析跨代理系统的技能利用责任提供了词汇和诊断框架。

Original abstract: Agent skills externalise reusable agent-facing behavioural knowledge and guidance as persistent artefacts that can be discovered, activated, and interpreted by LLM agents. Although a skill artefact is static at rest, its architectural responsibilities arise in use, when the artefact is selected for a run, bound to context and authority constraints, interpreted by a stochastic agent, and recorded as run evidence. We call this run-specific relation skill-in-use. This paper studies agent skill harnessing: the architectural responsibilities that govern the transition from skill artefacts to skill-in-use, bound the executable consequences associated with skill-in-use, and capture evidence for attribution, verification, repair, and evolution. This paper provides a catalogue of ten empirically grounded architectural patterns (five core, five supporting) for skill harnessing and synthesises them into a reference architecture with four responsibility layers: Supply Chain, Mediation, Execution Control, and Evidence & Feedback. We evaluate the architecture through cross-instantiation across 8 selected systems. The resulting patterns and reference architecture provide a vocabulary and diagnostic frame for analysing skill-harnessing responsibilities across agent systems.

### [14] [Learning Agent-Compatible Context Management for Long-Horizon Tasks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30785v1)
*Lu Yi,Runlin Lei,Liuyi Yao,Yuexiang Xie,Yuyang Li,Wenhao Zhang,Zhewei Wei,Yaliang Li,Jian-Yun Nie*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: AdaCoM通过外部LLM管理agent上下文，可迁移至coding agent的长程任务。

TL;DR: 提出自适应上下文管理（AdaCoM），通过外部LLM和强化学习为冻结代理管理上下文，在长时任务中提升性能并揭示保真度-可靠性权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长上下文管理方法需要训练代理本身，不适用于闭源代理且忽略代理差异；因此需要一种无需修改代理、可泛化的上下文管理方法。

Method: 训练一个外部LLM，通过灵活修改动作和端到端强化学习来管理冻结代理的上下文，实现自适应上下文管理（AdaCoM）。

Result: 在多种代理的网络搜索和深度研究基准上，AdaCoM显著提升性能；发现保真度-可靠性权衡：高性能代理需高保真度，低性能代理需激进压缩；迁移实验表明与代理能力匹配时泛化最好。

Conclusion: AdaCoM为闭源代理提供了可复用的上下文管理方案，通过强化学习学习策略，并揭示不同能力代理需不同管理策略，为实际部署提供指导。

中文摘要：LLM代理在现实应用中越来越多地面临长时任务，例如网络搜索和深度研究，其中累积的上下文可能导致长上下文退化和推理失败。先前的工作通过代理端上下文控制或固定策略（如摘要）进行上下文管理来缓解这一问题，但这需要训练代理本身以适应——这对于闭源代理来说不切实际，并且忽略了不同代理可能需要不同策略的事实。我们引入了自适应上下文管理（AdaCoM），该方法训练一个外部LLM，通过灵活修改操作和端到端强化学习来管理冻结代理的上下文。在多种代理的网络搜索和深度研究基准测试中，AdaCoM通过保留任务约束和进度同时修剪过时内容，显著提升了性能。学习到的策略揭示了一个保真度-可靠性权衡：具有更高原始ReAct性能的代理受益于更高保真度的上下文保留，而性能较低的代理则需要更激进的压缩以保持在可靠的推理范围内。迁移实验表明，AdaCoM在能力相似的代理（通过原始ReAct性能衡量）之间泛化效果最好，这为代理系统实现可复用的上下文管理器提供了一条实用路径。

Original abstract: LLM agents increasingly face long-horizon tasks such as web search and deep research in real-world applications, where accumulated context can cause long-context degradation and reasoning failures. Prior work mitigates this through context management with agent-side context control or fixed strategies such as summarization, which require training the agent itself for adaptation - making it impractical for closed-source agents and ignoring that different agents may require different strategies. We introduce Adaptive Context Management (AdaCoM), which trains an external LLM to manage the context of a frozen agent through flexible modification actions and end-to-end reinforcement learning. Across diverse agents on web search and deep research benchmarks, AdaCoM substantially improves performance by preserving task constraints and progress while pruning stale content. The learned strategies reveal a Fidelity-Reliability Trade-off: agents with higher vanilla ReAct performance benefit from higher-fidelity context preservation, whereas lower-performing agents require more aggressive compression to stay within a reliable reasoning regime. Transfer experiments show that AdaCoM generalizes most effectively across agents with similar capability (measured by vanilla ReAct performance), suggesting a practical path toward reusable context managers for agent systems.

### [15] [PReMISE: Policy Rubrics as Measurement Specifications for LLM Judges](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30803v1)
*Swastik Roy,Rajkumar Pujari,Tharindu Kumarage,Charith Peris,Rahul Gupta,Anna Rumshisky,Pradeep Natarajan,Venkatesh Saligrama*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM评委评估框架，对agent性能评估有参考价值。

TL;DR: 提出PReMISE框架来发现和审计评分标准，通过修复操作提升LLM评估器的可靠性和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM评估器的评分严重依赖模糊的评分标准，导致高分可能奖励不准确或违背用户意图的回答，现有评分标准来源在可靠性、偏好预测性和对抗鲁棒性上无法兼顾。

Method: 提出PReMISE框架，从成对人类偏好数据中发现策略级评分标准集，并从四个维度审计评分标准；引入偏好排名选择和可靠性约束精炼两种修复操作。

Result: 原始来源无法同时满足三个关键性质；PReMISE在多个维度上表现最佳；偏好排名选择将准确率从65.0%提升至68.6%，可靠性约束精炼将可利用回答的高分率从46.4%降至36.0%。

Conclusion: PReMISE能有效发现和审计评分标准，修复操作显著提升评估器性能，且高评分者一致性不保证低可利用性需额外审计。

中文摘要：LLM评估器被越来越多地用于评估开放式回答，但它们的得分在很大程度上取决于约束它们的评分标准。一个要求回答“有帮助且符合事实”的模糊标准可能会奖励那些编造事实或违反用户意图的精心编写的回答。我们将可重用的评分标准视为测量规范：改变评分标准会改变由固定评估器引发的回答质量测量。我们引入了PReMISE框架，该框架给定成对的人类偏好数据，(i) 发现一个策略级别的评分标准集，以及(ii) 在LLM评估器使用下沿着四个轴审计任何评分标准集：结构充分性、可靠性、偏好拟合和对抗鲁棒性。在评分标准来源中，没有原始来源能同时满足可靠性、偏好预测性和对抗鲁棒性；高评分者间一致性并不意味低可利用性。PReMISE是唯一在适用性、特异性和有效维度上同时获得非平凡分数的评分标准来源。我们贡献了两个针对审计的修复操作：偏好排名选择将评估器在成对回答上的准确率从65.0%提高到68.6%，与最强的评分标准发现基线相当，并在我们的跨评估器扫描中在三个评估器中的两个上领先；可靠性约束精炼将利用性回答获得高分的比率从46.4%降低到36.0%，而评分者间一致性变化很小（α=0.531→0.519）。

Original abstract: LLM judges are increasingly used to evaluate open-ended responses, but their scores depend strongly on the rubrics that condition them. A vague rubric asking for a response to be ``helpful and factual'' can reward polished answers that invent facts or violate user intent. We treat reusable rubrics as measurement specifications: changing the rubric changes the response quality measurement induced by a fixed judge. We introduce PReMISE, a framework that, given pairwise human-preference data, (i) discovers a policy-level rubric set, and (ii) audits any rubric set under LLM-judge use along four axes: structural adequacy, reliability, preference fit, and adversarial robustness. Across rubric sources no raw source is simultaneously reliable, preference-predictive, and adversarially robust; and high inter-rater agreement does not imply low exploitability. PReMISE is the only rubric source to score non-trivially on applicability, specificity, and effective dimensionality simultaneously. We contribute two audit-targeted repair operations: preference-rank selection raises judge accuracy on paired responses from $65.0\%$ to $68.6\%$, competitive with the strongest rubric-discovery baselines and leading on two of three judges in our cross-judge sweep; reliability-constrained refinement reduces the rate at which exploit responses receive high scores from $46.4\%$ to $36.0\%$ with little change in inter-judge agreement ($α{=}.531\to.519$).

### [16] [Planner-Centric Reinforcement Learning for Deep Research with Structure-Aware Reward](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30824v1)
*Mustafa Anis Hussain,Xinle Wu,Yao Lu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出基于DAG规划的agent框架，规划器RL训练，可迁移至coding agent的规划组件。

TL;DR: 提出DecomposeR，通过将研究计划表示为类型化DAG并分阶段训练规划器和回答器，实现更细粒度的规划优化，在长形式基准上提升5.1-8.0分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有训练范式要么依赖短形式QA作为代理，要么优化单一路径，导致规划与执行难以解耦且规划过程信用分配薄弱，需要更结构化的规划方法。

Method: 提出DecomposeR框架，用类型化有向无环图（DAG）显式表示研究计划；分两阶段训练Qwen3-8B：规划器RL学习图结构和查询分解，回答器RL学习分支执行和最终综合，并对规划令牌和结构组件分配奖励。

Result: 在多个长形式基准测试上，DecomposeR-8B相比强开源基线提升5.1-8.0分。

Conclusion: 通过显式结构化规划并细粒度优化，显著提升了长形式问答任务中规划和回答的综合性能。

中文摘要：深度研究任务要求大语言模型规划调查内容、检索证据并跨多个查询分支综合生成长期形式答案。现有的训练范式要么依赖短形式可验证的问答作为代理，要么优化单一的长轨迹，这使得规划和执行难以解耦，并导致规划过程的信用分配薄弱。我们提出DecomposeR，一个以规划者为中心的深度研究框架，将研究计划表示为类型化有向无环图（DAG），使得规划变得显式、结构化且可奖励。我们分两个阶段训练Qwen3-8B模型：规划器强化学习（RL）首先学习图结构和查询分解以改进研究规划，然后回答器强化学习（RL）基于所学到的计划学习分支执行和最终综合。通过将奖励分配给显式的规划器令牌和结构化组件而非扁平轨迹，DecomposeR实现了更细粒度的规划优化，同时减少了端到端训练的模糊性。实验表明，DecomposeR-8B在流行的长形式基准测试上，由于改进的规划和回答能力，相比强大的可比开源基线提高了5.1-8.0分。

Original abstract: Deep research tasks require LLMs to plan what to investigate, retrieve evidence, and synthesize long-form answers across multiple branches of inquiry. Existing training paradigms either rely on short-form verifiable QA as a proxy or optimize monolithic long trajectories, which makes planning and execution difficult to disentangle and yields weak credit assignment for the planning process. We propose DecomposeR, a planner-centric deep research framework that represents research plans as typed directed acyclic graphs (DAGs), allowing planning to be made explicit, structured, and rewardable. We train a Qwen3-8B model in two stages: planner reinforcement learning (RL) first learns graph structure and query decomposition to improve research planning, and answerer reinforcement learning (RL) then learns branch-level execution and final synthesis conditioned on the learned plan. By assigning rewards to explicit planner tokens and structured components rather than to a flat trajectory, DecomposeR enables finer-grained optimization of planning while reducing the ambiguity of end-to-end training. Experiments show that DecomposeR-8B improves over strong comparable open baselines by 5.1-8.0 points on popular long-form benchmarks due to improved planning and answering capabilities.

### [17] [SLAT: Segment-Level Adaptive Trimming for Efficient CoT Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30832v1)
*Jian Yao,Xiongcai Luo,Ran Cheng,Kay Chen Tan*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: CoT推理的片段级修剪框架，可提升agent推理效率，虽非直接agent但方法通用。

TL;DR: SLAT通过片段级别的自适应修剪，在不降低准确率的情况下将推理链长度减少50%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法使用令牌统一的长度惩罚，无法区分冗余和有用推理，导致抑制冗余时也损害了性能。

Method: 提出SLAT框架，基于片段次优性的理论表征，通过强化学习选择性抑制高概率低边际效用的冗余片段。

Result: 在标准基准上，SLAT相对于未压缩基线将推理长度减少50%，同时保持竞争性的准确率，建立了更优的准确率-效率帕累托前沿。

Conclusion: 理论基础的、片段感知的修剪是大语言模型中高效思维链推理的一个有前景方向。

中文摘要：近期大型推理模型的进展通过强化学习显著提升了思维链能力。然而，生成的推理链经常存在结构冗余（即“过度思考”），导致高计算开销而不提高答案正确性。现有的缓解策略通常依赖于令牌统一的长度惩罚，这提供了粗糙的、片段不可知的缩短输出的压力，并可能在不经意间抑制有用的推理与冗余。为了解决这个问题，我们证明了低效集中在具有低边际效用的高概率片段中。我们在正确性-长度权衡目标下推导了片段次优性的理论表征，并提出了SLAT（片段级自适应修剪），一种基于此标准选择性抑制冗余片段的强化学习框架。在标准基准上的实验结果表明，SLAT建立了优越的准确率-效率帕累托前沿，相对于未压缩的基线将推理长度减少50%，同时保持有竞争力的准确率。总体而言，我们的结果表明，理论基础的、片段感知的修剪是大语言模型中高效思维链推理的一个有前景的方向。

Original abstract: Recent advances in Large Reasoning Models have significantly improved chain-of-thought (CoT) capabilities via reinforcement learning (RL). However, generated reasoning chains frequently suffer from structural redundancy (i.e., \emph{overthinking}), incurring high computational overhead without improving answer correctness. Existing mitigation strategies typically rely on token-uniform length penalties, which provide coarse, segment-agnostic pressure toward shorter outputs and can inadvertently suppress useful reasoning alongside redundancy. To address this, we demonstrate that inefficiency concentrates in high-probability segments with low marginal utility. We derive a theoretical characterization of segment suboptimality under the correctness-length trade-off objective and propose \textsc{SLAT} (Segment-Level Adaptive Trimming), an RL framework that selectively suppresses redundant segments based on this criterion. Empirical results on standard benchmarks indicate that \textsc{SLAT} establishes a superior accuracy-efficiency Pareto frontier, reducing reasoning length by $50\%$ relative to uncompressed baselines while maintaining competitive accuracy. Overall, our results suggest that theoretically grounded, segment-aware trimming is a promising direction for efficient CoT reasoning in large language models.

### [18] [COMPASS: Cognitive MCTS-Guided Process Alignment for Safe Search Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30838v1)
*Wenkai Shen,Pengyang Zhou,Jiahe Xu,Jiaming Qian,Haozhe He,Zhihao Huang,Chaochao Chen,Xiaolin Zheng*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 搜索agent安全对齐的MCTS过程奖励框架，直接贡献通用agent安全方法。

TL;DR: COMPASS通过认知树探索和内省步骤级对齐，在减少训练数据的同时实现了LLM搜索智能体的鲁棒安全对齐。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM搜索智能体的多步推理和工具使用能力导致检索诱导的安全退化，现有对齐方法无法有效捕获稀疏安全信号和监督多步交互中的违规行为。

Method: 提出COMPASS框架，包含认知树探索（CTE）高效合成隐蔽攻击轨迹，和内省步骤级对齐（ISA）隔离风险中间动作进行细粒度过程监督。

Result: COMPASS在显著更少训练数据下实现了有利的安全-效用权衡。

Conclusion: COMPASS通过过程对齐有效解决了LLM搜索智能体的安全对齐问题，平衡了安全性和通用效用。

中文摘要：LLM驱动的搜索智能体能够进行多步推理和工具使用。然而，这些能力引入了检索诱导的安全退化，因为有害意图可能分解成看似无害的子查询，从而导致不安全的结果。现有的对齐方法难以捕获稀疏的安全信号，并且未能监督多步交互中的各种违规。我们提出了COMPASS，一种认知MCTS引导的过程对齐框架，旨在实现整个智能体工作流中的鲁棒安全对齐，同时保持通用效用。COMPASS集成了认知树探索（CTE）以高效合成隐蔽的攻击轨迹，以及内省步骤级对齐（ISA）以隔离风险中间动作进行细粒度过程监督。实验结果表明，COMPASS在需要显著更少训练数据的情况下实现了有利的安全-效用权衡。

Original abstract: LLM-powered search agents enable multi-step reasoning and tool use. However, these capabilities introduce retrieval-induced safety degradation, as harmful intents may decompose into seemingly innocuous sub-queries that lead to unsafe outcomes. Existing alignment methods struggle to capture sparse safety signals and fail to supervise diverse violations across multi-step interactions. We propose COMPASS, a Cognitive MCTS-Guided Process Alignment framework designed to achieve robust safety alignment throughout the agent workflow while preserving general utility. COMPASS integrates cognitive tree exploration (CTE) to efficiently synthesize stealthy attack trajectories, and introspective step-wise alignment (ISA) to isolate risky intermediate actions for fine-grained process supervision. Empirical results show that COMPASS achieves a favorable safety-utility trade-off while requiring substantially less training data.

</details>


### [19] [Distilling LLM Feedback for Lean Theorem Proving](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30861v1)
*Gaetan Narozniak,Gérard Biau,Rémi Munos,Ahmad Rammal,Pierre Marion*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 定理证明中的反馈蒸馏方法，结合RL与自我蒸馏，可迁移至代码生成agent训练。

TL;DR: 提出反馈蒸馏方法，通过token级匹配自身分布与语言模型提供的特权反馈，在定理证明中优于GRPO并与之互补。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GRPO算法存在稀疏奖励、探索有限和模式崩溃问题，需要更有效的后训练方法。

Method: 反馈蒸馏（Feedback Distillation），训练模型在token级别匹配其自身在语言模型产生的特权反馈条件下的分布，提供token级监督并注入外部知识。

Result: 在Lean4定理证明中，反馈蒸馏比GRPO保持更高的轨迹多样性、策略熵和更好的pass@k缩放；从反馈蒸馏检查点初始化GRPO优于单独方法。

Conclusion: 反馈蒸馏是改进复杂推理后训练的有前景途径，可与GRPO互补使用。

中文摘要：推理模型的后训练通常结合了监督微调和基于可验证奖励的强化学习，最常用的是GRPO。然而，该算法存在奖励稀疏、探索有限和模式崩溃的问题。基于近期关于自蒸馏的工作，我们提出反馈蒸馏（Feedback Distillation），这是一种训练方法，其中模型被训练为在token级别匹配其自身在由语言模型产生的特权反馈条件下的分布。反馈蒸馏提供token级别的监督，并能注入外部知识。在Lean4定理证明任务上评估我们的方法，我们发现反馈蒸馏比GRPO在生成的轨迹中保持更大的多样性，产生更高的策略熵和更好的pass@k缩放。这两种方法相辅相成：从反馈蒸馏检查点初始化GRPO优于单独使用任一方法。总体而言，我们的结果表明，这是改进复杂推理后训练的一条有前景的途径。

Original abstract: Post-training for reasoning models typically combines supervised fine-tuning with reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards, most commonly with GRPO. However, this algorithm suffers from sparse rewards, limited exploration, and mode collapse. Building upon recent works on self-distillation, we propose Feedback Distillation, a training method where the model is trained to match, at the token level, its own distribution conditioned on privileged feedback produced by a language model. Feedback Distillation offers token-level supervision and can inject external knowledge. Evaluating our method for Lean4 theorem-proving, we find that Feedback Distillation maintains greater diversity in generated trajectories than GRPO, yielding higher policy entropy and better pass@k scaling. The two methods are complementary: initializing GRPO from a Feedback Distillation checkpoint outperforms either method alone. All in all, our results suggest a promising avenue to improve post-training for complex reasoning.

### [20] [UniScale: Adaptive Unified Inference Scaling via Online Joint Optimization of Model Routing and Test-Time Scaling](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30898v1)
*Kaiyu Huang,Xingyu Wang,Mingze Kong,Zhubo Shi,Yuqian Hou,Hong Xu,Zhongxiang Dai,Minchen Yu,Qingjiang Shi*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 统一模型路由与测试时缩放，可优化agent推理成本，属一般部署方法。

TL;DR: UniScale通过将模型路由和测试时扩展统一为上下文多臂老虎机问题，实现了细粒度且更优的质量-成本权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将模型路由和测试时扩展分开处理，导致粗粒度、有限适应性和收益递减，限制了动态推理环境中的性能。

Method: 提出UniScale框架，将统一推理扩展（UIS）建模为上下文多臂老虎机问题，使用LinUCB学习推理策略，并融入效率感知学习和成本建模。

Result: 在多样化动态推理场景中，UniScale有效利用UIS空间中的协同作用，实现了细粒度且一致更好的质量-成本权衡。

Conclusion: 统一模型路由和测试时扩展能有效协同，提升推理效率，为动态推理环境提供更优的平衡方案。

中文摘要：在大型语言模型（LLM）的实际部署中，平衡推理质量和计算成本已成为核心挑战。现有方法沿着两个大致独立的维度处理这种权衡：模型路由（根据请求复杂度在不同规模的模型间切换）和测试时扩展（在固定模型内调整推理时的计算量以实现细粒度控制）。然而，这种解耦设计带来了固有的局限性。模型路由由于模型规模的稀疏集合而产生粗粒度、离散的性能变化，而单模型测试时扩展常常遇到能力上限，并且随着计算量增加出现收益递减。此外，将两种机制分开处理限制了在动态推理环境中的适应性。为了克服这些限制，我们引入了统一推理扩展（UIS），它将模型路由和测试时扩展统一到单个优化空间中。基于此公式，我们提出了UniScale，一个在线框架，将自适应UIS建模为上下文多臂老虎机问题，并通过LinUCB学习推理策略。该框架结合了效率感知学习和成本建模，以确保在高维动作空间中的稳定和可扩展优化。评估表明，UniScale有效地利用了UIS空间中的协同作用，在多样化的动态推理场景中提供细粒度且一致更好的质量-成本权衡。

Original abstract: In real-world deployments of large language models (LLMs), balancing inference quality and computational cost has become a central challenge. Existing approaches tackle this trade-off along two largely independent dimensions: model routing, which switches among models of different scales to match request complexity, and test-time scaling (TTS), which adjusts inference-time compute within a fixed model for fine-grained control. However, this decoupled design introduces inherent limitations. Model routing yields coarse-grained, discrete performance changes due to the sparse set of model scales, while single-model TTS often encounters capacity ceilings and exhibits diminishing returns as compute increases. Moreover, treating the two mechanisms separately restricts adaptability in dynamic inference environments. To overcome these limitations, we introduce Unified Inference Scaling (UIS), which unifies model routing and TTS in a single optimization space. Building on this formulation, we propose UniScale, an online framework that models adaptive UIS as a contextual multi-armed bandit problem and learns inference policies via LinUCB. The framework incorporates efficiency-aware learning and cost modeling to ensure stable and scalable optimization over high-dimensional action spaces. Evaluation shows that UniScale effectively exploits the synergy in the UIS space to deliver a fine-grained and consistently better quality-cost trade-off across diverse, dynamic inference scenarios.

Original abstract: This work addresses the problem of autonomous resource management in heterogeneous satellite cluster conducting Earth Observation (EO) missions including optical and Synthetic Aperture Radar (SAR) satellites. In autonomous operation mode, satellites are equipped with intelligent capabilities enabling real-time decision-making based on the latest conditions, while requiring minimal interaction with ground operators. Traditional scheduling approaches typically rely on mathematical models to represent satellite mission and resource management. Then, this problem is solved by using optimization algorithms. However, such solutions become less effective when the underlying models are not available, over complex, and inaccurate due to dynamic changes and uncertainties inherent in the space mission environment. A promising alternative is to reformulate the problem as a sequential decision-making process and apply model-free reinforcement learning techniques to enable adaptive and real-time resource management. To this end, we propose a novel transformer-based architecture tailored for heterogeneous satellite cluster autonomous EO Mission with relational observations-actions tokenization and differential attention mechanism. Our experimental results demonstrate significant performance improvements compared to the available baselines. Moreover, the proposed architecture exhibits strong adaptability and transferability with respect to varying numbers of satellite clusters.

### [22] [COLLEAGUE.SKILL: Automated AI Skill Generation via Expert Knowledge Distillation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31264v1)
*Tianyi Zhou,Dongrui Liu,Leitao Yuan,Jing Shao,Xia Hu*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法无法从异质痕迹中端到端地提取可检查、可纠正且智能体可用的技能。

Method: 自动化痕迹到技能蒸馏，生成包含能力轨道和行为轨道的版本化技能包，支持检查、更新、回滚和跨主机部署。

Result: 开源系统，拥有约18.5k GitHub星标，215个技能来自165名贡献者，累计超100k星标。

Conclusion: 展示了基于人的技能可作为可移植、可纠正的包，而非不透明提示或隐藏记忆。

中文摘要：LLM智能体越来越期望不仅能够完成孤立的任务，还能够携带人类专业知识、判断和交互风格的有界表示。构建这种基于人的智能体仍然困难，因为与个人或角色相关的可操作知识通常嵌入在异质痕迹中，而不是以清晰的指令形式书写。现有的记忆和角色系统捕捉了这些证据的片段，而技能框架提供了可移植的打包格式；然而，目前没有端到端的工作流来将这些痕迹提炼成可检查、可纠正且智能体可使用的技能。我们提出了一种自动化的痕迹到技能提炼系统，通过专家知识蒸馏生成基于人的AI技能。给定目标个人或角色的材料，COLLEAGUE.SKILL生成一个版本化的技能包，包含两个协调的轨道：能力轨道（用于实践、思维模型和决策启发法）和有界行为轨道（用于沟通风格、交互规则和纠正历史）。该技能包可以被检查、调用、通过自然语言反馈进行更新、回滚、跨智能体主机安装，并可选择为受控分发做准备。我们描述了开源系统中实现的工件合同、生成工作流、纠正生命周期、部署表面和领域预设。在撰写本文时，公共仓库拥有约18.5k个GitHub星标；图库列出了来自165名贡献者的215个技能，以及跨列出的技能卡累计超过10万个星标。该系统展示了如何将基于人的技能表示为可移植、可纠正的包，而不是不透明的提示或隐藏的记忆。

Original abstract: LLM agents are increasingly expected not only to complete isolated tasks, but also to carry bounded representations of human expertise, judgment, and interaction style. Building such person-grounded agents remains difficult because actionable knowledge associated with a person or role is usually embedded in heterogeneous traces rather than written as clean instructions. Existing memory and persona systems capture fragments of this evidence, while skill frameworks provide portable packaging formats; however, there is no end-to-end workflow for distilling these traces into inspectable, correctable, and agent-usable skills. We present an automated trace-to-skill distillation system for generating person-grounded AI skills via expert knowledge distillation. Given materials from a target person or role, COLLEAGUE.SKILL produces a versioned skill package with two coordinated tracks: a capability track for practices, mental models, and decision heuristics, and a bounded behavior track for communication style, interaction rules, and correction history. The package can be inspected, invoked, updated through natural-language feedback, rolled back, installed across agent hosts, and optionally prepared for controlled distribution. We describe the artifact contract, generation workflow, correction lifecycle, deployment surface, and domain presets implemented in the open-source system. At the time of writing, the public repository has approximately 18.5k GitHub stars; the gallery lists 215 skills from 165 contributors and more than 100k cumulative stars across listed skill cards. The system illustrates how person-grounded skills can be represented as portable, correctable packages rather than opaque prompts or hidden memories.

### [23] [Industrializing Prediction-Powered Inference: The GLIDE Library for Reliable GenAI and Agentic Systems Evaluation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31278v2)
*Grégoire Martinon,Ibrahim Merad,Mohammed Raki*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: agent系统评估的PPI库，直接用于可靠评估与标注节省。

TL;DR: GLIDE是一个开源Python库，统一了多种PPI估计器和采样器，用于可靠且高效的智能系统评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人工标注昂贵且LLM代理有偏，需要无偏估计与有效不确定性，而现有PPI方法分散且实现不完整。

Method: 开发GLIDE库，集成PPI++、分层PPI、Predict-Then-Debias及其变体、Active Statistical Inference等估计器，以及均匀、分层、主动、成本最优采样器，并提供验证套件和方法选择决策树。

Result: 在智能评估案例研究中，GLIDE在同等精度下大幅节省标注成本。

Conclusion: GLIDE为实际应用提供了一个统一、可复现的PPI工具，有助于可靠且高效地评估智能系统。

中文摘要：可靠评估智能系统需要无偏估计和有效的不确定性，但标准实践在昂贵的人工标注和有偏差的LLM-as-judge代理之间权衡。预测功率推断（PPI）结合两者，产生去偏估计和有效置信区间，但其各种方法仍分散在论文中，实现不完整。我们推出GLIDE，一个开源Python库，将最先进的PPI估计器（PPI++、分层PPI、先预测后去偏及其分层变体、主动统计推断）和采样器（均匀、分层、主动、成本最优）统一在专门用于均值估计的scipy风格API下。GLIDE附带可重复的蒙特卡洛验证套件、经验驱动的方法选择决策树，以及一个智能评估案例研究，显示在同等精度下大幅节省标注。GLIDE包可从此URL获取：https://github.com/EmertonData/glide

Original abstract: Reliable evaluation of agentic systems requires unbiased estimates with valid uncertainty, but standard practice navigates between costly human annotation and biased LLM-as-judge proxies. Prediction-powered inference (PPI) combines both into debiased estimates with valid confidence intervals, yet its various methods remain scattered across papers under partial implementations. We introduce GLIDE, an open-source Python library that unifies state-of-the-art PPI estimators (PPI++, Stratified PPI, Predict-Then-Debias and its stratified variants, Active Statistical Inference) and samplers (uniform, stratified, active, cost-optimal) under a scipy-style API specialized to mean estimation. GLIDE ships with a reproducible Monte Carlo validation suite, an empirically grounded decision tree for method selection, and an agentic evaluation case study showing substantial annotation savings at equivalent precision. The GLIDE package is available at this URL: https://github.com/EmertonData/glide

### [24] [CAST: Non-Privileged Clipped Asymmetric Self-Teaching with Advantage Flipping for GRPO](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00172v1)
*Yang Li,Gongle Xue,Yijia Guo,Yuheng Yuan,Liwen Hu,Lei Ma*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: GRPO改进训练方法，可迁移至agent训练中的奖励信号设计。

TL;DR: 提出CAST方法，通过无答案自蒸馏和双向局部优势符号反转，改进GRPO风格的RLVR训练，解决稀疏奖励和组相对优势消失问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 结果级奖励稀疏且组相对优势在全部正确或错误时消失；OPSD的令牌偏好与轨迹正确性不一致，导致噪声信号。

Method: 保留GRPO目标，使用停止梯度自教师根据轨迹正确性塑造令牌级优势；无需参考解，保持自教师对数概率差距活跃；应用双向局部优势符号反转；为零方差全正确/全错误组分配有界符号约束基础优势。

Result: 数学推理实验表明，CAST改进RLVR训练，同时保持轻量级、基于验证器的轨迹级目标。

Conclusion: CAST有效提升RLVR训练，提供更密集且与轨迹正确性对齐的令牌级反馈。

中文摘要：具有可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR），特别是组相对策略优化（GRPO），已被广泛用于改进大型语言模型的推理能力。然而，结果级奖励仅提供稀疏监督，并且当某个提示的所有采样轨迹都是正确或错误时，组相对优势会消失。在线策略自蒸馏（OPSD）提供了密集的令牌级引导，但其令牌偏好不一定与轨迹正确性对齐；经验诊断表明，OPSD信号在正确和错误的轨迹上表现不同，教师正向和教师负向差距信号展现出不同的噪声特征。这些诊断仅在OPSD风格的特权教师背景下进行分析，而CAST训练使用无答案的自教师评分。受这些观察启发，本工作提出了CAST，一种用于GRPO风格RLVR的无答案自蒸馏方法。CAST保留了基于验证器的GRPO目标，但使用停止梯度的自教师根据轨迹正确性来塑造令牌级优势。与先前的自蒸馏RLVR方法不同，CAST不需要参考解条件化的教师评分，在整个训练过程中保持自教师对数概率差距活跃，并应用双向局部优势符号反转：正确轨迹中教师负向的令牌可以接收负的令牌级优势，而错误轨迹中教师正向的令牌可以接收有界正向局部优势。对于零方差的全正确和全错误组，CAST分配有界符号约束的基础优势，从而使这些原本零梯度的组能够贡献具有验证器签名的令牌反馈。数学推理实验表明，CAST在改进RLVR训练的同时，保留了轻量级、基于验证器的轨迹级目标。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), especially Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), has been widely used to improve reasoning in large language models. However, outcome-level rewards provide only sparse supervision, and group-relative advantages vanish when all sampled trajectories for a prompt are either correct or incorrect. On-Policy Self-Distillation (OPSD) offers dense token-level guidance, but its token preferences are not necessarily aligned with trajectory correctness; empirical diagnostics show that OPSD signals behave differently on correct and incorrect rollouts, with teacher-positive and teacher-negative gap signals exhibiting different noise profiles. These diagnostics are conducted under an OPSD-style privileged teacher context for analysis only, whereas CAST training uses answer-free self-teacher scoring.Motivated by these observations, this work proposes CAST, an answer-free self-distillation method for GRPO-style RLVR. CAST keeps the verifier-grounded GRPO objective, but uses a stop-gradient self-teacher to shape token-level advantages according to trajectory correctness. Unlike prior self-distilled RLVR methods, CAST does not require reference-solution-conditioned teacher scoring, keeps the self-teacher log-probability gap active throughout training, and applies bidirectional local advantage sign reversal: teacher-negative tokens in correct trajectories can receive negative token-level advantages, while teacher-positive tokens in incorrect trajectories can receive bounded positive local advantages. For zero-variance all-correct and all-wrong groups, CAST assigns bounded sign-constrained base advantages, so these otherwise zero-gradient groups can contribute verifier-signed token feedback. Experiments on mathematical reasoning show that CAST improves RLVR training while retaining a lightweight, verifier-grounded trajectory-level objective.

</details>


### [25] [TraceGraph: Shared Decision Landscapes for Diagnosing and Improving Agent Trajectories](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31308v1)
*Junjie Nian,Kang Chen,Ge Zhang,Yixin Cao,Yugang Jiang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出TraceGraph框架诊断和改进agent轨迹，在SWE-bench上提升解决率，直接相关coding agent。

TL;DR: TraceGraph通过构建共享决策图并标记陷阱与修复，揭示了智能体轨迹中隐藏的行为差异，并利用陷阱检测提升了SWE-bench的解决率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体评估仅关注最终得分（如通过率），忽略了轨迹中的丰富过程信息，无法区分不同模型的导航策略差异。

Method: 将多模型轨迹池化构建状态图，基于结果标注生产核心与陷阱区域，将每个轨迹简化为访问、陷阱暴露和修复三个事件，并设计陷阱感知恢复流程（运行时检测+轻量级策略）。

Result: 在SWE-bench上，陷阱感知恢复使官方解决率从40.4%提升至43.5%（提供者触发子集）和从41.0%提升至44.8%（共同触发实例）。

Conclusion: TraceGraph提供了一个分析智能体基准测试的过程框架，能够揭示模型在共享景观上的差异，并利用失败区域指导性能改进。

中文摘要：智能体基准测试越来越多地记录丰富的交互轨迹，然而评估往往将每次运行简化为通过率或奖励分数。我们引入了TraceGraph，一个基于图的框架，将发布的多模型智能体轨迹转化为共享的决策景观。对于每个任务，TraceGraph在池化展开（引入模型身份之前）中基于可观测的动作-观测状态构建一个图。然后，它叠加由结果信息驱动的生产核心和陷阱区域，并用三个事件总结每次运行：访问、陷阱暴露和修复。跨越五个基准测试分割的轨迹中，TraceGraph特征揭示了被聚合分数隐藏的导航差异，并显示不同分割在奖励避免陷阱还是从陷阱中恢复方面有所不同。相同的TraceGraph景观还促使了SWE-bench上的陷阱感知恢复流程：一个运行时检测器在状态匹配历史陷阱区域时触发，然后从相同前缀评估轻量级连续策略。在触发状态下，最佳池化单因素策略将官方解决率从40.4%提高到43.5%（基于每个提供者的触发子集）以及从41.0%提高到44.8%（共同触发实例），且涉及提供者特定的活跃组件。总体而言，TraceGraph提供了一个过程词汇，用于询问智能体基准测试了什么、模型在共享景观上哪里出现分歧，以及失败区域如何指导下游改进。

Original abstract: Agent benchmarks increasingly record rich interaction trajectories, yet evaluation often reduces each rollout to a pass rate or reward score. We introduce TraceGraph, a graph-based framework that turns released multi-model agent trajectories into shared decision landscapes. For each task, TraceGraph builds a graph over observable action-observation states from pooled rollouts before model identity is introduced. It then overlays outcome-informed productive cores and trap regions, and summarizes each rollout with three events: Access, Trap exposure, and Repair. Across trajectories spanning five benchmark splits, TraceGraph profiles reveal navigation differences hidden by aggregate scores and show that splits differ in whether they reward avoiding traps or recovering from them. The same TraceGraph landscape also motivates a trap-aware recovery pipeline for SWE-bench: aruntime detector fires on states matching historical trap regions, then lightweight continuation policies are evaluated from the same prefix. On fired states, the best pooled single-factor policy raises official resolved rate from 40.4% to 43.5% on the per-provider fired subset and from 41.0% to 44.8% on common-fired instances, with provider-specific active components. Overall, TraceGraph provides a process vocabulary for asking what agent benchmarks test, where models diverge on a shared landscape, and how failure regions can guide downstream improvement.

### [26] [Diagnosing Failure Modes of Shared-State Collaboration in Resource-Constrained Visual Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31354v1)
*Yunpeng Zhou*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 诊断共享状态协作失败模式，对资源受限coding agent有启发。

TL;DR: 本文研究弱学习者模块化视觉推理中的失败模式，发现共享工作空间会放大幻觉，识别出噪声强化和策略崩溃两种失败模式，并指出通信保真度是资源受限智能体的瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 模块化视觉推理系统依赖共享工作记忆，但低容量机制下中间状态演变的失败动态未被充分探索。

Method: 提出CoSee审计框架，形式化读-写-验证循环，在多个视觉问答基准上分析失败模式，使用成本-准确性帕累托前沿评估。

Result: 发现共享工作空间反直觉地放大幻觉；识别出噪声强化和策略崩溃两种失败模式；增加计算量可能负相关于性能。

Conclusion: 对于资源受限智能体，瓶颈在于通信保真度而非推理深度，为可靠模块化设计提供诊断和基线。

中文摘要：模块化视觉推理系统越来越依赖共享工作记忆进行多步协作，然而低容量机制下中间状态演变的失败动态仍未得到充分探索。我们通过噪声累积的视角研究了弱学习者（4B-8B模型）协作推理的失败模式。我们引入了CoSee，一个审计框架，它形式化了读-写-验证循环，以追踪文档视觉问答中的信息流。在多页、图表和基于网页的基准测试中，我们发现了一个反直觉的退化：朴素的共享工作空间往往放大了幻觉，而不是解决它们。我们识别出两种主要的失败模式：噪声强化，即无根据的笔记被重复用作证据；以及策略崩溃，即添加的上下文使模型转向未指定的简短答案。通过成本-准确性帕累托前沿，我们表明增加计算量可能与性能负相关，而无需显式验证。我们的发现表明，对于资源受限的智能体，瓶颈不在于推理深度，而在于通信保真度，为可靠的模块化设计提供了痕迹级诊断和机制基线。

Original abstract: Modular visual reasoning systems increasingly rely on shared working memory for multi-step collaboration, yet the failure dynamics of intermediate state evolution in low-capacity regimes remain underexplored. We study failure modes of collaborative reasoning with weak learners (4B--8B models) through the lens of noise accumulation. We introduce CoSee, an auditing framework that formalizes the read-write-verify loop to trace information flow in document visual question answering. Across multi-page, chart, and web-based benchmarks, we find a counter-intuitive degradation: naive shared workspaces often amplify hallucinations rather than resolve them. We identify two dominant failure modes: Noise Reinforcement, where ungrounded notes are reused as evidence, and Policy Collapse, where added context shifts the model toward under-specified, short-form answers. Using cost-accuracy Pareto frontiers, we show that increased compute can correlate negatively with performance without explicit verification. Our findings suggest that for resource-constrained agents, the bottleneck lies not in reasoning depth but in communication fidelity, providing trace-level diagnostics and a mechanistic baseline for reliable modular design.

### [27] [Learning to Adapt: Self-Improving Web Agent via Cognitive-Aware Exploration](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31365v1)
*Weile Chen,Bingchen Miao,Qifan Yu,Wendong Bu,Guoming Wang,Wenqiao Zhang,Shengyu Zhang,Juncheng Li,Siliang Tang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有网络代理依赖手工流程或专家轨迹，适应性差，无法应对复杂动态环境。

Method: 提出SCALE框架，包含三个对抗角色（Selector, Predictor, Judger）和SCALE-Hop图探索策略，并构建大规模数据集SCALE-20k。

Result: 显著提升多种MLLMs在不同网络环境中的性能和泛化能力。

Conclusion: SCALE为构建自主、自适应的网络代理提供了可扩展且可泛化的解决方案。

中文摘要：多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）的最新进展推动了网络代理（web agents）的发展。然而，现有的网络代理通常依赖手工制作的执行流程或昂贵的专家轨迹，限制了它们在复杂动态环境中的适应性。为了解决这些挑战，我们提出了SCALE（自我认知学习与探索），它利用三个对抗角色——选择器（Selector）、预测器（Predictor）和裁判（Judger）——通过环境探索自主发现代理的局限性并扩展其认知边界。此外，我们提出了SCALE-Hop，一种图探索策略，促进全局规划并帮助代理避免局部探索陷阱。为了进一步支持学习，我们构建了SCALE-20k，一个从19个真实网站收集的大规模数据集，包含多样化的任务类型和由SCALE探索轨迹生成的结构化演示。实验结果表明，我们的方法显著提升了多种MLLMs在不同网络环境中的性能和泛化能力。我们的框架为构建真正自主和自适应的网络代理提供了一种可扩展且可泛化的解决方案。

Original abstract: Recent advances in Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have led to promising progress in web agents. However, existing web agents often rely on handcrafted execution pipelines or expensive expert trajectories, limiting their adaptability to complex, dynamic environments. To address these challenges, we propose SCALE (Self-Cognitive-Aware Learning and Exploration), which leverages three adversarial roles, Selector, Predictor, and Judger to autonomously discover the agent's limitations and expand its cognitive boundaries through environmental exploration. Moreover, we propose SCALE-Hop, a graph exploration strategy that facilitates global planning and helps agents avoid local exploration traps. To further support learning, we construct SCALE-20k, a large-scale dataset collected from 19 real-world websites, containing diverse task types and structured demonstrations generated from SCALE's exploration traces. Experimental results show that our approach significantly improves the performance and generalization of multiple MLLMs in various web environments. Our framework offers a scalable and generalizable solution for building truly autonomous and adaptive web agents.

### [28] [HypoAgent: An Agentic Framework for Interactive Abductive Hypothesis Generation over Knowledge Graphs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31370v1)
*Yisen Gao,Yixi Cai,Tianshi Zheng,Jiaxin Bai,Yangqiu Song*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent回溯假设生成框架，含意图识别与根因分析，可用于代码诊断。

TL;DR: 提出了HypoAgent框架，通过三个智能体（意图识别、假设生成、根因分析）解决知识图谱上交互式溯因假设生成中的多轮对话意图理解和失败诊断问题，达到SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有可控假设生成方法在多轮对话中难以理解不断变化的自然语言意图，且无法在生成假设失败时提供细粒度诊断。

Method: 提出HypoAgent框架，集成三个智能体：意图识别智能体将用户话语和历史转化为可执行条件；假设生成智能体根据意图生成假设；根因分析智能体诊断不可靠片段并通过KG邻域探测找到改进。

Result: 在常识和生物医学KG上，单轮、多轮和无条件设置下均达到最先进语义相似度。

Conclusion: HypoAgent能有效进行交互式溯因假设生成，实现多轮对话意图理解和失败诊断。

中文摘要：知识图谱上的溯因推理旨在生成能够解释观察到实体或事实的逻辑假设。现有的可控假设生成方法允许用户通过显式条件指导这一过程，但在交互式场景中仍存在局限：它们难以在多轮对话中理解不断变化的自然语言意图，并且在生成的假设失败时无法提供细粒度的诊断。为解决这些局限，我们提出了HypoAgent，一个用于知识图谱交互式溯因假设生成的智能体框架。HypoAgent集成了三个智能体：意图识别智能体，将用户话语和对话历史转化为可执行的知识图谱条件；假设生成智能体，根据提取的用户意图执行可控假设生成；根因分析智能体，诊断不可靠的假设片段，并利用知识图谱邻域探测来识别支持的改进。在常识和生物医学领域特定知识图谱上的实验表明，HypoAgent在单轮、多轮和无条件设置下均达到了最先进的语义相似度。我们的代码可在https://github.com/HKUST-KnowComp/HypoAgent获取。

Original abstract: Abductive reasoning over knowledge graphs aims to generate logical hypotheses that explain observed entities or facts. Existing controllable hypothesis generation methods allow users to guide this process with explicit conditions, but they remain limited in interactive settings: they struggle to ground evolving natural-language intents across multi-turn dialogues and provide little fine-grained diagnosis when generated hypotheses fail. To address these limitations, we propose HypoAgent, an Agentic framework for interactive abductive Hypothesis Generation over knowledge graphs. HypoAgent integrates three agents: an Intent Recognition Agent that grounds user utterances and dialogue history into executable KG conditions, a Hypothesis Generation Agent that performs controllable hypothesis generation according to the extracted user intention, and a Root Cause Analysis Agent that diagnoses unreliable hypothesis fragments and leverages KG neighborhood probing to identify supported refinements. Experiments on commonsense and biomedical domain-specific knowledge graphs demonstrate that HypoAgent achieves state-of-the-art semantic similarity under single-turn, multi-turn, and unconditional settings. Our code is available at https://github.com/HKUST-KnowComp/HypoAgent.

### [29] [AutoSci: A Memory-Centric Agentic System for the Full Scientific Research Lifecycle](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31468v1)
*Weitong Qian,Beicheng Xu,Zhongao Xie,Bowen Fan,Guozheng Tang,Jiale Chen,Xinzhe Wu,Mingtian Yang,Chenyang Di,Jiajun Li,Lingching Tung,Peichao Lai,Yifei Xia,Ziyi Guo,Yanwei Xu,Yanzhao Qin,Shaoduo Gan,Xupeng Miao,Bin Cui*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有系统无法同时满足支持完整研究生命周期、维护结构化持久记忆和自我进化流程的需求，存在统一自动化科学研究系统的缺口。

Method: 提出AutoSci系统，包含四个模块：SciMem提供模式管理的研究记忆（长期知识记忆和活动研究记忆）；SciFlow通过框架控制状态、上下文、验证、反馈和编排，执行从文献理解到反驳的五阶段生命周期；SciDAG使用DAG形状的多智能体操作符和阶段特定模板增强困难技能；SciEvolve将反馈信号转换为系统组件的版本化更新。

Result: AutoSci能跨研究项目执行、记忆和进化，成为持久的研究环境。

Conclusion: AutoSci通过以记忆为中心的设计，实现了完整的自动化科学研究流程。

中文摘要：科学研究传统上是人力密集型的工作，需要研究人员在漫长的项目周期中协调文献、想法、实验、手稿和审稿回复。基于LLM的科学智能体的兴起为自动化这一过程创造了机会。这样的系统必须支持完整的研究生命周期，跨项目维护结构化的持久记忆，并随时间改进其自身的研究流程。然而，现有系统要么部分满足要么未能满足这些要求，留下了一个统一自动化科学研究系统的缺口。因此，我们提出了AutoSci，一个以记忆为中心的智能体系统，用于完整的科学研究生命周期。AutoSci围绕四个模块组织。SciMem提供由模式管理的研究记忆，将可重复使用的科学知识的长期知识记忆与项目级工件（如想法、实验、手稿和审稿意见）的活动研究记忆分开。SciFlow通过一个控制状态、上下文、验证、反馈和编排的框架执行一个从文献理解到反驳的五阶段生命周期。SciDAG通过DAG形状的多智能体操作符和可重复使用的阶段特定模板增强了困难技能。SciEvolve将来自用户、实验、审稿和外部环境的反馈信号转换为对SciMem组织、SciFlow技能和SciDAG模板的版本化更新。这些模块共同使AutoSci成为一个持久的研究环境，可以跨研究项目执行、记忆和进化。代码仓库可在https://github.com/skyllwt/AutoSci获取。

Original abstract: Scientific research has traditionally been human-intensive, requiring researchers to coordinate literature, ideas, experiments, manuscripts, and review responses across long project cycles. The rise of LLM-based scientific agents creates an opportunity to automate this process. Such a system must support the full research lifecycle, maintain structured persistent memory across projects, and improve its own research procedures over time. However, existing systems either partially satisfy or fail to satisfy these requirements, leaving a gap for a unified automated scientific research system. As a result, we present AutoSci, a memory-centric agentic system for the full scientific research lifecycle. AutoSci is organized around four modules. SciMem provides schema-governed research memory, separating Long-Term Knowledge Memory for reusable scientific knowledge from Active Research Memory for project-level artifacts such as ideas, experiments, manuscripts, and reviews. SciFlow executes a five-stage lifecycle from literature understanding to rebuttal through a harness that controls state, context, verification, feedback, and orchestration. SciDAG augments difficult skills with DAG-shaped multi-agent operators and reusable stage-specific templates. SciEvolve converts feedback signals from users, experiments, reviews, and external environments into versioned updates to SciMem organization, SciFlow skills, and SciDAG templates. Together, these modules make AutoSci a persistent research environment that can execute, remember, and evolve across research projects. The code repository is available at https://github.com/skyllwt/AutoSci.

### [30] [LinTree: Improving LLM Reasoning with Explicitly Structured Search Histories](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31492v1)
*Liwei Kang,Yee Whye Teh,Wee Sun Lee*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 显式树结构改善LLM推理，对agent规划与搜索有启发

TL;DR: LLM的推理轨迹中隐式包含搜索树结构，但显式化该结构（如添加父指针）能显著提升性能和效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究LLM在推理时是否利用了其轨迹中隐含的搜索树结构优势，以及如何通过显式化该结构来改进推理。

Method: 在积木世界、网格导航和推箱子三个环境中，比较轨迹条件推理策略、最佳优先搜索（基于LLM启发式）以及添加父指针显式线性化树结构的模型。

Result: 仅凭原始搜索历史不足以超越启发式搜索；添加父指针显式表示树结构后，任务性能和搜索效率均优于隐式模型和启发式搜索。

Conclusion: 搜索历史在显式表示其树结构时最为有用，应推动LLM推理中采用更多结构感知的表示。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）通常通过生成中间轨迹来解决推理问题，这些轨迹探索并修改部分解决方案。从搜索的角度来看，这些轨迹可以被视为线性化的搜索树，其中模型扩展部分解决方案，在失败时放弃它，并回溯以尝试替代方案。与传统的启发式引导搜索相比，这种策略有一个潜在优势：它基于整个搜索轨迹而非仅当前局部状态进行条件化。我们首先通过将轨迹条件推理策略与配备仅观察当前局部状态的LLM启发式的最佳优先搜索进行比较，来测试LLM是否利用了这一优势。在三个受控推理环境（积木世界、网格导航和推箱子）中，我们发现仅凭原始搜索历史的访问权不足以可靠地超越启发式搜索。然后我们研究了一个可能的原因：在LLM推理轨迹中，底层搜索树仅被隐式表示，当模型回溯或切换分支时，轨迹并未明确标识正在重新访问哪个先前的搜索状态。我们表明，添加简单的父指针以显式表示线性化树（LinTree）结构，相比隐式推理模型和LLM启发式引导搜索，能提高任务性能和搜索效率。这些结果表明，当树结构被显式化时，搜索历史变得最为有用，从而激励在LLM推理中采用更多结构感知的表示。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) often solve reasoning problems by generating intermediate traces that explore and revise partial solutions. From a search perspective, these traces can be viewed as linearized search trees, where the model extends a partial solution, abandons it when it fails, and backtracks to try alternatives. Compared with traditional heuristic-guided search, such a policy has a potential advantage: it conditions on the whole search trace rather than only on the current local state. We first test whether LLMs utilize this advantage by comparing trace-conditioned reasoning policies against best-first search equipped with an LLM heuristic that only observes the current local state. Across three controlled reasoning environments, Blocks World, grid Navigation, and Sokoban, we find that raw access to search history alone is not enough to reliably outperform heuristic search. We then study one possible reason: in LLM reasoning traces, the underlying search tree is only implicitly represented, and when the model backtracks or switches branches, the trace does not explicitly identify which earlier search state is being revisited. We show that adding simple parent pointers to explicitly represent the linearized tree (LinTree) structure improves both task performance and search efficiency relative to implicit reasoning models and LLM-heuristic-guided search. These results suggest that search history becomes most useful when its tree structure is made explicit, motivating more structure-aware representations for LLM reasoning.

</details>


### [31] [TIGER: Traceable Inference with Graph-Based Evidence Routing for Mitigating Hallucinations in Multimodal Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00232v1)
*Kaixiang Zhao,Tianrun Yu,Shawn Huang,Porter Jenkins,Yushun Dong,Amanda Hughes*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 推理时修复多模态幻觉，方法可应用于agent生成修复。

TL;DR: TIGER通过独立提取输入和输出的图表示并分配风险分数，在推理时局部修复多模态生成中的事实级幻觉。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有推理时修复方法因输出中的幻觉偏差输入解读且无法在事实级排序反馈而受限。

Method: TIGER独立从输入提取观察图、从输出提取声明图，根据支持与冲突为每个声明分配图条件风险分数，然后选择性修复高风险声明而保持主干冻结。

Result: 在图像到文本、图像+文本到文本、音频到文本和视频到文本四种跨模态路径上，TIGER减少不支持内容并保持任务质量，增益在多个主干上一致，且CrisisFACTS案例表明可改善多源接地。

Conclusion: TIGER为多模态生成提供有效的事实级修复机制，可推广至多源设置，具有理论收敛保证。

中文摘要：我们研究多模态生成中的事实级修复，其中流畅的输出可能包含输入不支持的具体事实。现有的推理时修复方法通常通过联合条件化输入和当前输出来生成反馈。这种设计有两个局限性：输出中的幻觉声明可能偏差模型对输入的解读，且自由形式的反馈无法在事实级进行排序或调度。我们提出TIGER，一个推理时框架，重新设计反馈以实现局部修复。TIGER独立从输入中提取观察图，从当前输出中提取声明图，然后根据支持和冲突为每个声明分配一个图条件风险分数。该模型在保持主干冻结的同时修复选定的高风险声明。我们提供了一个收敛性分析，表明在温和假设下，期望总风险几何级数递减到一个明确的渐近界限。跨四种跨模态路径的实验，包括图像到文本、图像+文本到文本、音频到文本和视频到文本，表明TIGER减少了不支持内容同时保持了任务质量。该增益在多个主干上成立，并且一个CrisisFACTS案例研究表明相同的修复机制可以改善多源设置中的接地。

Original abstract: We study fact-level repair for multimodal generation, where a fluent output may contain specific facts that are not supported by the input. Existing inference-time repair methods often generate feedback by jointly conditioning on the input and the current output. This design has two limitations: hallucinated claims in the output can bias the model's interpretation of the input, and free-form feedback cannot be ranked or scheduled at the fact level. We present TIGER, an inference-time framework that redesigns feedback for localized repair. TIGER independently extracts an observation graph from the input and a claim graph from the current output, then assigns each claim a graph-conditioned risk score based on support and conflict. The model repairs selected high-risk claims while keeping the backbone frozen. We provide a convergence analysis showing that the expected total risk decreases geometrically to an explicit asymptotic bound under mild assumptions. Experiments across four cross-modal paths, including image-to-text, image+text-to-text, audio-to-text, and video-to-text, show that TIGER reduces unsupported content while preserving task quality. The gains hold across multiple backbones, and a CrisisFACTS case study suggests that the same repair mechanism can improve grounding in multi-source settings.

### [32] [MindZero: Learning Online Mental Reasoning With Zero Annotations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00240v1)
*Shunchi Zhang,Jin Lu,Chuanyang Jin,Yichao Zhou,Zhining Zhang,Tianmin Shu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出自我监督强化学习训练 MLLM 进行在线心理推理，可迁移到 agent 规划与状态推断。

TL;DR: MindZero是一个自监督强化学习框架，训练多模态大语言模型进行高效鲁棒的在线心理推理，无需显式标注，在准确性和效率上优于基于模型的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有心理推理方法面临在线推断、实时效率和缺乏标注的挑战，需要更高效且无需标注的解决方案。

Method: 提出MindZero框架，采用自监督强化学习，模型通过生成最大化规划器估计的观察动作似然的心理状态假设来获得奖励，从而内化基于模型的推理为单次前向传播。

Result: 在网格世界和家庭领域的任务中，MindZero显著优于LLM基线和基于模型的方法，在准确性和效率上均表现更佳。

Conclusion: 心理推理可以作为自监督技能有效学习，MindZero增强了MLLM的内在ToM能力，无需显式标注即可实现高效在线推理。

中文摘要：有效的现实世界辅助需要AI代理具有强大的心理理论（ToM）：从人类行为推断心理状态。尽管最近取得了进展，但仍存在几个关键挑战，包括（1）在线推断，对多个假设进行鲁棒的置信度更新；（2）适合实时辅助的高效推理；（3）在现实领域缺乏真实心理状态标注。我们通过引入MindZero来解决这些挑战，这是一个自监督强化学习框架，训练多模态大语言模型（MLLM）进行高效且鲁棒的在线心理推理。在训练过程中，模型因生成能够最大化由规划器估计的观察动作似然的心理状态假设而获得奖励，类似于基于模型的ToM推理。因此，该方法消除了对显式心理状态标注的需求。训练后，MindZero将基于模型的推理内化为快速的单次推理。我们在网格世界和家庭领域的具有挑战性的心理推理和AI辅助任务中评估了MindZero与基线。我们发现，仅靠LLM是不够的；基于模型的方法提高了准确性，但速度慢、成本高，并且受限于骨干MLLM容量。相比之下，MindZero增强了MLLM的内在ToM能力，在准确性和效率上都显著优于基于模型的方法，表明心理推理可以作为自监督技能有效学习。

Original abstract: Effective real-world assistance requires AI agents with robust Theory of Mind (ToM): inferring human mental states from their behavior. Despite recent advances, several key challenges remain, including (1) online inference with robust uncertainty updates over multiple hypotheses; (2) efficient reasoning suitable for real-time assistance; and (3) the lack of ground-truth mental state annotations in real-world domains. We address these challenges by introducing MindZero, a self-supervised reinforcement learning framework that trains multimodal large language models (MLLMs) for efficient and robust online mental reasoning. During training, the model is rewarded for generating mental state hypotheses that maximize the likelihood of observed actions estimated by a planner, similar to model-based ToM reasoning. This method thus eliminates the need for explicit mental state annotations. After training, MindZero internalizes model-based reasoning into fast single-pass inference. We evaluate MindZero against baselines across challenging mental reasoning and AI assistance tasks in gridworld and household domains. We found that LLMs alone are insufficient; model-based methods improve accuracy but are slow, costly, and limited by backbone MLLM capacity. In contrast, MindZero enhances MLLMs' intrinsic ToM ability and significantly outperforms model-based methods in both accuracy and efficiency, showing that mental reasoning can be effectively learned as a self-supervised skill.
