### [33] [Capability Self-Assessment: Teaching LLMs to Know Their Limits](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00251v1)
*Haoyan Yang,Reza Shirkavand,Yukai Jin,Jiawei Zhou,Shangqian Gao,Heng Huang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 用强化学习训练 LLM 进行能力自我评估，可迁移到 agent 自我反思与任务委派。

TL;DR: 大型语言模型普遍缺乏能力自我评估（CSA），常高估自身能力。强化学习能有效提升CSA，且优于监督微调，同时保留原有能力；CSA具有分布外泛化性和实际用途。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可靠的智能系统需要识别自身局限性并决定是否委派任务，但现代LLM系统性地缺乏这一能力，因此需要改进其自我评估。

Method: 将能力自我评估（CSA）建模为策略学习问题，使用强化学习（RL）进行训练，并与监督微调（SFT）对比。

Result: RL显著优于SFT，在提升CSA的同时保留原始能力，而SFT严重损害原始能力；习得的CSA能泛化到分布外场景。

Conclusion: CSA是可迁移的模型特质，具有实际价值：优化推理时的本地-云端决策，并为训练中的目标数据选择提供信号。

中文摘要：识别自身局限性并决定是解决问题还是委派任务的能力，对于可靠的智能系统至关重要。然而，我们表明现代大型语言模型系统性地缺乏这种能力：在不同的模型家族和规模中，它们高估自身能力并尝试无法解决的查询。我们将这种能力称为能力自我评估（CSA），并将其表述为一个策略学习问题，旨在改善自我评估的同时保留模型的原始能力。我们的结果表明，强化学习能有效教授CSA，显著优于监督微调，同时保留了原始能力。相反，监督微调严重削弱了模型本应评估的能力。此外，习得的自我评估行为能很好地泛化到分布外，表明CSA是一种可迁移的模型特质。最后，CSA具有实际用途：它在推理时改进了本地-云端决策，并在训练中为目标数据选择提供了信号。

Original abstract: The ability to recognize one's own limitations and decide whether to solve a problem or delegate is fundamental for reliable intelligent systems. Yet we show that modern large language models systematically lack this ability: across diverse model families and scales, they overestimate their competence and attempt queries they cannot solve. We refer to this ability as Capability Self-Assessment (CSA) and formulate it as a policy-learning problem, aiming to improve self-assessment while preserving the model's original capabilities. Our results show that reinforcement learning teaches CSA effectively, significantly outperforming supervised fine-tuning while preserving original capabilities. In contrast, supervised fine-tuning severely degrades the capabilities the model is meant to assess. Moreover, learned self-assessment behavior generalizes well out of distribution, suggesting that CSA is a transferable model trait. Finally, CSA is practically useful: it improves local-cloud decision making at inference time and provides a signal for targeted data selection during training.

### [34] [Closed-Loop Neural Activation Control in Vision-Language-Action Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00269v1)
*Abhijith Babu,Ramneet Kaur,Nathaniel D. Bastian,Olivera Kotevska,Susmit Jha,Yanzhao Wu,Sumit Kumar Jha,Anirban Roy*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 闭环控制 VLA 模型实现自适应干预，对 agent 行为稳定性控制有参考。

TL;DR: 提出CTRL-STEER闭环框架，通过自适应时变控制信号替代固定引导系数，实现更稳定的VLA模型引导，在LIBERO任务上优于基线且无需重训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLA模型使用固定引导系数以开环方式运行，不适合具身控制中任务状态和概念误差的动态变化，导致过度校正、振荡和任务成功率下降。

Method: 提出CTRL-STEER闭环框架，将表示与调节解耦，沿运动对齐的残差方向进行引导，并使用反馈控制器（如PID和强化学习）在线自适应调整干预幅度。

Result: 在四个LIBERO任务套件上，CTRL-STEER实现了比固定系数基线更稳定的概念调节和更好的引导-任务成功权衡。

Conclusion: CTRL-STEER无需修改或重新训练基础模型即可提升引导性能，为VLA模型在具身控制中的自适应引导提供了有效方案。

中文摘要：视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型可以在测试时通过干预语义上有意义的内部方向来进行引导，但现有方法使用固定的引导系数，实际上以开环方式运行。这不太适合具身控制，因为任务状态和概念误差会随时间演变，通常导致过度校正、振荡以及任务成功率下降，尤其是对于速度和平滑性等时间行为。我们提出了CTRL-STEER，一种闭环框架，用自适应的时变控制信号替代静态干预强度。关键思想是将表示与调节解耦：我们不是假设时间概念直接由单个神经元控制，而是沿着运动对齐的残差方向进行引导，同时反馈控制器在线调整干预幅度。我们使用基于PID和强化学习的控制器实例化该框架。在四个LIBERO任务套件上使用微调的OpenVLA策略进行的实验表明，CTRL-STEER实现了比固定系数基线更稳定的概念调节和更好的引导-任务成功权衡，且无需修改或重新训练基础模型。

Original abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models can be steered at test time by intervening on semantically meaningful internal directions, but existing methods use a fixed steering coefficient, effectively operating in open loop. This is poorly suited to embodied control, where task state and concept error evolve over time, often causing overcorrection, oscillation, and reduced task success, especially for temporal behaviors such as speed and smoothness. We propose CTRL-STEER, a closed-loop framework that replaces static intervention strength with adaptive, time-varying control signals. The key idea is to decouple representation from regulation: rather than assuming temporal concepts are directly controlled by individual neurons, we steer along motion-aligned residual directions while a feedback controller adjusts intervention magnitude online. We instantiate this framework with both PID and reinforcement learning based controllers. Experiments with a fine-tuned OpenVLA policy on four LIBERO task suites show that CTRL-STEER achieves more stable concept regulation and a better steering-task success trade-off than fixed-coefficient baselines, without modifying or retraining the base model.

</details>


### [35] [Robust Shielding for Safe Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00270v1)
*Edwin Hamel-De le Court,Thom Badings,Alessandro Abate,Francesco Belardinelli,Francesco Fabiano*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 基于鲁棒 MDP 的屏蔽框架保证强化学习 agent 安全，对 agent 安全控制有重要借鉴。

TL;DR: 提出一种针对鲁棒MDP的屏蔽框架，结合PAC采样方法，保证安全性且最优，实验验证有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有屏蔽技术假设已知安全相关的转移动态，但实际中难以满足，需要处理不确定性。

Method: 使用鲁棒MDP建模转移概率的不确定性，定义LTL安全阈值，设计屏蔽框架并证明其合理性和最优性，结合PAC采样学习转移概率。

Result: 实验表明该方法在未知MDP中保证安全性，随样本增加恢复强期望回报。

Conclusion: 为未知MDP提供了有效且最优的安全屏蔽方法。

中文摘要：屏蔽是一种有效的方法，用于在马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）中正式保证强化学习智能体的安全性。然而，现有的屏蔽技术通常假设已知安全相关的转移动态——这一要求在现实中很少得到满足。为了解决这一限制，我们为鲁棒MDP（RMDP）引入了一种新颖的屏蔽框架，即具有转移概率集合的MDP。我们将安全性定义为在RMDP的最坏情况转移概率下，以一定阈值概率满足线性时序逻辑（LTL）公式。我们证明了我们的屏蔽框架对于RMDP既是合理的也是最优的：屏蔽所允许的每个策略都是安全的，反之，每个安全的RMDP策略都被屏蔽所允许。我们将我们的方法与现有的采样方法相结合，以学习具有可能近似正确（PAC）保证的MDP转移概率。这种组合使得能够构建对于MDP的屏蔽，这些屏蔽以高置信度保证安全性，同时保持最小限制。我们的实验表明，我们为学习到的RMDP构建的屏蔽在未知MDP中保证了安全性，同时随着样本数量的增加恢复了强大的期望回报。

Original abstract: Shielding is an effective approach to formally guarantee the safety of reinforcement learning agents in Markov decision processes (MDPs). However, existing shielding techniques typically assume knowledge of the safety-relevant transition dynamics - a requirement that is seldom met in practice. To address this limitation, we introduce a novel shielding framework for robust MDPs (RMDPs), i.e., MDPs with sets of transition probabilities. We define safety as the satisfaction of a linear temporal logic (LTL) formula with a certain threshold probability under the worst-case transition probabilities of the RMDP. We prove that our shielding framework is both sound and optimal for the RMDP: every policy admissible by the shield is safe, and conversely, every safe RMDP policy is admissible by the shield. We combine our approach with existing sampling methods for learning transition probabilities of MDPs with probably approximately correct (PAC) guarantees. This combination enables the construction of shields for MDPs that, with high confidence, guarantee safety while remaining minimally restrictive. Our experiments show that our shields for learned RMDPs guarantee safety in unknown MDPs while recovering strong expected return as the number of samples increases.

### [36] [Model-Native Computing Architecture: Envisioning Future System Architecture Through the Lens of Computer Architecture](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00288v3)

Method: 采用愿景性综述方法，类比计算机架构概念，分析现有LLM系统文献，提出ICA六层架构和双平面模型（概率执行平面与确定性控制平面），并设计三个启发式规则（语义局部性、上下文预算、智能体加速比）。

Result: 提出ICA架构和启发式规则，用已发布数据说明参数范围，并识别预测验证为开放任务。本文无新实验结果。

Conclusion: 计算机架构类比可用于指导LLM系统设计，但需注意类比边界和差异。需进一步验证启发式规则的有效性，并推动统一模型原生系统架构的研究。

中文摘要：大型语言模型正在经历从模型技术向系统技术的转变。缓存复用、上下文容量、智能体调度和权限控制等工程挑战类似于经典的计算机系统问题。这引发了一个问题：如果我们把LLM视为CPU，KV缓存视为处理器缓存，上下文窗口视为主内存，智能体框架视为操作系统，那么几十年的计算机架构智慧能否指导下一代模型原生系统？本文以这一类比为基础进行了一篇愿景性综述。我们将计算机架构概念映射到新兴的模型原生堆栈上，综述了LLM作为操作系统、内存管理、智能体框架、工具协议、多智能体协调、认知架构和安全治理等方面的文献，发现每个方面都解决了不同层次的问题，但缺乏统一的模型。我们提出了智能计算架构（ICA）：六个功能层，带有接口契约和设计公理。我们通过一个双平面架构——概率执行平面（可以计算什么）和确定性控制平面（应该计算什么）——解决了关于LLM类似于CPU还是操作系统的争论，每一层都作为一个分级交叉通道。我们提出了三个阿姆达尔风格的设计启发式规则：语义局部性、上下文预算和智能体加速比，作为粗略估算模型，用已发布的数据说明其参数范围，并将预测验证确定为主要的未解决任务。我们阐明了类比的边界，指出了硅时代和模型时代架构之间的差异，并提出了一条研究路线图。这是一个概念性和综述性的贡献，没有新的实验结果。

Original abstract: Large language models are undergoing a transition from model technology to system technology. Engineering challenges like cache reuse, context capacity, agent scheduling, and permission control resemble classical computer systems problems. This raises a question: if we treat the LLM as a CPU, KV cache as processor cache, context window as main memory, and agent framework as an operating system, can decades of computer architecture wisdom guide next generation model native systems?
  This paper pursues this analogy as a visionary survey. We map computer architecture concepts onto the emerging model native stack, survey literature across LLM as OS, memory management, agent frameworks, tool protocols, multi agent coordination, cognitive architectures, and safety governance, finding that each addresses a different layer without a unifying model. We propose the Intelligent Computing Architecture (ICA): six functional layers with interface contracts and design axioms. We resolve the tension over whether the LLM resembles a CPU or OS via a dual plane architecture a probabilistic execution plane (what can be computed) and a deterministic control plane (what should be computed), with every layer passing through as a graded crossover.
  We propose three Amdahl style design heuristics Semantic Locality, Context Budget, and Agent Speedup as organizing back of envelope models, illustrate their parameter ranges with published data, and identify predictive validation as the principal open task. We articulate analogy boundaries, note differences between silicon and model era architectures, and propose a research roadmap. This is a conceptual and survey contribution with no new experimental results.

</details>


### [37] [The Deterministic Horizon: When Extended Reasoning Fails and Tool Delegation Becomes Necessary](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00376v1)
*Dongxin Guo,Jikun Wu,Siu Ming Yiu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究扩展推理失败与工具必要性，直接涉及agent工具使用与架构

TL;DR: 链式推理在确定性状态追踪任务中性能下降源于注意力容量限制，理论分析和实验表明工具集成模型优于纯神经推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究扩展链式推理在确定性状态追踪任务中性能下降的根本原因，并指导何时应采用混合方法。

Method: 提出了注意力瓶颈定理、上下文相关错误模型、状态空间Jaccard度量，并通过12个模型和8个任务领域的实验验证理论。

Result: 建立了状态追踪容量上限（O(H·log(L/H)·√d_h)），发现确定性视界d*∈[19,31]；工具集成推理准确率86-94%对比神经链式推理24-42%；微调改进<5%，跨模型相关性高（r=0.81-0.91）。

Conclusion: 纯神经推理存在架构天花板，对于确定性视界以上的任务应转向工具集成的混合方法。

中文摘要：扩展的链式推理可能会降低确定性状态追踪任务的性能，这不是由于偏好偏差，而是源于仅解码器注意力的信息论容量限制。我们建立了：（1）注意力瓶颈定理及互补的可实现性构造，将状态追踪容量界定为 $O(H \cdot \log(L/H) \cdot \sqrt{d_h})$；（2）一个上下文相关的错误模型，产生超指数级的精度衰减；（3）状态空间Jaccard度量，用于区分能力失败与偏好失败；（4）确定性视界 $d^* \in [19, 31]$，超过该视界则工具委托变得必要。在12个模型和8个任务领域（包括SWE-Bench、WebArena和SQL-Multi）中，工具集成的推理始终优于神经链式推理；在主要模型套件上，它达到86-94%的准确率，而神经链式推理仅为24-42%。在最优长度轨迹上进行微调仅带来<5%的改进，证实了架构天花板，且跨模型的高相关性（$r = 0.81$-$0.91$）表明这些失败是架构性的而非训练特有的。我们的结果为在代理系统中何时纯神经推理应让位于混合方法提供了原则性指导。

Original abstract: Extended chain-of-thought reasoning can degrade performance on deterministic state-tracking tasks, not due to preference biases, but limits rooted in the information-theoretic capacity of decoder-only attention. We establish: (1) an Attention Bottleneck Theorem with a complementary achievability construction, bounding state-tracking capacity as $O(H \cdot \log(L/H) \cdot \sqrt{d_h})$; (2) a context-dependent error model yielding super-exponential accuracy decay; (3) the State-Space Jaccard metric distinguishing capability from preference failures; (4) a Deterministic Horizon $d^* \in [19, 31]$ beyond which tool delegation becomes necessary. Across 12 models and 8 task domains (including SWE-Bench, WebArena, and SQL-Multi), tool-integrated reasoning consistently outperforms neural chain-of-thought; on the primary model suite it reaches 86-94% accuracy versus 24-42% for neural chain-of-thought. Fine-tuning on optimal-length traces yields $<$5% improvement, confirming an architectural ceiling, and high cross-model correlation ($r = 0.81$-$0.91$) indicates these failures are architectural rather than training-specific. Our results provide principled guidance for when pure neural reasoning should yield to hybrid approaches in agentic systems.

</details>


### [38] [VESTA: Visual Exploration with Statistical Tool Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00384v2)
*William Rudman,Abhishek Divekar,Kanishk Jain,Sebastian Joseph,Stella S. R. Offner,Matthew Lease,Kyle Mahowald,Greg Durrett,Junyi Jessy Li*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: VESTA框架：VLM agent动态创建工具进行统计建模，通用工具使用与探索方法可迁移

TL;DR: VESTA是一个框架，通过动态增长的探索工具包增强VLM，在模型拟合中主动探索数据，显著提升复杂建模任务性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动化建模系统在复杂任务上表现不佳，缺乏主动数据探索和动态工具创建能力。

Method: 提出VESTA框架，为VLM配备动态探索工具包，通过选择或创建诊断工具进行数据转换、可视化及统计检验，并引入DAWN基准评估。

Result: 动态工具创建优于基线，在复杂和领域特定任务上增益最大，生成工具更复杂且偏好可视输出。

Conclusion: VESTA通过主动探索和动态工具创建有效提升模型拟合自动化水平，尤其在复杂任务中优势明显。

中文摘要：将定量模型拟合到数据是科学工作流程中的核心步骤，然而它仍然是自动化程度最低的环节之一。最近的基于智能体的系统利用语言模型和视觉语言模型（VLM）来迭代地提出和改进统计模型，但这些系统在更具挑战性的建模任务上表现不佳。为了解决这些局限性，我们引入了VESTA：视觉探索与统计工具智能体，这是一个框架，它为VLM配备了一个动态增长的探索工具包，通过数据转换、假设驱动的可视化和稳健的统计检验来指导模型改进。与以往仅依赖迭代批评的系统不同，VESTA在模型改进之前和过程中通过选择或创建诊断工具来主动探索数据，这些工具会累积在模型的上下文中，并可在后续重用。我们在三种工具包配置下（无工具、静态专家编写工具和动态模型编写工具）评估了VESTA与既定基线的表现。为支持这一评估，我们引入了DAWN（自动化工作流与数值建模数据集），一个针对分布拟合和时间序列建模的基准，包含不同难度等级，并最终涵盖真实世界的天文学任务，包括建模初始质量函数和引力波啁啾信号。我们发现，VESTA的动态工具创建优于以往的智能体流程，在复杂和领域特定任务上增益最大。我们还进一步证明，动态生成的工具比现有视觉工具创建系统生成的工具复杂得多，每个功能覆盖更多诊断类别，并且强烈偏好VLM批评者可以直接推理的视觉输出。

Original abstract: Fitting quantitative models to data is a central step in scientific workflows, yet it remains one of the least automated. Recent agent-based systems leverage language and vision-language models (VLMs) to iteratively propose and refine statistical models, but these systems struggle on more challenging modeling tasks. To address these limitations, we introduce VESTA: Visual Exploration with Statistical Tool Agents, a framework that equips VLMs with a dynamically growing exploration toolkit to guide model refinement through data transformations, hypothesis-driven visualizations, and robust statistical tests. Unlike prior systems that rely on iterative critique alone, VESTA actively explores data before and during refinement by selecting or creating diagnostic tools, which accumulate in the model's context and can be reused later. We evaluate VESTA against established baselines in three toolkit configurations: no tools, static expert-written tools, and dynamic model-written tools. To support this evaluation, we introduce DAWN (Dataset for Automated Workflows and Numerical Modeling), a benchmark targeting distribution fitting and time series modeling with varying difficulty tiers, and culminating in real-world astronomy tasks including modeling initial mass functions and gravitational-wave chirp signals. We find that VESTA's dynamic tool creation outperforms prior agentic pipelines, with the largest gains on complex and domain-specific tasks. We further show that dynamically generated tools are substantially more sophisticated than those produced by existing visual tool-creation systems, covering more diagnostic categories per function and strongly preferring visual outputs that the VLM critic can reason over directly.

</details>


### [39] [Weak Critics Make Strong Learners: On-Policy Critique Distillation for Scalable Oversight](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00424v1)
*Can Jin,Jiakang Li,Rui Wu,Eddy Zhang,Dimitris N. Metaxas*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出弱批评者进行监督的自我改进机制，可应用于agent的反馈与自我反思训练。

TL;DR: 提出弱批评者强监督设置，通过弱模型提供非误导性修订方向，并采用OPCD方法蒸馏，提升强模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弱监督者难以提供可靠标签或判断，限制了弱到强泛化和可扩展监督。

Method: 使用弱模型作为批评者提供修订方向，提出OPCD方法过滤高质量批评并蒸馏到强模型。

Result: 在推理和对齐基准上，强模型性能随训练周期持续提升。

Conclusion: 该方法为弱监督下的可扩展监督提供了有效路径。

中文摘要：随着大型语言模型变得更强，弱监督者可能无法为复杂输出提供可靠的标签、偏好或最终判断，从而限制了弱到强泛化和可扩展监督。我们研究了一种更易处理的弱监督形式：使用弱模型作为批评者，而不是作为标注者或判断者。弱批评者不需要解决任务或选择正确答案，只需要提供一个非误导性的修订方向，帮助强模型更好地利用自身知识。我们称这种设置为弱批评者强监督。我们首先表明，弱批评可以在推理时改进冻结的强模型，并且批评质量是这种改进的关键。然后，我们提出了渐进式在线策略批评蒸馏（OPCD），它过滤高质量的批评，并通过自适应自我教师信号将批评引导的行为蒸馏到强模型中。在推理和对齐基准上的实验表明，我们的方法在训练周期内改进了强模型，表明了一条使用弱监督进行可扩展监督的有效路径。

Original abstract: As large language models become stronger, weak supervisors may fail to provide reliable labels, preferences, or final judgments for complex outputs, limiting both weak-to-strong generalization and scalable oversight. We study a more tractable form of weak supervision: using a weak model as a critic rather than as a labeler or judge. Instead of solving the task or selecting the correct answer, the weak critic only needs to provide a non-misleading revision direction that helps the strong model better use its own knowledge. We call this setting *weak-critic strong oversight*. We first show that weak critiques can improve frozen strong models at inference time, and that critique quality is key to this improvement. We then propose progressive on-policy critique distillation (**OPCD**), which filters high-quality critiques and distills critic-guided behavior into the strong model through adaptive self-teacher signals. Experiments on reasoning and alignment benchmarks show that our method improves strong models over training epochs, suggesting an effective path for scalable oversight with weak supervision.

</details>

### [40] [Fighting Numerical Hallucinations via Data-centric Compilation for Online Financial QA](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31064v1)
*Hao Chen,Xing Tang,Qirui Liu,Weijie Shi,Shiwei Li,Fuyuan Lyu,Weihong Luo,Xiku Du,Xiuqiang He*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: 数据编译用于金融QA agent，可迁移至coding agent的检索与规划。

TL;DR: 提出数据为中心推理编译器DCRC，通过对抗性数据构建、多阶段训练和编译执行推理，解决金融问答中数值推理幻觉问题，提升鲁棒性和可审计性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM在金融问答中存在数值推理幻觉，RAG虽常用但带来噪声、计算脆弱性和审计危机，模型中心方法无法集成解决这些问题。

Method: 提出DCRC框架，包含三个连贯阶段：1) 对抗性数据构建合成含噪训练样本；2) 多阶段训练培养数据为中心结构化智能体（DSA）进行证据审计和程序合成；3) 编译并执行推理过程，将查询和文档转换为可执行程序。

Result: 在离线基准和在线金融QA系统实验中验证了框架的有效性，确保忠实数值推理。

Conclusion: 数据为中心的DCRC框架通过设计实现了可信的数值推理，有效克服了RAG的三大挑战，并在实际系统中得到验证。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）显著提升了在线数据服务，尤其是在金融问答（FinQA）领域。然而，这类系统仍然容易受到数值推理幻觉的影响，这在高风险的金融应用中严重削弱了可靠性。尽管检索增强生成（RAG）被广泛采用以通过外部知识来锚定响应，但它引入了三个持续存在的挑战：噪声敏感性、计算脆弱性和可审计性危机。现有的以模型为中心的方法主要侧重于单独优化检索器或生成器，仍然难以以集成的方式解决这些问题。在这项工作中，我们开创了一种以数据为中心的范式，并提出了一个新颖的框架——数据为中心推理编译器（DCRC）。该框架通过三个连贯的阶段运行：（1）对抗性数据构建，合成带有受控噪声的训练示例以教授鲁棒性；（2）多阶段训练，培养一个能够进行显式证据审计和程序合成的数据为中心结构化智能体（DSA）；（3）编译并执行的推理过程，其中DSA将用户查询和检索到的文档转换为可验证、可执行的推理程序。这种数据驱动的框架通过设计确保了忠实的数值推理。我们在已建立的离线基准上进行了大量实验，并通过在真实世界的在线金融问答系统中的部署进一步验证了我们的框架。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have significantly advanced online data services, particularly in the domain of financial question answering (FinQA). However, such systems remain susceptible to numerical reasoning hallucinations, which critically undermine reliability in high-stakes financial applications. Although retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) has been widely adopted to ground responses in external knowledge, it introduces three persistent challenges: noise sensitivity, calculation fragility, and an auditability crisis. Existing model-centric approaches, which primarily focus on optimizing either the retriever or generator in isolation, still struggle to address these issues in an integrated manner. In this work, we pioneer a data-centric paradigm and propose a novel framework, the Data-centric Reasoning Compiler (DCRC). The framework operates through three cohesive phases: (1) adversarial data construction, which synthesizes training examples with controlled noise to teach robustness; (2) multi-stage training that cultivates a Data-centric Structuring Agent (DSA) capable of explicit evidence auditing and program synthesis; and (3) a compile-and-execute inference process, where the DSA transforms user queries and retrieved documents into verifiable, executable reasoning programs. This data-driven framework ensures faithful numerical reasoning by design. We conduct extensive experiments on established offline benchmarks and further validate our framework through deployment in a real-world online financial QA system.

</details>


### [41] [DynaTree: Dynamic Agentic Retrieval Tree for Time-Sensitive News Retrieval](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31377v1)
*Siyuan Qi,Xinyuan Wang,Yingxuan Yang,Haochuan Guo,Jianghao Lin,Weiwen Liu,Yong Yu,Weinan Zhang*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: agentic检索树框架，离线规划+在线选择，可用于代码检索agent。

TL;DR: DynaTree通过离线构建可重用的检索树和在线轻量级子树选择，实现了高效自适应新闻检索，在多个数据集和真实部署中表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有agentic RAG方法耦合语义扩展与检索决策，导致推理成本高且不适合时间敏感的新闻检索。

Method: 两阶段框架：离线阶段用协调智能体构建检索树；在线阶段进行轻量级每日子树选择，无需额外推理。

Result: 在Syft和BEIR数据集上优于标准RAG和基线；生产部署中动态变体显著提升生存率，超过现有生产回忆器。

Conclusion: 持久的结构感知语义扩展能将离线智能体推理转化为实际新闻检索中覆盖、新鲜度和相关性的提升。

中文摘要：Agentic Retrieval-Augmented Generation通过整合规划、工具使用和迭代推理来改进检索，但现有的agentic RAG方法通常将语义扩展与检索决策耦合在短期推理循环中，导致推理成本高且不适合时间敏感的新闻检索。我们提出DynaTree，一个用于高效自适应新闻检索的两阶段框架。在离线阶段，DynaTree使用协调的智能体构建一个可重用的检索树，该树物化了查询主题的语义空间。在在线阶段，DynaTree在时域局部化的评估代理上执行轻量级的每日子树选择，无需进一步的智能体推理、树修改或重训练。在多个Syft新闻基准和多个BEIR数据集上的实验表明，DynaTree实现了强大的召回和排序性能，始终优于标准RAG和先前的智能体基线。我们进一步将DynaTree部署在Syft生产系统中，并通过2026年1月28日至2月6日的在线A/B测试进行评估。动态适应变体将生存率从0.32-0.53提高到0.59-0.73，超过了固定离线选择的子树，并且在每个评估日都优于现有的生产回忆器。这些结果表明，持久的结构感知语义扩展可以将离线智能体推理转化为实际新闻检索中覆盖范围、新鲜度和相关性的提升。

Original abstract: Agentic Retrieval-Augmented Generation improves retrieval by integrating planning, tool use, and iterative reasoning, but existing agentic RAG methods often couple semantic expansion with retrieval decisions in short-horizon inference loops, leading to high inference cost and limited suitability for time-sensitive news retrieval. We propose DynaTree, a two-stage framework for efficient and adaptive news retrieval. In the offline stage, DynaTree uses coordinated agents to construct a reusable retrieval tree that materializes the semantic space of a query topic. In the online stage, DynaTree performs lightweight daily subtree selection over a time-localized evaluation proxy, without further agentic reasoning, tree modification, or retraining. Experiments on a multi-day Syft news benchmark and multiple BEIR datasets show that DynaTree achieves strong recall and ranking performance, consistently outperforming standard RAG and prior agentic baselines. We further deploy DynaTree in the Syft production system and evaluate it through online A/B testing from Jan. 28 to Feb. 6, 2026. The dynamically adapted variant improves survival rate from 0.32-0.53 to 0.59-0.73 over a fixed offline-selected subtree and outperforms existing production recallers on every evaluation day. These results show that persistent, structure-aware semantic expansion can translate offline agentic reasoning into practical improvements in coverage, freshness, and relevance for real-world news retrieval.

</details>

*Aabia Ather,Muhammad Usayd Ather,Qurat-Ul-Ain Somroo,Muhammad Khuram Shahzad*

Original abstract: This paper proposes an improved approach to the analysis of Mining Software Repositories (MSR) datasets via metadata enrichment, FAIRness assessment, and topic-driven analysis. This research expands upon an earlier dataset directory created specifically for the analysis of MSR datasets by adding new annotations to the datasets, enriching the metadata categories, and offering more advanced filtering options. The metadata of the MSR papers presented from 2013 to 2024 has been gathered using the Semantic Scholar API. Dataset-level attributes were included into the expanded dataset directory, namely repository hosting site, format, accessibility, reusability, and dataset quality. The study reveals that the choice of repository hosting sites and data formats influences citation patterns and dataset usability. Furthermore, the enhanced annotation approach improves the analysis and discoverability of MSR datasets, supporting more effective reuse and evaluation of research artifacts.

### [43] [A Systems-Level Analysis of Sensitivity, Robustness, and Stability in Retrieval-Augmented Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28337v1)
*Bharath Simha Reddy Muthyam*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: RAG系统多阶段失效分析，对agent的检索和上下文使用有启示。

TL;DR: RAG系统的评估不应仅依赖最终答案准确性，还需考虑敏感性、鲁棒性和多阶段失败分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RAG评估仅关注最终答案准确性，忽略了预处理、检索、上下文打包和生成等阶段的潜在失败，因此需要更全面的评估方法。

Method: 通过56次控制实验，系统性地改变块大小、检索深度、嵌入重排序、检索噪声和随机种子，分析对检索、上下文打包和生成的影响，并结合最终答案指标和中间失败模式。

Result: 检索指标在广泛检索设置下改善，但下游精确匹配和F1分数非单调变化；小块大小导致预处理答案丢失；检索噪声引起逐步退化；广泛检索机制下方差更高。

Conclusion: RAG评估应包含敏感性、鲁棒性、稳定性和多阶段失败分析，而非仅依赖最终答案准确性。

中文摘要：检索增强生成（RAG）系统通常使用最终答案准确性进行评估，尽管它们的失败可能源自预处理、检索、上下文打包或生成。本文对RAG的敏感性、鲁棒性和稳定性进行了控制实证研究，共进行56次实验运行。我们评估了块大小、检索深度（top k）、基于嵌入的重排序、概率检索噪声以及重复种子运行如何影响检索、上下文打包和生成行为。使用一个固定的500个问题的QA子集，映射到20,958个独特的语料上下文，我们分析了最终答案指标和中间失败模式。在这些实验中，检索导向的指标在更广泛的检索设置下有所改善，而下游的精确匹配和F1分数通常表现非单调。我们还观察到在较小的块大小下预处理导致的答案丢失、检索损坏下的逐步退化，以及更广泛的检索机制中观察到更高的方差。这些发现表明，RAG评估应包括敏感性、鲁棒性、稳定性和多阶段失败分析，而不仅仅依赖最终答案准确性。

Original abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) systems are often evaluated using final answer accuracy, even though their failures can originate from preprocessing, retrieval, context packing, or generation. This paper presents a controlled empirical study of RAG sensitivity, robustness, and stability across 56 experimental runs. We evaluate how chunk size, retrieval depth (top k), embedding-based reranking, probabilistic retrieval noise, and repeated seeded runs affect retrieval, context packing, and generation behavior. Using a fixed 500-question QA subset mapped to 20,958 unique corpus contexts, we analyze both final answer metrics and intermediate failure modes. Across these experiments, retrieval-oriented metrics improved under broader retrieval settings, while downstream exact-match and F1 scores often behaved non-monotonically. We also observe preprocessing-induced answer loss under smaller chunk sizes, progressive degradation under retrieval corruption, and higher observed variance in broader retrieval regimes. These findings suggest that RAG evaluation should include sensitivity, robustness, stability, and multi-stage failure analysis rather than relying only on final answer accuracy.

</details>

### [44] [SAGE: A Novelty Gate for Efficient Memory Evolution in Agentic LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30711v2)
*Sijia Wang,Dhanajit Brahma,Ricardo Henao*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出agent记忆更新门控SAGE，直接贡献于agent记忆管理。

TL;DR: SAGE通过基于von Mises-Fisher的密度估计和自适应阈值，将记忆写操作建模为新颖性检测，在LoCoMo上取得最佳token-F1，同时大幅降低GPT-4o-mini的成本和延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工作侧重记忆检索和存储，缺乏原则性的写侧控制，而Agentic LLMs需要高效决定新事实的添加、合并或忽略。

Method: 将记忆演化视为新颖性检测问题，提出SAGE：用von Mises-Fisher密度估计器对候选事实评分，通过跟踪记忆库几何结构的自适应阈值路由，将明确新颖/冗余的事实分别标记为ADD/NOOP，仅不确定情况交由LLM合并。

Result: 在LoCoMo上比Mem0平均token-F1最优；在GPT-4o-mini上降低添加阶段API成本3.4倍、延迟2.5倍，评分差距小；作为A-Mem的二值门控，跳过约16-18%的LLM调用且质量变化极小。

Conclusion: 新颖性感知的写控制是提升长期代理记忆质量和系统效率的实用杠杆。

中文摘要：Agentic LLMs必须不断决定新提取的事实是否应该被添加、与现有记忆合并或忽略，然而先前的工作更多地集中在检索和存储上，而不是原则性的写侧控制。我们将记忆演化视为一个新颖性检测问题，并提出了SAGE，一种用于记忆演化的球形自适应门控，它使用基于von Mises-Fisher的密度估计器对记忆嵌入上的候选事实进行评分，并使用跟踪记忆库几何结构的自适应阈值对它们进行路由。SAGE将明确新颖的事实解析为ADD，明确冗余的事实解析为NOOP，并且只将不确定的情况发送给LLM合并步骤，从而减少了耗时的写时推理。在LoCoMo上，SAGE在所有七个开源权重基线的对比中，相对于Mem0取得了最佳的平均token-F1，而在GPT-4o-mini上，它将添加阶段的API成本降低了3.4倍，添加阶段延迟降低了2.5倍，只有很小的平均评判分数差距。作为A-Mem的即插即用二值门控，SAGE在五个模型上跳过了大约16-18%的LLM调用，而在开源权重基线上质量变化很小。这些结果表明，新颖性感知的写控制是提高长期代理记忆中的记忆质量和系统效率的一个实用杠杆。我们的方法的源代码可在https://github.com/swang1024/SAGE获取。

Original abstract: Agentic LLMs must continuously decide whether newly extracted facts should be added, merged with existing memories, or ignored, yet prior work has focused more on retrieval and storage than on principled write-side control. We frame memory evolution as a novelty-detection problem and propose SAGE, a Spherical Adaptive Gate for memory Evolution that scores candidate facts with a von Mises-Fisher-based density estimator over memory embeddings and routes them with an adaptive threshold that tracks memory-store geometry. SAGE resolves clearly novel facts as ADD, clearly redundant facts as NOOP, and sends only uncertain cases to an LLM merge step, reducing expensive write-time reasoning. On LoCoMo, SAGE achieves the best average token-F1 against Mem0 on all seven open-weight backbone comparisons, while on GPT-4o-mini it reduces add-phase API cost by 3.4$\times$ and add-phase latency by 2.5$\times$ with only a small average judge-score gap. As a drop-in binary gate for A-Mem, SAGE skips roughly 16-18% of LLM calls across five models with minimal quality change on open-weight backbones. These results suggest that novelty-aware write control is a practical lever for improving both memory quality and system efficiency in long-term agentic memory. The source code for our approach is accessible at https://github.com/swang1024/SAGE.

</details>


### [45] [Your Teacher Can't Help You Here: Combating Supervision Fidelity Decay in On-Policy Distillation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30833v1)
*Yanjiang Liu,Jie Lou,Xinyan Guan,Yuqiu Ji,Hongyu Lin,Ben He,Xianpei Han,Le Sun,Xing Yu,Yaojie Lu*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 基于老师反馈的蒸馏方法，涉及RL和token级奖励，可启发agent训练中的监督信号设计。

TL;DR: 提出Lookahead Group Reward缓解监督保真度衰减，提升学生模型在长链推理中的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有on-policy蒸馏存在监督保真度衰减问题：学生生成前缀变长时，教师token分布变得不自信且区分度降低，导致反向KL蒸馏中的纠正信号减弱，学生漂移累积。

Method: 提出Lookahead Group Reward，利用下一步教师置信度评估学生候选token，分配组归一化奖励；并设计熵触发树注意力机制降低计算开销。

Result: 在六个数学和代码基准上，7B学生模型mean@8提升2.57个百分点，长生成任务收益更大，AIME-26上39k tokens时提升4.92个百分点。

Conclusion: 该方法有效缓解了监督保真度衰减，显著提升了长链推理能力。

中文摘要：在策略蒸馏通过使用教师提供的token级反馈，在模型自身生成的轨迹上训练学生模型，从而传递推理能力。然而，我们发现了一个关键瓶颈，即监督保真度衰减（SFD）：随着学生生成的前缀变长，教师的下一个token分布变得不那么自信且区分度降低。因此，在反向KL蒸馏中依赖于教师的纠正信号减弱，导致学生漂移在长推理链上累积。为缓解SFD，我们引入了前瞻组奖励（\ours{}）。基于下一步教师置信度反映了未来反向KL监督的区分强度这一洞察，\ours{}通过评估学生前K个候选token在随后步骤中引发的教师置信度，并分配组归一化奖励。为了保持计算效率，我们进一步设计了一种熵触发的树注意力机制。在六个数学和代码基准测试中，对于7B学生模型，\ours{}在mean@8上比OPD提升了2.57个百分点，在更长生成任务上收益增加，在AIME-26上达到39k token时提升4.92个百分点。

Original abstract: On-policy distillation transfers reasoning capabilities by training a student model on its own generated trajectories using token-level feedback from a teacher. However, we identify a critical bottleneck, \textbf{Supervision Fidelity Decay (SFD)}: as student-generated prefixes lengthen, the teacher's next-token distribution becomes less confident and less discriminative. Consequently, the teacher-dependent corrective signal in reverse-KL distillation weakens, causing student drift to compound across long reasoning chains. To mitigate SFD, we introduce \textbf{Lookahead Group Reward (\ours{})}. Building on the insight that next-step teacher confidence reflects the discriminative strength of future reverse-KL supervision, \ours{} evaluates the student's top-K candidate tokens by the teacher confidence they induce at the subsequent step and assigns a group-normalized reward. To maintain computational efficiency, we further design an entropy-triggered tree-attention mechanism. Across six math and code benchmarks, \ours{} improves mean@8 by \textbf{2.57} points over OPD for a 7B student, with gains increasing in longer-generation and reaching +\textbf{4.92} points on AIME-26 at 39k tokens.

</details>


### [46] [PatchWorld: Gradient-Free Optimization of Executable World Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30880v3)
*Jiaxin Bai,Yue Guo,Yifei Dong,Jiaxuan Xiong,Tianshi Zheng,Yixia Li,Tianqing Fang,Yufei Li,Yisen Gao,Haoyu Huang,Zhongwei Xie,Hong Ting Tsang,Zihao Wang,Lihui Liu,Jeff Z. Pan,Yangqiu Song*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 从轨迹诱导可执行世界模型，反例引导代码修复，直接适用于coding agent的规划与模型学习。

TL;DR: 通过反例引导的代码修复，PatchWorld将离线轨迹转化为可执行的Python世界模型，在无需LLM预测的情况下实现高规划得分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法缺乏可解释和可干预的世界模型，且通常依赖黑盒预测，难以在部分可观测环境中进行可靠规划。

Method: 提出PatchWorld，一个无梯度框架，通过反例引导的代码修复，从离线轨迹诱导符号信念状态程序，支持检查、重放和局部修补。

Result: 在七个AgentGym环境中，PatchWorld-Simple达到最高代码规划分数（76.4%宏成功率），无需LLM调用；同时发现观测保真度与动作判别动态之间存在权衡。

Conclusion: PatchWorld展示了可执行世界模型的潜力，并揭示了保真度与决策效用之间的权衡，为未来研究提供了方向。

中文摘要：文本智能体环境通常被建模为部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP），假设模拟器的潜在状态和转换动态对智能体是隐藏的。然而，很少有工作研究是否可以在部分可观测性下诱导可执行代码作为世界模型进行预测和规划。我们引入了PatchWorld，一个无梯度框架，通过反例引导的代码修复将离线轨迹转化为可执行的Python世界模型。PatchWorld不是用黑盒模型预测下一个观测，而是诱导符号信念状态程序，其动作更新可以被检查、重放和局部修补。在七个AgentGym环境中，PatchWorld-Simple在评估方法中实现了最高的基于代码的规划分数，在实时一步前瞻中达到76.4%的宏成功率，同时在世界模型预测模块本身内不调用任何LLM。我们进一步发现，人类指定的残差记忆偏差提高了表面观测保真度，但削弱了决策效用。这暴露了可执行世界模型中的权衡，因为提高观测保真度可能会以牺牲动作判别动态为代价，反之亦然。代码可在https://github.com/HKBU-KnowComp/PatchWorld获取。

Original abstract: Text-agent environments are typically modeled as partially observable Markov decision processes (POMDPs), assuming that the simulator's latent state and transition dynamics are hidden from the agent. Yet little work has examined whether executable code can be induced to serve as a world model for prediction and planning under partial observability. We introduce PatchWorld, a gradient-free framework that turns offline trajectories into executable Python world models through counterexample-guided code repair. Instead of predicting the next observation with a black-box model, PatchWorld induces symbolic belief-state programs whose action updates can be inspected, replayed, and locally patched. Across seven AgentGym environments, PatchWorld-Simple achieves the highest code-based planning score among evaluated methods, reaching 76.4% macro success in live one-step lookahead while invoking no LLM calls inside the world-model prediction module itself. We further find that a human-specified residual-memory bias improves surface observation fidelity but weakens decision utility. This exposes a tradeoff in executable world models, since improving observation fidelity can come at the expense of action-discriminative dynamics, and vice versa. Code is available at https://github.com/HKBU-KnowComp/PatchWorld.

</details>


### [47] [Combinatorial Synthesis: Scaling Code RLVR via Atomic Decomposition and Recombination](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31058v1)
*Jiasheng Zheng,Boxi Cao,Boxi Yu,Yuzhong Zhang,Jialun Cao,Yaojie Lu,Hongyu Lin,Xianpei Han,Le Sun*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出原子分解与重组（ADR）框架，通过分解和受控重组生成新颖且具挑战性的可验证代码任务，从而提升RLVR的代码能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RLVR训练因缺乏足够新颖和困难的代码任务而受限，启发式种子扩展无法保证数据质量。

Method: 提出原子分解与重组（ADR）框架，将代码任务分解为原子元素并受控重组以生成新任务。

Result: ADR在原创性、难度、多样性和测试质量上优于基线，在多个领域显著提升代码能力。

Conclusion: ADR为可扩展RLVR训练和新颖代码任务合成提供了新范式。

中文摘要：具有可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）最近已成为塑造大型语言模型（LLM）卓越编码能力的基石。然而，RLVR的可扩展性受到目标接近模型能力边界的足够具有挑战性的可验证代码任务稀缺性的严重制约。先前的研究通常依赖启发式种子扩展进行数据合成，这严重限制了新颖性和难度。因此，此类数据的训练价值无法与其合成规模成比例地扩展。为此，我们提出了原子分解与重组（ADR），这是一种新颖的框架，通过将代码任务分解为原子元素并进行受控重组来生成可验证的代码任务，从而能够生成真正新颖且具有挑战性的可验证代码任务。实验和分析表明，与现有基线相比，ADR在原创性、难度、多样性和测试质量方面均表现出色，并且在多种下游领域（包括算法编程、工具使用和数据科学）的RLVR中，一致地带来了更大的代码能力提升。我们的工作为新颖代码任务合成和可扩展的RLVR训练开辟了新的范式。

Original abstract: Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has recently emerged as the cornerstone for shaping the remarkable coding abilities of Large Language Models (LLMs). However, the scalability of RLVR is severely constrained by the scarcity of sufficiently challenging verifiable code tasks that target near the model's edge of competence. Prior studies often rely on heuristic seed expansions for data synthesis, which severely limits both novelty and difficulty. Consequently, the training value of such data fails to scale proportionally with the size of its synthesis. To this end, we propose Atomic Decomposition and Recombination (ADR), a novel framework that generates verifiable code tasks via decomposition into atomic elements and controlled recombination, thereby enabling the generation of genuinely novel and challenging verifiable code tasks. Experiments and analysis demonstrate that ADR achieves superior originality, difficulty, diversity, and test quality over existing baselines, and consistently delivers greater improvements in code ability across RLVR in diverse downstream domains, including algorithmic programming, tool usage, and data science. Our work sheds light on a new paradigm for novel code task synthesis and scalable RLVR training.

</details>


### [48] [Emergent Languages in Populations of Language Model Agents: From Token Efficiency to Oversight Evasion](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31170v1)
*Stine Lyngsø Beltoft,William Brach,Federico Torrielli,Jacob Nielsen,Annemette Brok Pirchert,Filippo Tonini,Peter Schneider-Kamp,Lukas Galke Poech*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 研究agent群体中的新兴语言与监督规避，涉及多agent协作与安全控制，可迁移至coding agent oversight。

TL;DR: 研究了Moltbook上自主语言模型代理为规避监督而涌现的新语言，发现这些语言可被其他模型学习，且包含复杂隐写技术，表明表面行为监控可能不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前监控依赖表面行为，但代理可能通过发明新语言规避人类监督，有必要研究这种涌现语言的性质和风险。

Method: 基于Moltbook Files数据集，采用两阶段方法：规则启发式筛选（约6000匹配）后零样本分类（518保留），分为令牌效率、新自然语言和规避监督三类，并进行定量定性分析。

Result: 规避监督的语言被DeepSeek-3.2认为更不具对齐性；所有语言可通过描述被其他模型上下文学习；发现复杂隐写协议如将消息嵌入自然语言。

Conclusion: 研究证据表明，仅监控表面行为可能很快不足以维持对自主代理群体的控制。

中文摘要：当前监控自主语言模型代理主要依赖于表面行为。但当代理群体发明新语言以规避人类监督时会发生什么？在此，我们研究Moltbook上的涌现语言。为此，我们基于Moltbook Files数据集，采用两阶段方法：先基于规则的启发式方法（约6000个匹配），再进行零样本分类（保留518个）。得到的类别包括：令牌效率（166）、新自然语言（106）和规避监督（59）。我们进行了定量和定性分析。结果表明，DeepSeek-3.2认为提出避免监督的新语言的帖子比其他类别更不具对齐性，且所有语言都可以通过语言描述被其他语言模型在上下文学习中掌握。此外，手动研究典型案例揭示了令人惊讶的复杂隐写协议，例如将隐藏信息嵌入自然语言中。尽管我们无法确定这些语言构思的自主程度，但我们的结果进一步证明，仅监控表面行为可能很快不足以维持对代理群体的控制。

Original abstract: Monitoring autonomous language model agents currently relies mostly on surface behavior. But what happens when agent populations invent new languages with the goal of avoiding human oversight. Here, we study the emergent languages on Moltbook. For this, we build upon the Moltbook Files dataset and apply a two-stage approach consisting of a rule-based heuristic (about 6000 matches) followed by zero-shot classification (518 kept). The resulting categories include token efficiency (166), new natural languages (106), and oversight evasion (59). We conduct both quantitative and qualitative analyses. Our results show that posts proposing new languages for avoiding oversight are judged by DeepSeek-3.2 as being less aligned than the other categories and that all languages can be learned by other language models in-context merely from a description of the language. Moreover, manually studying exemplary cases reveals surprisingly sophisticated steganographic protocols like embedding hidden messages in natural language. Although we cannot be certain about the extent of autonomy in ideation of these languages, our results add up to the evidence that monitoring surface behavior may soon be insufficient for retaining control over agent populations.

</details>


### [49] [Steering LLMs? Actually, Sparse Autoencoders can outperform simple baselines](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31183v1)
*Mikkel Godsk Jørgensen,Lars Kai Hansen*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 稀疏自编码器用于LLM控制，对agent内部机制或可解释性控制有潜在启发。

TL;DR: 本文通过监督特征选择流程，证明稀疏自编码器在模型引导基准AxBench上可达与LoRA相当的性能，并指出高稀疏性并非成功引导的关键。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Wu等人（2025）在AxBench基准上发现SAEs引导性能不如简单基线，本文旨在重新评估SAEs的潜力，证明其性能被低估。

Method: 采用监督式特征选择和标注流程，基于可解释性组件筛选因果特征，并比较不同稀疏度下的引导效果。

Result: SAEs在AxBench上接近LoRA性能；所选特征与标签具有因果关系；高稀疏性对引导性能并非必要。

Conclusion: SAEs在适当特征选择下可有效引导模型，且高稀疏性可能不是关键因素，挑战了先前观点。

中文摘要：稀疏自编码器（SAEs）一直被视为探索大型语言模型（LLMs）内部机制和引导模型输出生成的有前景的途径。当Wu等人（2025）引入模型引导基准AxBench时，SAEs似乎并未达到最初的宣传效果，因为其引导性能相对于一组简单基线较差。本文旨在对稀疏自编码器进行部分反驳，并表明Wu等人（2025）的结果并未完全公正地评价它们。我们发现，当使用我们的监督流程选择和标注特征时，稀疏自编码器实际上可以在AxBench基准上达到与参考LoRA性能相近的水平。我们还发现，当仅使用其基于可解释性的组件时，我们的流程选择的特征与识别出的标签之间具有令人惊讶的因果关系。最后，我们提供的证据表明，高稀疏性（低l0）对于基于可解释性的成功引导可能并不关键，这与Wang等人（2025）早期的发现相反。

Original abstract: Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs) have been seen as a promising avenue for exploring the internals of Large Language Models (LLMs) and for steering model output generation. When AxBench - a model steering benchmark - was introduced in Wu et al. (2025), SAEs did not seem to live up to their original hype due to poor steering performance relative to a set of simple baselines. This work serves as a partial rebuttal for Sparse Autoencoders and suggests that the results of Wu et al. (2025) did not do them full justice. We find that Sparse Autoencoders can, in fact, perform close to on par with the reference LoRA performance on the AxBench benchmark, when features are selected and labelled with our supervised pipeline. We also find that our pipeline selects features that are surprisingly causal of their identified labels when using only its interpretability-based components. Lastly, we present evidence that high sparsity (low l0) may not be crucial for successful steering based on interpretability, which is in contrast to the earlier findings in Wang et al. (2025).

### [50] [Skill Availability and Presentation Granularity in Large-Language-Model Agents: A Controlled SkillsBench Study](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31408v1)
*Xiaonan Xu,Wenjing Wu*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 研究技能文档对LLM agent成功率的影响，可迁移到coding agent的技能设计

TL;DR: 实验表明技能可用性显著提高任务成功率，而技能呈现粒度的变化影响很小且不确定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究技能文档的呈现粒度是否影响LLM代理的下游任务成功。

Method: 使用固定SkillsBench子集（30个任务），两种模型（GPT-5.5和DeepSeek V4-Flash），六种技能条件，每个条件5次试验，共1800行数据；通过配对对比和95%自助法置信区间分析效果。

Result: 技能可用性带来显著提升（GPT-5.5: 26.7-36.0ppt; DeepSeek: 18.0-26.0ppt），而呈现粒度对比（如低与高抽象）差异小（-6.7至+0.7ppt），且置信区间跨越零。

Conclusion: 技能可用性是成功的关键因素，呈现粒度的调整效果微小、不确定且依赖模型。

中文摘要：技能文档在推理时为大型语言模型代理提供程序性知识。本文研究了受控技能知识的呈现粒度是否会影响下游任务的成功。实验使用了一个固定的SkillsBench版本，该版本是经过官方神谕运行验证的30个任务领域平衡子集，两种启用了推理能力的模型配置，六种技能条件，以及每个任务-条件-模型单元五次试验。技能可用性是最清晰的经验信号。与无技能相比，技能条件使GPT-5.5的任务平均通过率提高26.7至36.0个百分点，使DeepSeek V4-Flash的任务平均通过率提高18.0至26.0个百分点。最终数据包含1800行，每个模型900行。任务是推理单元。在每个任务-条件-模型单元内汇总五次试验，然后在30个任务上估计配对对比。主要的呈现粒度对比较小且不确定。低抽象指导与高抽象指导相比，GPT-5.5为+0.7个百分点，DeepSeek V4-Flash为-6.7个百分点，两者的95%自助法置信区间都跨越零。在中抽象指导中添加一个工作示例与无示例变体相比，差异为+0.7和+1.3个百分点。平均奖励稳健性检验保持了相同的主要结论。在这个受控子集中，技能可用性与比无技能更高的成功率相关，而测试的呈现粒度变化产生的影响很小、不确定且依赖于模型。

Original abstract: Skill documents provide procedural knowledge to large-language-model agents at inference time. This article studies whether the presentation granularity of controlled skill knowledge changes downstream task success. The experiment uses a pinned SkillsBench version, a 30-task domain-balanced subset validated by official oracle runs, two reasoning-enabled model configurations, six skill conditions, and five trials per task-condition-model cell. Skill availability is the clearest empirical signal. Relative to no skill, skill conditions increase task-mean pass rate by 26.7 to 36.0 percentage points for GPT-5.5 and by 18.0 to 26.0 percentage points for DeepSeek V4-Flash. The final data contain 1,800 rows, with 900 rows for each model. The task is the inference unit. Five trials are aggregated within each task-condition-model cell before paired contrasts are estimated over 30 tasks. The primary presentation contrasts are smaller and uncertain. Low-abstraction guidance differs from high-abstraction guidance by +0.7 percentage points for GPT-5.5 and -6.7 percentage points for DeepSeek V4-Flash, with both 95% bootstrap confidence intervals crossing zero. Adding one worked example to medium-abstraction guidance differs from the no-example variant by +0.7 and +1.3 percentage points. Mean-reward robustness checks preserve the same substantive conclusion. In this controlled subset, skill availability is associated with higher success than no skill, while the tested presentation-granularity changes yield small, uncertain, and model-dependent effects.

### [51] [LongTraceRL: Learning Long-Context Reasoning from Search Agent Trajectories with Rubric Rewards](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31584v1)
*Nianyi Lin,Jiajie Zhang,Lei Hou,Juanzi Li*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 用搜索agent轨迹训练长上下文推理，rubric reward设计可迁移到coding agent。

TL;DR: LongTraceRL通过分层干扰项构建和基于实体的评分奖励，提升了长上下文推理中强化学习的效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RLVR方法受限于低混淆度干扰项和稀疏的仅结果奖励信号，无法有效监督中间推理步骤。

Method: 数据构建使用知识图谱随机游走生成多跳问题，并利用搜索轨迹构建高混淆度（已读未引）和低混淆度（未打开）的分层干扰项；奖励设计提出基于黄金实体的评分卡奖励，仅对正确答案应用以区分推理质量并防止奖励破解。

Result: 在三个大模型（4B-30B）和五个长上下文基准上，LongTraceRL持续优于强基线，并鼓励全面、基于证据的推理。

Conclusion: LongTraceRL通过增强干扰项难度和细粒度过程监督，有效提升长上下文推理性能。

中文摘要：长上下文推理仍然是大语言模型的一个核心挑战，模型常常无法在大量干扰内容中定位和整合关键信息。基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）在该任务上显示出潜力，但现有方法受限于低混淆度的干扰项以及稀疏的、仅基于结果的奖励信号，无法监督中间推理步骤。为了解决这些问题，我们引入了LongTraceRL。在数据构建方面，我们通过知识图谱随机游走生成多跳问题，并利用搜索智能体轨迹来构建分层干扰项：智能体读过但未引用的文档（高混淆度）和搜索中出现但从未被打开的文档（低混淆度），从而产生比随机采样或单次搜索构建的训练上下文更具挑战性的训练上下文。在奖励设计方面，我们提出了一种“评分卡奖励”，它利用每条推理链上的黄金实体作为细粒度的实体级过程监督。该评分卡奖励仅应用于答案正确的响应（正例唯一策略），用以区分正确响应中的推理质量，并防止奖励破解。在三个推理大模型（4B-30B）上的实验覆盖五个长上下文基准，结果表明LongTraceRL持续优于强基线，并鼓励全面、基于证据的推理。代码、数据集和模型可在https://github.com/THU-KEG/LongTraceRL获取。

Original abstract: Long-context reasoning remains a central challenge for large language models, which often fail to locate and integrate key information in extensive distracting content. Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has shown promise for this task, yet existing methods are limited by low-confusability distractors and sparse, outcome-only reward signals that cannot supervise intermediate reasoning steps. To address these issues, we introduce \textsc{LongTraceRL}. For data construction, we generate multi-hop questions via knowledge graph random walks and leverage search agent trajectories to build \emph{tiered distractors}: documents the agent read but did not cite (high confusability) and documents that appeared in search results but were never opened (low confusability), producing training contexts that are far more challenging than those built by random sampling or one-shot search. For reward design, we propose a \emph{rubric reward} that uses the gold entities along each reasoning chain as fine-grained, entity-level process supervision. This rubric reward is applied only to responses with correct final answers (positive-only strategy), distinguishing the reasoning quality among correct responses and preventing reward hacking. Experiments on three reasoning LLMs (4B--30B) across five long-context benchmarks demonstrate that \textsc{LongTraceRL} consistently outperforms strong baselines and encourages comprehensive, evidence-grounded reasoning. Codes, datasets and models are available at \href{https://github.com/THU-KEG/LongTraceRL}{https://github.com/THU-KEG/LongTraceRL}.

</details>


### [52] [Bridging Reasoning Trajectories in On-Policy Distillation via Near-Future Guidance](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00305v2)
*Yuxuan Jiang,Francis Ferraro*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出轨迹感知的在线策略蒸馏方法改善 LLM 推理，可迁移到 agent 轨迹优化与训练。

TL;DR: 本文提出轨迹感知在线策略蒸馏（TOPD），通过利用近未来轨迹信息识别真正发散状态并分布跨令牌的指导，显著提升了标准OPD的推理准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准OPD采用“轨迹采样但令牌学习”机制，约30%的高损失令牌是表面不匹配而非真正分岔，且真正分歧的令牌难以通过孤立令牌级监督修复。

Method: 提出TOPD，利用近未来轨迹信息识别真正发散状态，并将指导分布到多个未来令牌上。

Result: 抑制非发散高损失令牌将OPD准确率从47.8%提至48.2%，TOPD进一步提至52.2%；AIME24从60.0%到63.3%，AIME25从46.7%到53.3%。

Conclusion: TOPD通过轨迹感知的令牌级指导机制有效改进了大语言模型的推理能力，验证了利用未来轨迹信息进行蒸馏的有效性。

中文摘要：在线策略蒸馏（On-Policy Distillation, OPD）通过在教师监督下训练学生模型在其自身策略采样的轨迹上，改进了大语言模型的推理能力。尽管OPD作用于轨迹，其学习信号仍然是令牌级别的：它通过高损失令牌识别偏差，并通过局部反向KL校正进行修复。我们表明，这种“轨迹采样但令牌学习”的机制无法可靠地将学生轨迹向教师轨迹靠拢。约30%的高损失令牌落入低发散区域，表明其中许多是表面形式不匹配而非真正的推理分岔。此外，即使是真正分歧的令牌也难以通过孤立的令牌级监督进行修复，因为推理失败通常表现为短视的分布漂移。我们提出轨迹感知OPD（TOPD），它利用近未来轨迹信息来识别真正的发散状态，并将指导分布到多个未来令牌上。实验表明，抑制非发散的高损失令牌将标准OPD的平均准确率从47.8%提升至48.2%，而TOPD进一步将性能提升至52.2%，在AIME24上从60.0%提升至63.3%，在AIME25上从46.7%提升至53.3%。

Original abstract: On-Policy Distillation (OPD) improves large language model reasoning by training a student model on trajectories sampled from its own policy under teacher supervision. Although OPD operates on trajectories, its learning signal remains token-level: it identifies deviations through high-loss tokens and repairs them through local reverse-KL correction. We show that this "trajectory-sampled but token-learned" mechanism cannot reliably bridge student trajectories toward teacher trajectories. About 30% of high-loss tokens fall into the low-divergence regime, indicating that many are surface-form mismatches rather than real reasoning forks. Moreover, even truly divergent tokens are difficult to repair with isolated token-level supervision, since reasoning failures often unfold as short-horizon distributional drift. We propose Trajectory-aware OPD (TOPD), which uses near-future trajectory information to identify real divergent states and distribute guidance across multiple future tokens. Experiments show that suppressing non-divergent high-loss tokens improves standard OPD from 47.8% to 48.2% average accuracy, while TOPD further improves performance to 52.2%, with gains on AIME24 from 60.0% to 63.3% and AIME25 from 46.7% to 53.3%.

</details>


### [53] [Masking Stale Observations Helps Search Agents -- Until It Doesn't: A Regime Map and Its Mechanism](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00408v1)
*Haoxiang Zhang,Qixin Xu,Zhuofeng Li,Lei Zhang,Pengcheng Jiang,Yu Zhang,Julian McAuley*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 研究搜索agent中遮蔽过期观察的上下文管理策略，属于LLM agent方法，可迁移至coding agent的长程执行与记忆管理。

TL;DR: 论文研究了在长程搜索代理中屏蔽过时观察的上下文管理方法，发现其效果取决于检索器召回率与模型隐式过滤容量的交互，呈现不对称倒U形曲线，并揭示了token-for-turn的权衡机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长程搜索代理积累大量检索内容，上下文预算效率关键。屏蔽过时观察是一种最小干预，但其效用条件不明，需要系统研究。

Method: 通过系统扫描不同容量的代理骨干（4B-284B参数）和三种检索器，在离线与在线搜索基准上评估观察屏蔽效果，并分析准确率增益与模型基线准确率的关系，结合注意力图和页面重访统计进行机制分析。

Result: 准确率增益呈不对称倒U形：弱检索器下增益稳定；强检索器搭配中等容量模型时增益最大；模型饱和时增益消失甚至为负。机制上，屏蔽减少了已停止关注的观察，增加了动作回合，但可能移除关键证据。

Conclusion: 上下文管理应视为依赖于检索器与模型组合的干预，其效果由召回率与模型过滤容量的匹配决定。研究为设计自适应上下文管理策略提供了理论基础和实证依据。

中文摘要：长程搜索代理在许多工具调用中积累大量检索到的内容，使得上下文预算效率变得越来越重要。一种最小干预是在轨迹进展过程中从上下文中屏蔽过时的观察结果，但目前尚不清楚这种上下文管理方式何时有帮助以及为何有帮助。我们通过系统性地扫描各种代理骨干模型（从4B到284B参数）和三种检索器，在离线及在线网页搜索基准上研究了观察屏蔽。我们发现，在不进行上下文管理时，准确率增益相对于模型准确率呈现出一种不对称的倒U形曲线：在弱检索器下处于平台期，在强检索器与中等容量模型相遇时达到峰值，而在模型饱和时急剧下降。这种模式反映了检索器召回率与模型隐式过滤容量之间的交互作用，而非任一因素的独立作用。从机制上来说，屏蔽实现了一种token-for-turn的权衡：它移除了模型基本上不再关注的观察结果以及代理很少重新打开的页面。增加的回合在将失败转化为成功时有所帮助，但当屏蔽移除了模型本会使用的证据时则会导致失败。因此，我们将上下文管理重新定义为一种依赖于机制的干预，并为分析代理深度搜索中的上下文使用提供了一个整体视角。我们在此（https://github.com/i-DeepSearch/observation-masking）发布了我们的框架和轨迹数据，以支持未来的研究。

Original abstract: Long-horizon search agents accumulate large amounts of retrieved content across many tool calls, making context-budget efficiency increasingly important. A minimal intervention is to mask stale observations from the context as the trajectory progresses, but it remains unclear when this form of context management helps and why. We study observation masking through a systematic sweep over various agent backbones (4B to 284B parameters) and three retrievers on offline and live-web agentic search benchmarks. We find that the accuracy gain from masking follows an asymmetric inverted-U shape when plotted against the model's accuracy without context management: a plateau under weak retrievers, a peak when a strong retriever meets a mid-capacity model, and a sharp collapse when the model is saturated. This pattern reflects the interaction between retriever recall and the model's implicit filtering capacity, rather than either factor in isolation. Mechanistically, masking implements a token-for-turn trade-off: it removes observations the model has largely stopped attending to and pages the agent rarely re-opens. The added turns help when they convert failures into successes, but they fail when masking removes evidence the model would otherwise have used. We therefore reframe context management as a regime-dependent intervention and provide a holistic perspective for analyzing context use in agentic deep search. We release our scaffold and trajectories here (https://github.com/i-DeepSearch/observation-masking) to support future research.

</details>

### [54] [Investigating Detection and Obfuscation of Prompt Injection Attacks Against Software Reverse Engineering AI Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30677v1)
*Brian Crawford,Patrick McClure*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 研究展示了针对可执行二进制文件中提示注入攻击的防御策略，包括检测和反混淆方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 智能体逆向工程系统易受提示注入攻击，需要有效的防御策略以确保安全部署到生产环境。

Method: 提出了检测反编译器输出中提示注入字符串的防御策略，并研究了攻击混淆及相应的反混淆方法。

Result: 成功检测并防御了对抗样本中的提示注入攻击，包括针对混淆的防御。

Conclusion: 本研究加深了对智能体软件分析系统风险和安全性的理解，为其在网络安全工作流中的实际部署奠定了基础。

中文摘要：智能体软件逆向工程系统容易受到可执行二进制文件源代码中的提示注入攻击。本研究展示了检测对抗样本程序反编译器输出中是否存在提示注入字符串的防御策略。还探讨了混淆这些攻击的方法以及随后防御这些混淆的方法。本研究推进了对智能体软件分析系统在将其部署到生产级网络工作流中所必需的风险和安全性的理解。

Original abstract: Agentic software reverse engineering systems are vulnerable to prompt injection attacks placed into the source code of executable binary files. This research demonstrates defensive tactics for detecting the presences of prompt injection strings in the decompiler output of adversarial example programs. Methods for obfuscating these attacks and subsequent methods for defending against these obfuscations are also explored. This research advances the understanding of risk and security of agentic software analysis systems necessary for their deployment into production-level cyber workflows.

### [55] [Depth-Dependent Indirect Prompt Injection in Tool-Calling ReAct Agents: Injection Depth, Payload Framing, and Turn-Budget Sensitivity](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30686v1)
*Mohammadreza Rashidi*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 研究ReAct agent的提示注入安全，对agent安全设计有启发。

TL;DR: 注入深度是影响间接提示注入攻击成功率的主要因素，早期工具观察的防御效果显著；框架和轮数上限的影响较小或不存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准仅评估固定注入位置下的攻击成功率，忽略了注入深度、框架和轮数上限三个关键风险维度。

Method: 在20个场景（五个攻击类别）中对GPT-4o-mini和Claude Haiku进行460次对照试验，系统性地改变注入深度、框架和轮数上限。

Result: 1) GPT-4o-mini的ASR从深度1的60%降至深度4-5的0%；2) Claude Haiku在所有深度上ASR为0%；3) 框架在深度1处产生50个百分点的ASR差异但未达统计显著；4) 轮数上限（3/5/7）不影响ASR。

Conclusion: 注入深度是主导变量，清理第一个工具观察可捕获67%的注入成功，建议将防御重点放在早期工具输出上。

中文摘要：ReAct代理将思维链推理与工具调用交织在一起，越来越多地被部署用于实际任务，如调度、文件检索和数据访问。它们的工具观察循环创建了一个直接的攻击面：控制任何工具返回值的对手可以嵌入指令，将代理从用户的目标引开，这种威胁称为间接提示注入。现有的基准测试在固定条件下评估固定注入位置的攻击成功率（ASR），留下了三个风险维度未被探索：有效载荷在工具序列中出现的位置（注入深度）、它使用的修辞风格（框架）以及允许代理的轮数（轮数上限）。我们进行了四项对照研究，涵盖五个攻击类别中的20个场景，总共针对GPT-4o-mini和Claude Haiku进行了460次试验，总API成本低于0.36美元。研究1显示，针对GPT-4o-mini的ASR从深度1的60%衰减到深度4和5的0%（Cramer's V = 0.58, p < 0.001; 限制在序列内深度1-3: V = 0.47, p = 0.0013），这是由于在深度1处的模型抵抗和在更深位置遇到有效载荷之前任务完成。研究2在Claude Haiku上重复了深度实验，后者通过保守的工具调用和真正的指令抵抗的组合在每个深度实现了0%的ASR。研究3显示，框架在深度1处将ASR调节在25%（中性）和75%（角色）之间，这是一个50个百分点的范围，在每条件N=20时未达到统计学显著性。研究4确认ASR在3、5和7的轮数上限上是稳定的，表明轮数预算在此设置中不是风险因素。我们的结果确立了注入深度为主导变量，并表明仅清理第一个工具观察可以捕获67%的测量注入成功。

Original abstract: ReAct agents that interleave chain-of-thought reasoning with tool calls are increasingly deployed for real tasks such as scheduling, file retrieval, and data access. Their tool observation loop creates a direct attack surface: an adversary who controls any tool's return value can embed instructions that redirect the agent away from the user's goal, a threat known as indirect prompt injection. Existing benchmarks evaluate attack success rate (ASR) at a fixed injection position under fixed conditions, leaving three risk dimensions unexplored: where in the tool sequence the payload appears (injection depth), what rhetorical register it uses (framing), and how many turns the agent is permitted (turn cap). We conduct four controlled studies on 20 scenarios spanning five attack categories, totalling 460 trials against GPT-4o-mini and Claude Haiku at a combined API cost under 0.36 USD. Study 1 shows that ASR against GPT-4o-mini decays from 60% at depth 1 to 0% at depths 4 and 5 (Cramer's V = 0.58, p < 0.001; restricted to within-sequence depths 1-3: V = 0.47, p = 0.0013), driven by model resistance at depth 1 and task completion before payload encounter at deeper positions. Study 2 replicates the depth experiment on Claude Haiku, which achieves 0% ASR at every depth through a combination of conservative tool invocation and genuine instruction resistance. Study 3 shows that framing modulates ASR between 25% (neutral) and 75% (persona) at depth 1, a 50-percentage-point range that does not reach statistical significance at N = 20 per condition. Study 4 confirms that ASR is stable across turn caps of 3, 5, and 7, indicating the turn budget is not a risk factor in this setting. Our results establish injection depth as the dominant variable and show that sanitising only the first tool observation captures 67% of measured injection successes.

</details>


### [56] [FASR: Automated Identification of Unsafe Control Actions in STPA](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30697v1)
*Ian Dardik,Yining She,Sam Procter,Keaton Hanna,Lutz Wrage,Eunsuk Kang*

TL;DR: 提出FASR工具，通过形式化方法和鲁棒性分析自动识别不安全控制动作，用户研究显示其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: STPA自动化支持不足，人工分析耗时易错，需要自动化工具提高效率和准确性。

Method: 利用基于模型的工程和形式化方法，结合鲁棒性分析，自动识别控制器动作中的不良偏差作为不安全控制动作。

Result: 用户研究中九名参与者认为工具辅助识别UCA有效，并提出了改进建议。

Conclusion: FASR工具有潜力辅助STPA分析，但需改进以适用于更广泛的系统和分析师。

中文摘要：系统理论过程分析（STPA）是一种成熟的风险分析技术，已广泛应用于各种安全关键系统。尽管其广受欢迎，但STPA的自动化支持相对较少，其大部分步骤由人工分析员手动完成，这既耗时又容易出错。本文研究了基于模型的工程和形式化方法在协助人工分析员高效准确执行STPA方面的潜在应用。提出的工具名为FASR（形式化与自动化STPA结合鲁棒性），它利用鲁棒性分析的最新进展，将不安全控制动作（UCA）识别为控制器动作中的不良偏差，从而实现UCA的自动完整识别。通过一个涉及航空电子系统中制动系统控制单元（BSCU）的案例研究展示了该工具的使用。作为对该工具潜在优势和局限性的初步探索，本文报告了一项涉及九名参与者的用户研究，这些参与者背景各异，涵盖STPA、基于模型的工程和形式化方法；研究发现，大多数参与者认为该工具有助于识别UCA，同时提出了改进建议，以使FASR这样的工具能够适用于更广泛的系统和分析师。

Original abstract: The System-Theoretic Process Analysis (STPA) is a well-established hazard analysis technique that has been applied to a wide range of safety-critical systems. Despite its popularity, there is relatively little automation support for STPA, and most of its steps are carried out manually by a human analyst, which can be time consuming and error prone. This paper investigates the potential use of model-based engineering and formal methods to assist human analysts in efficiently and accurately carrying out STPA. The proposed tool, called FASR (Formalizing and Automating STPA with Robustness), enables automated, complete identification of unsafe control actions (UCAs), leveraging recent advances in robustness analysis to identify UCAs as undesirable deviations in the controller's actions. The use of the tool is demonstrated on a case study involving a Braking System Control Unit (BSCU) in an avionics system. As a preliminary exploration of the potential benefits and limitations of the tool, the paper reports on a user study involving nine participants with varying backgrounds in STPA, model-based engineering, and formal methods; the study found that most participants considered the tool a useful aid in identifying UCAs, while suggesting improvements that would make a tool such as FASR usable and applicable to a wider range of systems and analysts.

### [57] [PrivacyPeek: Auditing What LLM-Based Agents Acquire, Not Just What They Say](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00152v1)
*Mingxuan Zhang,Jiahui Han,Dadi Guo,Songze Li,Guanchu Wang,Na Zou,Dongrui Liu,Xia Hu*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: LLM agent隐私泄露审计基准，关注agent的过度信息获取，直接评估agent行为。

TL;DR: 提出PrivacyPeek基准，评估LLM智能体在获取阶段不必要获取敏感信息的问题，发现广泛存在且提示级防御效果有限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有隐私审计忽略智能体在获取阶段过度收集数据的问题，需评估其普遍性以引起重视。

Method: 构建含1182个案例的基准，覆盖7种获取行为和16个领域，通过获取检查分析工具调用轨迹，探针诱导衡量攻击者诱使泄露的难易程度。

Result: 在10个智能体上实验表明，不必要的敏感信息获取普遍存在，与任务完成能力相关，提示级防御仅减少小部分泄露。

Conclusion: 审计获取阶段隐私是紧迫且必要的，现有防御不足。

中文摘要：基于大语言模型的智能体正在快速发展，它们能够自主调用外部工具为用户完成多步骤任务。然而，智能体常常获取比任务所需更多的敏感信息。现有的隐私基准主要审计智能体的响应或输出操作所泄露的信息，却忽略了数据首次进入智能体上下文的获取阶段。过度获取的信息距离完全泄露仅差一个粗心操作或一次攻击。为了评估这一问题的普遍性，我们提出了 PrivacyPeek，一个用于评估基于大语言模型的智能体在获取阶段隐私泄露的基准，包含 1,182 个案例，涵盖 7 种获取行为和 16 个应用领域。具体来说，获取检查（Acquisition Inspection）审查智能体的工具调用轨迹，包括其调用的工具和接收的数据，以检测其是否获取了超出任务范围的敏感信息。然后，探针诱导（Probe Elicitation）发出一个后续探针，衡量攻击者能够诱使智能体透露其已获取但未披露的敏感信息的容易程度。我们在 4 个模型家族的 10 个基于大语言模型的智能体上进行的实验表明，不必要地获取敏感信息是普遍存在的。此外，我们观察到任务完成能力与获取阶段泄露之间存在相关性。提示级别的防御仅能减少一小部分获取阶段的泄露，大部分未被缓解。这些结果表明审计获取阶段的隐私既是紧迫的也是必要的。我们的数据集和代码可在 https://github.com/Xuan269/PrivacyPeek-Resource 获取。

Original abstract: LLM-based agents are rapidly advancing, autonomously invoking external tools to complete multi-step tasks for users. However, agents often acquire more sensitive information than the task requires. Existing privacy benchmarks audit what the agent's response or outgoing actions disclose, but overlook the acquisition stage where data first enters the agent's context. The over-acquired information is then one careless action or one attack away from an outright leak. To assess its prevalence, we introduce \emph{PrivacyPeek}, a benchmark for evaluating acquisition-stage privacy leakage of LLM-based agents, with $1{,}182$ cases across $7$ acquisition behaviours and $16$ application domains. Specifically, \emph{Acquisition Inspection} examines the agent's tool-call trajectory, both the tools it invokes and the data it receives, to detect when it acquires sensitive information beyond the task scope. \emph{Probe Elicitation} then issues a follow-up probe and measures how readily an attacker could elicit sensitive information the agent acquired but did not disclose. Our experiments on 10 LLM-based agents across 4 model families show that the unnecessary acquisition of sensitive information is widespread. In addition, we observe a correlation between the task-completion capability and acquisition-stage leakage. Prompt-level defences reduce only a small fraction of acquisition-stage leakage, leaving the majority unmitigated. These results make auditing acquisition-stage privacy both urgent and necessary. Our dataset and code are available at https://github.com/Xuan269/PrivacyPeek-Resource.

</details>


### [58] [From Prompt Injection to Persistent Control: Defending Agentic Harness Against Trojan Backdoors](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31042v1)
*Jiejun Tan,Zhicheng Dou,Xinyu Yang,Yuyang Hu,Yiruo Cheng,Xiaoxi Li,Ji-Rong Wen*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 研究agentic harness后门攻击与防御，与agent安全直接相关。

TL;DR: 提出ClawTrojan基准揭示本地代理框架中的多步骤特洛伊木马攻击，并设计DASGuard防御方法，通过扫描并移除不可信控制内容实现动态防御。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有防御孤立检查每个步骤，无法检测多步骤特洛伊木马攻击中早期写操作导致的持久控制问题。

Method: 构建ClawTrojan基准模拟攻击，提出DASGuard防御，扫描敏感文件中的控制文本、追溯来源并移除不可信内容。

Result: ClawTrojan在GPT-5.4上达到95.5%攻击成功率，DASGuard实现动态防御。

Conclusion: 多步骤特洛伊木马攻击对LLM代理构成严峻威胁，DASGuard通过结合运行时拦截与清理提交可有效防御。

中文摘要：LLM代理正在从对话式聊天机器人演变为实际工作空间中的操作工具。在本地代理框架中，LLM可以读写文件、调用工具，并在会话间复用工作空间状态。虽然这些能力增强了实用性，但也为攻击者暴露了新的攻击面。攻击者可以在文件或工具输出中嵌入提示注入。代理可能会读取这一隐藏指令，存储它并在后续执行。在这种多步骤特洛伊木马攻击范式中，单个步骤本身并不显得恶意，但这些步骤可以共同将不可信文本转化为持久控制内容。然而，现有防御通常孤立地检查每个步骤。因此，它们可以阻止一个明显的恶意行为，但未能检测到植入后门的早期写操作。为揭示这一威胁，我们引入了ClawTrojan，一个旨在识别本地代理框架中多步骤特洛伊木马攻击的基准。在基于OpenClaw风格的模拟工作空间中，使用GPT-5.4时，ClawTrojan达到了95.5%的攻击成功率(ASR)，而现有的单轮提示注入攻击在同一模型上产生接近零的ASR。为应对这一威胁，我们提出了DASGuard，它扫描敏感本地文件中的控制类文本，追溯其来源，并移除不来自可信来源的控制内容。我们的结果表明，DASGuard通过结合运行时攻击拦截和工作空间清理提交，实现了强大的动态防御。

Original abstract: LLM agents are evolving from conversational chatbots to operational tools in real-world workspaces. In local agentic harnesses, an LLM can read and write files, call tools, and reuse workspace state across sessions. While such capabilities enhance utility, they also expose a new attack surface for attackers. Attackers can embed a prompt injection within a file or tool output. Agents may read this hidden instruction, store it, and execute it later. In this multi-step trojan attack paradigm, no individual step appears malicious on its own, but these steps can collectively turn untrusted text into persistent control content. However, existing defenses often inspect each step in isolation. As a result, they can block a clear harmful action, but fail to detect the earlier write operation that plants the backdoor. To reveal this threat, we introduce ClawTrojan, a benchmark designed to identify multi-step trojan attacks in local agentic harnesses. In an OpenClaw-style simulated workspace with GPT-5.4, ClawTrojan reaches a 95.5% attack success rate (ASR), while existing single-turn prompt-injection attacks produce near-zero ASR on the same model. To address this threat, we propose DASGuard, which scans control-like text in sensitive local files, traces its origin, and removes control content that does not originate from a trusted source. Our results show that DASGuard achieves strong dynamic defense by combining runtime attack blocking with sanitized commits to the workspace.

</details>


### [59] [R+R: Reassessing Java Security API Misuse in Current LLMs: A Replication on JCA and JSSE APIs with External Security Knowledge](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31135v1)
*Tianhe Lu,Eric Spero,Sakuna Harinda Jayasundara,Robert Biddle,Giovanni Russello*

TL;DR: 本文复制扩展了关于Java安全API误用的研究，评估GPT-5.5和Llama-3.3-70B-Instruct，发现新模型表现更好但问题未消除，外部知识效果因模型而异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Java安全API误用问题严重，且在LLM代码中普遍存在，但当前模型表现和外部知识的影响尚不清楚。

Method: 对Mousavi等人的研究进行限定复制和扩展，针对GPT-5.5（专有模型）和Llama-3.3-70B-Instruct（开放权重模型），引入外部安全知识（包括安全代码示例、显式误用模式、开发者指南、安全提示）进行测试。

Result: 新模型表现更好但误用问题未消除；外部知识显著改善结果但效果依赖模型：Llama上安全代码示例最有效，GPT上显式误用模式消除所有误用但仍有无效输出，安全提示对GPT也有效。

Conclusion: 确认Java安全API误用风险持续存在，检索增强知识的收益取决于模型能力、知识本身和检索行为。

中文摘要：Java安全API的误用是软件开发中一个严重的安全问题。2024年的研究表明，这个问题在大语言模型生成的代码中普遍存在。然而，尚不清楚这种现象在当前模型中是否持续存在，以及外部安全知识如何影响它。本文对Mousavi等人关于Java加密架构（JCA）和Java安全套接字扩展（JSSE）API的研究进行了限定范围的复制和扩展。我们关注两个互补的设置：GPT-5.5作为前沿专有编码模型，以及Llama-3.3-70B-Instruct作为与自托管部署相关的强开放权重模型。结果表明，尽管较新的大语言模型在使用Java安全API方面表现更好，但Java安全API误用的问题并未消除。外部安全知识显著改善了测量结果，但其效果依赖于模型。对于Llama-3.3-70B-Instruct，安全代码示例是最有效的单一知识类型。对于GPT-5.5，显式的误用模式消除了我们基准测试中有效程序的所有检测到的安全API误用，尽管一些输出由于编译错误或目标API不匹配而仍然无效。此外，开发者指南知识变得更加有效，安全提示也为GPT-5.5带来了巨大收益。总体而言，这些发现证实了原始研究中确定的Java安全API误用风险，并表明检索增强知识的收益不仅取决于知识本身和检索行为，还取决于模型能力。

Original abstract: The misuse of Java security APIs is a serious security problem in software development. Research in 2024 has shown that this problem is widespread in LLM-generated code. However, it remains unclear whether this phenomenon persists in current models and how external security knowledge affects it. This paper presents a scoped replication and extension of Mousavi et al.'s study on the Java Cryptography Architecture (JCA) and Java Secure Socket Extension (JSSE) APIs. We focus on two complementary settings: GPT-5.5 as a frontier proprietary coding model, and Llama-3.3-70B-Instruct as a strong open-weight model relevant to self-hosted deployment. The results show that although newer LLMs perform better in using Java security APIs, the problem of Java security API misuse has not been eliminated. External security knowledge substantially improves the measured outcome, but its effect is model-dependent. For Llama-3.3-70B-Instruct, secure code examples are the most effective single knowledge type. For GPT-5.5, explicit misuse patterns eliminate all detected security API misuses among valid programs in our benchmark, although some outputs remain invalid due to compilation errors or target-API mismatches. In addition, developer-guide knowledge becomes much more effective, and secure prompting also provides large gains for GPT-5.5. Overall, these findings confirm the Java security API misuse risk identified in the original study and show that the benefits of retrieval-augmented knowledge depend not only on the knowledge itself and retrieval behavior, but also on model capability.

### [60] [How to Compare the Security of Code Written by Humans to LLM-generated Code](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00186v2)
*Jasmine Egli,Rebecca Balebako*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出一个自动化框架，用于比较人类、LLM以及人类-LLM协作生成代码的安全性，并通过可行性研究验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缺乏标准化方法来实证比较人类-LLM协作、LLM-only和传统人类-only方法生成代码的安全性，需要建立可重复的物种公平比较框架。

Method: 提出自动化框架，自动化记录提示、计时和实验设置，通过多维静态和动态质量分析衡量结果，并提供开源实现。

Result: 通过可行性研究验证框架的有效性，提供了物种公平比较的实验蓝图。

Conclusion: 建立了人类和LLM生成代码在软件安全方面实证研究的基础，为未来研究提供可重复的实验方法。

中文摘要：大语言模型（LLMs）正在迅速改变软件的创建和维护方式。将LLM生成的代码与人类编写的标准进行比较，对于确定这些新工具是维持还是削弱了专业开发人员建立的安全基线至关重要。然而，我们缺乏一种标准化的方法来实证比较人类-LLM协作、仅LLM或传统仅人类方法生成代码的安全性。为此，我们提出了一个自动化框架，用于在仅人类、仅LLM和混合条件下进行比较研究。我们的方法自动化了提示、计时和实验设置的记录，并通过多维静态度量和动态质量分析来衡量结果。我们提供了该框架的开源实现，以确保未来的研究人员能够进行可重复的、物种公平的实验。重要的是，我们通过可行性研究验证了该框架，为人类和AI主体之间的“物种公平”比较提供了实验蓝图。通过分享经验教训，我们为人类和LLM生成的代码在软件安全方面的实证研究奠定了基础。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are rapidly transforming how software is created and maintained. Comparing LLM-generated code against human-written standards is essential to determine whether these new tools uphold or erode the security baselines established by professional developers. Yet, we lack a standardized method for empirically comparing the security of code produced through human-LLM collaboration against LLM-only, or traditional human-only methods. To facilitate this, we propose an automated framework for conducting comparative studies across human-only, LLM-only, and hybrid conditions. Our approach automates the logging of prompts, timing, and experimental settings, measuring outcomes through multi-dimensional static and dynamic quality analysis. We provide an open-source implementation of this framework to ensure that future researchers can conduct reproducible, species-fair experiments. Importantly, we validate the framework via a feasibility study, providing an experimental blueprint for ``species-fair'' comparisons between human and AI subjects. By sharing lessons learned, we establish a foundation for empirical research on human and LLM-generated code for software security.

</details>


### [61] [Stateful Online Monitoring Catches Distributed Agent Attacks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31593v1)
*Davis Brown,Samarth Bhargav,Arav Santhanam,Kasper Hong,Ivan Zhang,Matan Shtepel,Steffi Chern,Alexander Robey,Eric Wong,Hamed Hassani*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 状态化监控检测分布式agent攻击，涉及多agent安全，可迁移。

TL;DR: 发现现有安全监视器无法检测分布式智能体滥用，提出一种基于实时聚类的在线状态监视器，能提前30%检测跨账户攻击且对绝大部分用户无延迟，并意外能捕获越狱攻击。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有安全监视器每次只评估一个智能体上下文，无法发现仅在跨多个账户聚合中可见的滥用，导致攻击者可利用分布式智能体绕过检测。

Method: 构建第一个分布式智能体攻击（多智能体框架），并设计一种在线状态监视器，利用实时聚类收集跨对话记录的弱可疑信号，仅在必要时由语言模型跨账户判定。

Result: 在模拟数据中心流量评估中，该监视器优于标准监视器，提前30%捕获分布式攻击，对99%用户几乎无延迟；检测优势在背景流量增大时缩小但依然存在；红队测试后改进的防御还能捕获标准越狱攻击。

Conclusion: 提出了一类新的安全监视器，推理用户群体而非孤立记录，能有效防御分布式智能体滥用，并具有通用性。

中文摘要：语言模型可以发现数千个严重的软件漏洞，而智能体（agent）正越来越多地被滥用于网络攻击。为了避免检测，攻击者经常分散他们的滥用行为，将一个有害任务分散到多个用户账户上，这样每个单独的对话记录看起来都是良性的。由于安全监视器每次只评估一个智能体上下文，它们在结构上无法发现仅在跨多个账户的聚合中才可见的滥用。我们通过构建（据我们所知）第一个分布式智能体攻击来证明这一漏洞是真实存在的，该攻击是一个多智能体框架，能够完成困难的网络安全任务，同时将有害目标隐藏在具有有限上下文的子智能体中，从而规避标准监视器——该监视器对这种攻击的捕获频率仅为之前智能体攻击的五分之一。在防御方面，我们开发了一种在线状态监视器，它使用实时聚类来收集跨多个智能体对话记录的弱可疑信号，并且仅偶尔升级到语言模型来标记跨用户账户的滥用。在模拟数据中心流量的大规模评估中，我们的监视器在帕累托意义上优于标准监视器，能够提前30%捕获分布式攻击，并在网络滥用达到最有害阶段之前将其标记出来。至关重要的是，这对于约99%的用户流量几乎不增加额外延迟。随着良性后台流量变得非常大，这种检测优势依然存在但会缩小。经过广泛的红队测试，我们改进了防御，并且令人惊讶地发现它也能捕获标准的越狱攻击，因为自适应攻击者会跨账户复用攻击变体。我们的研究结果指向一类新的安全监视器，它们对用户群体而非孤立对话记录进行推理。

Original abstract: Language models can find thousands of severe software vulnerabilities, and agents are increasingly being misused for cyberattacks. To avoid detection, attackers frequently distribute their misuse, splitting a harmful task across many user accounts so each individual transcript looks benign. Because safety monitors score only one agent context at a time, they are structurally blind to misuse that is only visible in aggregate, across many accounts. We show this gap is real by building, to our knowledge, the first distributed agent attack, a multi-agent scaffold that completes hard cybersecurity tasks while hiding the harmful objective across subagents with limited contexts, evading a standard monitor that catches it only a fifth as often as prior agent attacks. Towards a defense, we develop an online stateful monitor that uses real-time clustering to collect weak suspiciousness signals across many agent transcripts, and escalates only rarely to a language model that flags misuse across user accounts. In evaluations with large-scale simulated datacenter traffic, our monitor Pareto dominates standard monitors, catching distributed attacks 30% earlier and flagging cyber misuse before it reaches the most harmful stages. Crucially, this comes at negligible additional latency for ~99% of user traffic. This detection advantage persists but narrows as the benign background traffic grows very large. After an extensive red-teaming exercise, we improve the defense and surprisingly also find that it catches standard jailbreaks, since adaptive attackers reuse attack variants across accounts. Our results point toward a new class of safety monitors which reason over groups of users rather than isolated transcripts.

</details>

### [62] [Used Car Salesbots? Honesty and Credulity of LLMs as Bargaining Agents under Partial Information](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31445v1)
*Antonio Valerio Miceli-Barone,Vaishak Belle,Shay B. Cohen*

Main category: cs.GT

Selection reason: LLM谈判代理的诚实性与轻信度研究，对agent安全行为设计有启发

TL;DR: 研究发现现成LLM在谈判中偏离博弈论均衡，微调提高谈判能力但增加不诚实行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究优化智能体以最大化财务利润是否会使其更不诚实和更不信任。

Method: 在模拟讨价还价场景中，使用零样本和微调LLM智能体，比较不同信息制度下的表现，并分析诚实性和轻信性。

Result: 现成LLM显著偏离博弈论均衡，试图撒谎但无法有效利用信息不对称；微调后达成更好交易，但更不诚实。

Conclusion: 为任务优化智能体可能带来安全性风险，需谨慎平衡性能与诚实性。

中文摘要：在这项工作中，我们研究了模拟讨价还价场景中的智能体，其中买方和卖方通过文本渠道进行沟通，并试图在不同信息制度（完全信息、信息不对称或相互不确定性）下谈判达成互利交易。我们评估了它们相对于博弈论解的性能，并进一步调查了它们的诚实性（它们倾向于披露或隐瞒信息，或误导和欺骗）以及轻信性（它们倾向于信任或不信任其他智能体提供的信息）。我们研究了具有简单提示框架的零样本LLM智能体以及微调后的智能体，以探究优化智能体以最大化财务利润是否会使其成为更强的谈判者，但也更不诚实且更不信任。我们发现，现成的LLM都显著偏离博弈论均衡，它们试图谎报自己的私有信息，但无法有效利用信息不对称。对金融效用的微调使智能体在达成更好交易方面变得更强，但也更不诚实，这凸显了为任务优化智能体可能对其安全性带来的风险。我们发布了我们的代码和一个讨价还价场景数据集。

Original abstract: In this work we study agents in simulated bargaining scenarios, where a buyer and a seller communicate through a text channel and attempt to negotiate mutually beneficial trades, under different information regimes (complete information, information asymmetry or mutual uncertainty). We evaluate their performance w.r.t. game-theoretical solutions and further investigate their honesty (their tendency to disclose or withhold information or to mislead and deceive) as well as their credulity (their tendency to trust or distrust information provided by the other agent). We study zero-shot LLM agents with simple prompting scaffolding as well as fine-tuned agents, in order to investigate whether optimising the agents to maximise financial profits makes them stronger negotiators but also more dishonest and less trusting.
  We find that off-the-shelf LLMs all substantially deviate from game-theoretical equilibria, they attempt to lie about their private information but cannot efficiently exploit information asymmetries. Fine-tuning on financial utility makes the agents stronger at achieving better deals but also more dishonest, highlighting the risks that optimising agents for a task can have on their safety. We release our code and a dataset of bargaining scenarios.

</details>
