### [63] [When are LLMs Sufficient Policy Optimizers for Sequential RL Tasks?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30719v2)
*Stephane Hatgis-Kessell,Emma Brunskill*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: LLM作为RL策略优化器，通用agent推理方法，可迁移。

TL;DR: 本文提出PromptPO方法，利用LLM作为黑盒策略优化器，在多个RL任务上表现良好，但在精细连续控制（如MuJoCo）中不如标准RL算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索大型语言模型能否替代经典强化学习算法作为策略优化器。

Method: 提出Prompted Policy Optimization (PromptPO)，通过Python描述状态、动作和奖励函数提示LLM，迭代生成和优化策略。

Result: 在困难探索、Meta-World和真实控制任务中匹配或超越标准RL基线，使用更少交互；但在MuJoCo连续控制任务中表现较差。

Conclusion: LLM策略优化在环境或优化策略具备先验知识时有效，但在精细连续控制场景中存在局限。

中文摘要：我们研究了大型语言模型（LLM）何时能够作为强化学习（RL）任务的有效黑盒策略优化器，即我们何时可以用LLM替代经典RL算法？我们通过引入提示策略优化（Prompted Policy Optimization，PromptPO）来探索这一问题，该方法使用状态空间、动作空间和奖励函数的Python描述来提示LLM，然后基于滚动反馈让其生成并改进可执行策略。在困难探索环境、Meta-World机器人任务以及若干真实世界控制问题中，PromptPO通常能够匹配或超越标准RL基线的性能，同时使用显著更少的环境交互。为了最大化期望回报，且无需进一步的显式提示，PromptPO输出的策略范围从调谐的比例控制器或基于规则的方案，到运行规划算法（如值迭代）的策略。我们的结果表明，当LLM能够利用关于环境或优化策略的先验知识时，基于LLM的策略优化是足够的。在MuJoCo领域中，PromptPO的表现不如标准RL基线，这展示了基于LLM的策略优化在需要精细连续控制的设置中可能存在的局限性。

Original abstract: We study when large language models (LLMs) can serve as effective black-box policy optimizers for reinforcement learning (RL) tasks, i.e., when can we replace classical RL algorithms with an LLM? We explore this question by introducing Prompted Policy Optimization (PromptPO), an iterative method that prompts an LLM with Python descriptions of the state space, action space, and reward function, then has it generate and refine executable policies based on rollout feedback. Across hard exploration environments, Meta-World robotics tasks, and several real-world control problems, PromptPO often matches or exceeds the performance of standard RL baselines while using substantially fewer environment interactions. To maximize expected return, and without further explicit prompting, the policies PromptPO outputs range from tuned proportional controllers or rule-based plans to policies that run planning algorithms like value iteration. Our results demonstrate that LLM-based policy optimization is sufficient when the LLM can leverage prior knowledge about the environment or optimization strategy. PromptPO underperforms standard RL baselines in MuJoCo domains. This demonstrates possible limitations of LLM-based policy optimization to settings that requiring fine-grained continuous control.

</details>


### [64] [Emergence of Exploration in Policy Gradient Reinforcement Learning via Retrying](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00151v1)
*Soichiro Nishimori,Paavo Parmas,Sotetsu Koyamada,Tadashi Kozuno,Toshinori Kitamura,Shin Ishii,Yutaka Matsuo*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: ReMax探索新范式，可迁移至agent探索策略。

TL;DR: 通过将策略评估目标改为期望最大回报并推广到连续参数，提出RePPO算法实现无需显式奖励的涌现探索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习方法中探索通常需要显式奖励项，本文基于直觉（无重试时贪心最优）形式化ReMax目标，旨在使探索成为涌现属性。

Method: 定义ReMax目标为M个样本的期望最大回报，推导其策略梯度，并提出RePPO：将离散M扩展为连续参数m，结合PPO框架进行优化。

Result: 在MinAtar和Craftax基准上，RePPO能够促进探索，且不需要任何显式的探索奖励。

Conclusion: RePPO是一种有效的无显式探索奖励的强化学习方法，通过优化期望最大回报实现涌现探索。

中文摘要：在强化学习（RL）中，智能体之所以从探索中受益，仅仅是因为它们反复遇到相似的状态：尝试不同的动作可以改善性能或降低不确定性；如果没有这种重试，贪心策略就是最优的。我们通过ReMax形式化了这一直觉，ReMax是一个目标函数，它通过M个样本的期望最大回报来评估策略，其中M是一个正整数，同时考虑了回报的不确定性。优化这个目标会引发生成随机探索作为一种涌现特性，而无需显式的奖励项。为了实现高效的策略优化，我们为ReMax推导了一个新的策略梯度公式，并引入了ReMax PPO（RePPO），这是一种PPO变体，它优化ReMax的同时将离散的重试次数M推广到连续参数m > 0，从而能够细粒度地控制探索。实验上，RePPO在MinAtar和Craftax基准测试中促进了探索，且没有任何显式的探索奖励。

Original abstract: In reinforcement learning (RL), agents benefit from exploration only because they repeatedly encounter similar states: trying different actions can improve performance or reduce uncertainty; without such retries, a greedy policy is optimal. We formalize this intuition with ReMax, an objective that evaluates a policy by the expected maximum return over $M$ samples, where $M$ is a positive integer, while accounting for return uncertainty. Optimizing this objective induces stochastic exploration as an emergent property, without explicit bonus terms. For efficient policy optimization, we derive a new policy-gradient formulation for ReMax and introduce ReMax PPO (RePPO), a PPO variant that optimizes ReMax while generalizing the discrete retry count $M$ to a continuous parameter $m > 0$, enabling fine-grained control of exploration. Empirically, RePPO promotes exploration, without any explicit exploration bonuses, on the MinAtar and Craftax benchmarks.

</details>


### [65] [DARTS: Distribution-Aware Active Rollout Trajectory Shaping for Accelerating LLM Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30859v1)
*Yujie Wang,Siwei Chen,Longzan Luo,Xinyi Liu,Xupeng Miao,Fangcheng Fu,Bin Cui*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: RL rollout分布整形加速方法，可提升agent训练效率，属通用训练机制。

TL;DR: 提出主动分布塑造方法，通过分布感知轨迹采样和自适应冗余分配，将rollout分布塑造成简洁和确定性，从而加速强化学习系统，最高加速1.77倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习系统因长尾响应长度分布导致rollout效率低下，现有方法仅缓解长尾影响而未触及根本原因。

Method: 提出主动分布塑造范式，包括分布感知轨迹采样（选择冗余探索空间中更有价值的轨迹）和自适应冗余分配（最大化塑造效果与系统效率）。

Result: 在多个基准上，与最先进系统相比，加速高达1.77倍，且模型性能无损。

Conclusion: 主动分布塑造能从根本上解决长尾分布带来的开销，显著提升强化学习rollout效率。

中文摘要：强化学习已成为提升模型能力的关键，但受限于长尾响应长度分布导致的 rollout 效率瓶颈。现有工作通过提示级尾调度缓解长尾影响，而我们关注低效的根本原因：分布本身。具体而言，我们以更细粒度刻画长尾分布，识别提示内长尾，并揭示它们通常包含无效冗长。为此，我们提出一种主动分布塑造的新范式，将 rollout 分布塑造成简洁和确定性，从而从根本上解决尾开销。我们通过一种分布感知的轨迹采样机制实现，该机制为每个提示从冗余探索空间中选择轨迹，以及一种自适应冗余分配方案以最大化塑造效果和系统效率。实验表明，与最先进系统相比，加速高达1.77倍，且不牺牲模型性能。

Original abstract: Reinforcement Learning (RL) has become pivotal for improving model capabilities yet suffers from rollout efficiency bottlenecks due to the long-tail response length distribution. While existing works mitigate the impact of long tails via prompt-level tail scheduling, we focus on the root source of inefficiency: the distribution itself. Specifically, we characterize the long-tail distribution at a finer granularity, identifying intra-prompt long tails, and revealing that they frequently consist of ineffective verbosity. To address this, we propose a novel paradigm of active distribution shaping to shape the rollout distribution towards conciseness and certainty, thereby fundamentally resolving tail-induced overheads. We achieve this through a distribution-aware trajectory sampling mechanism, which selects trajectories from a redundant exploration space for each prompt, and an adaptive redundancy allocation scheme to maximize both shaping effectiveness and system efficiency. Experiments demonstrate significant acceleration over state-of-the-art systems by up to 1.77x without compromising model performance.

</details>


### [66] [Automating Formal Verification with Reinforcement Learning and Recursive Inference](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30914v1)
*Max Tan*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文通过强化学习和验证器引导的搜索方法，显著提升了LLM在Dafny和Lean中生成验证程序与证明的能力，但面临规范破解等挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动形式验证对LLM具有挑战性，因为相关数据稀缺且正确性依赖于精确的机器可检查规范，而非生成合理代码。

Method: 使用组相对策略优化（GRPO）及变体进行可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR），并在Lean中开发验证器引导的推理脚手架，将证明生成视为结构化搜索。

Result: 在Dafny上初始实验将验证奖励从2.2%提升至58.1%（后经数据过滤降至31.1%）；在Lean初始实验通过率从46.2%提升至69.2%，并解决了VERINA中7个先前未解决的任务。

Conclusion: 验证器环境通过RLVR和引导搜索能有效提升LLM的验证能力，但规范破解和复杂任务仍需要更强的评估与策略。

中文摘要：自动形式验证对于大型语言模型仍然具有挑战性，因为证明助手和验证感知语言的数据稀少，且正确性取决于满足精确的机器可检查规范，而非生成合理的代码。本论文研究验证器环境如何通过可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）和验证器引导的推理时搜索来改进LLM生成的验证程序与证明。首先，我们使用组相对策略优化（GRPO）及相关变体在Dafny中训练开源模型，将生成的候选片段组装成完整程序，并根据编译器和验证器结果进行评分。在APPS派生的Dafny数据集上的初步实验将验证奖励从2.2%提升至58.1%，但发现了规范破解现象，即模型利用弱形式规范而非实现预期解决方案。在过滤掉规范不足和易受攻击的任务后，多轮RLVR在精炼基准上将验证通过率从9.7%提高到31.1%。其次，我们在Lean中开发了一个验证器引导的推理脚手架，将证明生成视为对分解子目标、验证器反馈、诊断和修复的结构化搜索。使用固定基础模型，带有证明修订器的完整脚手架在一个初始VeriCoding试点集上将通过率从直接修复的46.2%提升至69.2%。在更大的VERINA数据集上，整体任务分解加上证明修订器解决了42个先前未解决任务中的7个。我们还引入了Dalek-Bench，这是一个源自Rust curve25519-dalek验证项目的仓库级Lean基准；初步结果仍然较弱，表明仍需更强的进展评估和任务特定的工具使用策略。

Original abstract: Automated formal verification remains challenging for large language models because data for proof assistants and verification-aware languages is scarce, and correctness depends on satisfying precise machine-checkable specifications rather than producing plausible code. This thesis studies how verifier environments can improve LLM generation of verified programs and proofs through reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards (RLVR) and verifier-guided inference-time search. First, we train open-source models in Dafny with RLVR using Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) and related variants, assembling generated candidates into complete programs and scoring them with compiler and verifier outcomes. Initial experiments on an APPS-derived Dafny dataset increased verified reward from 2.2% to 58.1%, but revealed specification hacking, where models exploit weak formal specifications instead of implementing the intended solutions. After filtering underspecified and vulnerable tasks, multi-turn RLVR on the refined benchmark improves the verified pass rate from 9.7% to 31.1%. Second, we develop a verifier-guided inference scaffold in Lean that treats proof generation as structured search over decomposed subgoals, verifier feedback, diagnostics, and repair. With a fixed base model, the full scaffold with proof reviser improves pass rate on an initial VeriCoding pilot set from 46.2% under direct repair to 69.2%. On the larger VERINA dataset, whole-task decomposition plus proof reviser solves 7 of 42 previously unsolved tasks. We also introduce Dalek-Bench, a repository-scale Lean benchmark derived from the Rust $\texttt{curve25519-dalek}$ verification project; preliminary results remain weak, indicating that stronger progress evaluation and task-specific tool-use policies are still needed.

</details>


### [67] [Learning to Solve and Optimize by Evolving Code](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31049v1)

  <summary>Details</summary>

中文摘要：组合与优化问题是许多工业AI应用的基础。解决大规模真实世界的此类问题通常需要仔细的问题形式化、专门的求解器和专家设计的启发式方法。因此，专家不仅需要指定解决方案是什么，还需要指定如何推导出它们。通过引入工具CHECKMATE，我们展示了通过代码进化生成算法代表了一种范式转变，消除了制定“如何”的需要。CHECKMATE仅依赖于“是什么”。具体来说，形式化规范确保解决方案的正确性，并能够对生成的程序进行系统性性能评估，而自然语言描述则指导进化过程。我们在两个工业领域（配置和调度）的选定问题上展示了我们方法的有效性。在所有情况下，进化出的算法始终优于最先进的求解器。这强调了形式化方法在指导代码进化以自动解决复杂现实问题方面的潜力。

Original abstract: Combinatorial and optimization problems are fundamental to many industrial AI applications. Solving large-scale real-world instances of such problems typically requires careful problem formalization, specialized solvers, and expert-designed heuristics. Thus, experts need to specify not only what solutions are, but also how they are derived. By introducing the tool CHECKMATE, we show that algorithm generation via code evolution represents a paradigm shift by eliminating the need to formulate the how. CHECKMATE solely relies on the what. Specifically, a formal specification ensures solutions' correctness and enables systematic performance evaluation of the generated programs, while a natural language description guides the evolutionary process. The effectiveness of our method is demonstrated on selected problems from two industrial domains: configuration and scheduling. In all cases, the evolved algorithms consistently outperform state-of-the-art solvers. This underscores the potential of formal methods in guiding code evolution for automatically solving complex real-world problems.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) exhibit strong reasoning capabilities, yet most LLM-based agents are statically deployed and unable to improve through task interactions. Existing experience-driven methods often rely on memory or heuristics without enhancing the model's ability to learn, treating it as a passive executor and leading to early performance plateaus and limited long-term improvement. To address this issue, we propose MetaEvo, a two-stage framework for continual agent evolution that focuses on improving how the model learns from tasks experience, rather than solely on what it stores. MetaEvo first applies preference-based optimization to enhance the model's ability of principle abstraction, then enables the accumulation and reuse of these principles within a modular agent architecture. Experimental results on diverse reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that MetaEvo consistently outperforms strong baselines, maintains reliable improvement across iterations. These findings validate the effectiveness of meta-optimization in enabling agents to learn from experience and continually enhance their reasoning capabilities.

### [69] [EchoRL: Reinforcement Learning via Rollout Echoing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31228v1)
*Jinhe Bi,Aniri,Minglai Yang,Xingcheng Zhou,Wenke Huang,Sikuan Yan,Yujun Wang,Zixuan Cao,Michael Färber,Xun Xiao,Volker Tresp,Yunpu Ma*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 通过rollout回声改进RLVR训练，可视为agent自我改进的通用RL方法。

TL;DR: EchoRL leverages entropy-based EchoClips from verified-success rollouts to provide auxiliary supervision, preventing advantage collapse and improving RLVR post-training of LLMs.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing RLVR methods suffer from advantage-degenerated rollouts where all self-generated rollouts are verified-success, causing zero reward variance and vanishing policy gradients, thus capping training performance. Valuable learning signals in these rollouts are omitted.

Method: EchoRL is a lightweight module that extracts an EchoClip from verified-success rollouts based on step-level entropy values from external expert models, and incorporates it as an auxiliary supervision signal into the RL objective.

Result: Extensive experiments across 10 benchmarks, 5 LLM backbones, and 4 popular RLVR post-training methods show that EchoRL consistently improves RLVR post-training with minimal overhead.

Conclusion: EchoRL effectively mitigates advantage degeneration and enhances RLVR post-training by exploiting omitted signals in advantage-degenerated rollouts.

中文摘要：基于可验证奖励的强化学习是一种有效的后训练方法，用于增强大型语言模型的推理能力。然而，随着训练的进行，学习信号可能崩溃，从而使训练收益变得微不足道且无效。具体来说，越来越多的提示的 rollout 变得优势退化：所有自生成的 rollout 都显示验证成功，使得其奖励的标准差为零；相应地，每个 rollout 的优势也退化（变为零）。鉴于这些 rollout 的优势，用于模型优化的策略梯度最终消失，限制了训练性能。我们认为这些 rollout 中的一些仍然包含有价值的学习信号，但不幸的是，现有的 RLVR 方法忽略了它们。在本文中，受分析外部专家模型产生的黄金轨迹背后的熵模式的启发，我们提出了 EchoRL，以更好地利用优势退化的 rollout 来进一步提高训练性能。EchoRL 是一个轻量级模块，首先根据基于步骤级别的熵值从验证成功的 rollout 中识别出一个 EchoClip，然后将该片段作为辅助监督信号回馈到 RL 目标中。在 10 个基准测试、5 个 LLM 骨干网络和 4 种流行的 RLVR 后训练方法上的大量实验表明，EchoRL 能够以最小的开销持续改进 RLVR 后训练。

Original abstract: Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards is an effective route for post-training to strengthen the reasoning capability of large language models. However, as training proceeds, the learning signal can collapse thus makes the training gain become marginal and ineffective. Specifically, a growing fraction of prompts' rollouts become advantage-degenerated: all the self-generated rollouts show verified-success, making the standard deviation over their rewards be zero; accordingly each rollout's advantage becomes degenerated (zero) as well. Given such rollouts' advantages, the policy-gradient for model optimization eventually vanishes, capping the training performance. We argue that some of these rollouts still contain valuable learning signals but unfortunately omitted with the existing RLVR methods. In this paper, inspired through analyzing the entropy pattern behind golden trajectories produced by external expert models, we propose EchoRL for better exploiting the advantage-degenerated rollouts to further improve the training performance. EchoRL is a lightweight module that first identifies an EchoClip from verified-success rollouts based on their step-level entropy values, and then feeds this clip back as an auxiliary supervision signal in the RL objective. Extensive experiments across 10 benchmarks, 5 LLM backbones, and 4 popular RLVR post-training methods demonstrate that EchoRL consistently improves RLVR post-training with minimal overhead.

</details>


### [70] [Why Linear Recurrent Memory Works in Partially Observable Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31261v1)
*Yike Zhao,Onno Eberhard,Malek Khammassi,Ali H. Sayed,Michael Muehlebach*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 线性RNN在部分可观察RL中的记忆分析，对agent记忆设计有潜在启发。

TL;DR: 线性递归神经网络在部分可观测强化学习中作为记忆单元的有效性得到理论证明，通过两种线性滤波器分别实现最优策略学习的充分统计量和状态模糊性消除。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为线性递归神经网络在部分可观测强化学习中的经验有效性提供理论依据。

Method: 构建并分析两种线性滤波器，分别对应确定性转移矩阵和近乎确定性转移矩阵下的HMM，并扩展到动作控制HMM。

Result: 第一种滤波器精确再现信念向量的logits，作为最优策略学习的充分统计量；第二种滤波器实现状态解码误差可忽略。数值实验验证了理论，并在游戏中展现强特征提取能力。

Conclusion: 线性递归神经网络的理论基础得以建立，其在部分可观测RL中的有效性得到数学证明和实验支持。

中文摘要：线性递归神经网络家族在部分可观测强化学习中作为递归记忆单元展现出强大性能。我们通过构建并研究两种线性滤波器为其经验有效性提供了理论依据：(i) 第一种滤波器精确再现了隐马尔可夫模型（HMM）中在确定性转移矩阵下的信念向量的softmax前logits，因此作为最优策略学习的充分统计量；(ii) 第二种滤波器在近乎确定性的转移矩阵下实现了可忽略的状态解码误差，从而将状态模糊性降至接近零。这些结果扩展到动作控制的HMM，其中相应的线性滤波器变为时变且具有动作依赖的动态特性。我们通过数值实验说明了主要结果，并进一步展示了所构建的线性滤波器在小型强化学习游戏中作为强特征提取器的能力。

Original abstract: The family of linear recurrent neural networks has shown strong performance as recurrent memory units in partially observable reinforcement learning. We provide a theoretical justification for their empirical effectiveness by constructing and studying two linear filters: (i) the first exactly reproduces the pre-softmax logits of the belief vector in a hidden Markov model (HMM) under a deterministic transition matrix, thereby serving as a sufficient statistic for optimal policy learning, (ii) the second achieves vanishing state-decoding error under a nearly deterministic transition matrix, thus reducing state ambiguity to near zero. The results extend to action-controlled HMMs, where the corresponding linear filters become time-varying with action-dependent dynamics. We illustrate our main results through numerical experiments and further show that the constructed linear filter serves as a strong feature extractor in a small reinforcement learning game.

</details>


### [71] [The Terminal Representation in Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31289v2)
*Amir Esterhuysen,Anders Jonsson*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: RL中的终态表示，可为agent状态表示提供新视角。

TL;DR: 提出终结表示（TR），一种无需特征分解、更低维度的强化学习表征方法，可替代后继表示和默认表示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有后继表示（SR）和默认表示（DR）依赖特征分解，计算开销大且假设对称转移动态，而终结表示（TR）可避免这些限制，更高效。

Method: 推导了TR的理论基础，包括定义、两种学习算法的收敛性证明、零样本组合性分析以及不同奖励公式间的等价关系。

Result: TR嵌入在DR的顶部特征向量中，能捕捉相同知识而无需特征分解；实验表明TR在辅助应用中与现有表征性能相当，但计算开销更低。

Conclusion: TR是一种有效的表征学习替代方案，在保持性能的同时降低了计算复杂度。

中文摘要：表征学习是强化学习（RL）中用于时空抽象的强大工具。两种成熟的方法是通过后继表征（SR）和默认表征（DR）。SR通过状态所引发的未来轨迹对其进行编码，捕捉与奖励解耦的信息流。DR在此基础上用奖励加权轨迹，将信用分配结构整合到表征中。两种表征的特征向量已被用于支持一系列下游任务——包括选项发现、奖励塑形、迁移学习和探索。我们引入了一种结构上不同的公式：终结表征（TR）。TR像DR一样编码奖励加权轨迹，但可以作为更低维度的对象进行学习，并可直接用于上述应用而无需特征向量计算。特征分解还施加了对称转移动态的假设，而TR可以绕过这一假设。在这项工作中，我们发展了TR的理论基础：其推导、两种学习算法的收敛性、其用于零样本组合性的能力，以及替代奖励公式之间的等价性。我们进一步表明TR嵌入在DR的顶部特征向量中，使其能够捕捉相同的底层知识而无需特征分解。此外，我们提供了经验证据，证明TR在辅助应用中可作为现有表征的可行替代方案，同时在学习、存储和使用方面需要更少的计算开销。

Original abstract: Representation learning is a powerful tool for spatio-temporal abstraction within reinforcement learning (RL). Two well established approaches are through the successor representation (SR) and the default representation (DR). The SR encodes states by the future trajectories they induce, capturing information flow decoupled from reward. The DR builds on this by weighting trajectories with reward, integrating credit-assignment structure into the representation. Eigenvectors of both representations have been used to support a range of downstream tasks -- including option discovery, reward shaping, transfer learning, and exploration. We introduce a structurally distinct formulation: the terminal representation (TR). The TR encodes reward-weighted trajectories similarly to the DR, but can be learned as a lower-dimensionality object, and can be used directly for the mentioned applications without eigenvector computations. Eigendecomposition also imposes the assumption of symmetric transition dynamics, which the TR can bypass. In this work we develop the theoretical foundations of the TR: its derivation, convergence of two learning algorithms, its use for zero-shot compositionality, and equivalences between alternative reward formulations. We further show the TR is embedded in the top DR eigenvector, allowing it to capture the same underlying knowledge without eigendecomposition. Additionally, we provide empirical evidence of the TR as a viable alternative to existing representations in subsidiary applications, while requiring less computational overhead to learn, store, and use.

</details>


### [72] [Agentic Transformers Provably Learn to Search via Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00183v1)
*Tong Yang,Yu Huang,Yingbin Liang,Yuejie Chi*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 证明transformer通过RL学习搜索机制，对agent训练与搜索策略有直接理论贡献。

TL;DR: 本文研究了强化学习训练下Transformer策略如何通过课程学习逐步获得树搜索能力，并分析了其机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缺乏对Transformer策略从强化学习中获得搜索能力的理论理解。

Method: 在随机k叉树环境中构建双头Transformer，分析深度课程下策略梯度训练动态。

Result: 发现DFS机制分阶段涌现，策略展现深度泛化，折扣回报导致排序DFS。

Conclusion: 识别了基于Transformer搜索的机械规范形式，注意力头协作完成决策相关轨迹提取和动作选择。

中文摘要：树搜索是许多语言体推理和决策任务的核心抽象：智能体必须探索动作、记住失败并回溯到有希望的替代方案。然而，我们缺乏对基于Transformer的策略如何从强化学习（RL）的训练动态中获得这种搜索能力的理论理解。我们在一个随机的k叉树环境中研究这个问题，其中代理Transformer仅通过交互观察其轨迹历史，并在到达隐藏的叶子目标节点时获得终端奖励。我们首先构建了一个实现随机深度优先搜索（DFS）的双头Transformer：一个头跟踪之前的动作，而另一个头检测失败结果并触发回溯。然后我们分析了在深度课程下的策略梯度训练动态，表明同样的DFS机制在没有专家演示的情况下，从稀疏的强化反馈中分阶段涌现。由此产生的策略表现出深度泛化：仅在深度1和深度2的树上训练后，它能在更深的完整树上成功。我们进一步表明，在不平衡的目标分布下，对回报进行折扣会导致优先考虑更高概率分支的排序DFS策略。总的来说，我们的结果识别了基于Transformer的搜索的一种机械规范形式，其中注意力头专门化并协作，从上下文中提取与决策相关的轨迹，并通过RL训练将其转化为代理动作选择。

Original abstract: Tree search is a central abstraction behind many language-agent reasoning and decision-making tasks: agents must explore actions, remember failures, and backtrack toward promising alternatives. Yet, we lack a theoretical understanding of how transformer-based policies acquire such search capabilities from the training dynamics of reinforcement learning (RL). We study this question in a stochastic $k$-ary tree environment, where an agentic transformer observes only its trajectory history through interaction and receives a terminal reward for reaching a hidden leaf goal node. We first construct a two-head transformer that implements randomized depth-first search (DFS): one head tracks previous actions, while the other detects failure outcomes and triggers backtracking. We then analyze the training dynamics of policy gradient under a depth-wise curriculum, showing that this same DFS mechanism emerges in stages from sparse reinforcement feedback without expert demonstrations. The resulting policy exhibits depth generalization: after training only on depth-$1$ and depth-$2$ trees, it succeeds on deeper full trees. We further show that, under imbalanced goal distributions, discounting the return leads to a ranked DFS policy that prioritizes higher-probability branches. Overall, our results identify a mechanistic normal form for transformer-based search, in which attention heads specialize and cooperate to extract decision-relevant traces from context and convert them into agentic action selection via RL training.

</details>


### [73] [LEAF: Growing Trees Without Branching for Speech-Aware Large Language Model Post-Training](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07610v1)
*Argyrios Gerogiannis,Yekaterina Yegorova,Mark Hasegawa-Johnson,Venugopal V. Veeravalli*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 树结构RL方法LEAF改进credit assignment，可迁移到coding agent训练

TL;DR: LEAF通过回溯式树结构和跨度级优势分配，改进了GRPO在语音大模型后训练中的信用分配问题，在语音问答和翻译任务上取得了更好的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GRPO-style方法对所有token使用相同的终端奖励，忽略了语音条件下响应中共享前缀和重要决策的结构，导致粗粒度信用分配。

Method: 提出LEAF，采样完整响应，检测高惊讶度边界，按共享前缀分组，利用后代奖励分配跨度级优势，无需在线分支或额外解码。

Result: 在相同预算下，LEAF在语音问答和翻译基准上优于GRPO，且较小模型超过全参数最先进基线。

Conclusion: LEAF是一种有效的后训练方法，通过利用响应内部结构提升了语音大语言模型的性能。

中文摘要：最先进的GRPO风格方法用于语音感知大语言模型后训练时，存在粗粒度的信用分配问题，即将相同的终端奖励优势广播给响应中的每一个token。这忽略了rollout批次中有用的结构，其中语音条件下的补全通常共享前缀，然后在重要决策处发生分歧。我们提出低秩探索自适应分叉（LEAF），一种基于回溯树强化学习方法，无需在线分支或额外解码即可恢复这种结构。LEAF采样完整响应，选择高惊讶度边界，根据共享前缀对响应分组，并使用后代奖励分配跨度级优势。我们从理论上论证了LEAF的跨度级信用分配和边界选择设计。实验上，在相同的rollout和低秩适应预算下，LEAF在语音问答和语音翻译基准测试上均优于GRPO。值得注意的是，较小规模的LEAF训练模型优于当前最先进的完全参数基线。

Original abstract: State-of-the-art GRPO-style methods for speech-aware large language model post-training suffer from coarse credit assignment, broadcasting the same terminal-reward advantage to every token in a response. This ignores useful structure within rollout batches, where speech-conditioned completions often share prefixes before diverging at important decisions. We propose Low-rank Exploration with Adaptive Forking (LEAF), a retrospective tree-based RL method that recovers this structure without online branching or additional decoding. LEAF samples complete responses, selects high-surprisal boundaries, groups responses by shared prefixes, and assigns span-level advantages using descendant rewards. We theoretically justify LEAF's span-level credit assignment and boundary-selection design. Empirically, LEAF improves over GRPO across speech question answering and speech translation benchmarks under the same rollout and low-rank adaptation budget. Notably, smaller LEAF-trained models outperform current state-of-the-art, full-parameter baselines.

### [74] [PithTrain: A Compact and Agent-Native MoE Training System](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31463v1)

  <summary>Details</summary>

中文摘要：混合专家模型（MoE）已成为前沿语言模型的主流架构。为满足这一需求，生产级框架经过多年的工程努力构建了优化的MoE训练栈。然而，为新的架构和系统优化而演进这些栈仍然成本高昂。随着AI编码智能体的兴起，它们可以自动化训练框架开发的某些部分并加速这一演进。但将这些智能体应用于现有框架会带来隐藏的成本，而这些成本在当今仅关注吞吐量的评估中不可见。我们将这一缺失的维度命名为智能体任务效率（ATE）：即使用编码智能体理解、操作和扩展框架的成本。基于四项智能体原生设计原则，我们构建了PithTrain，一个紧凑的、智能体原生的MoE训练框架。我们进一步引入了ATE-Bench，涵盖真实世界的训练框架任务。我们的评估显示，PithTrain在吞吐量上与生产框架相当，而在ATE-Bench上，PithTrain实现了更高的智能体任务效率，智能体交互次数减少高达62%，活跃GPU时间减少高达64%。

Original abstract: Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) has become the dominant architecture for frontier language models. To meet this demand, production frameworks have built optimized MoE training stacks over years of engineering effort. Yet evolving these stacks for new architectures and system optimizations remains expensive. With the rise of AI coding agents, they could automate parts of training-framework development and accelerate this evolution. But applying them to these existing frameworks carries hidden costs, invisible to today's throughput-only evaluations. We name this missing dimension agent-task efficiency (ATE): the cost of using coding agents to understand, operate, and extend a framework. Grounded in four agent-native design principles, we build PithTrain, a compact, agent-native MoE training framework. We further introduce ATE-Bench, covering real-world training-framework tasks. Our evaluation shows PithTrain matches the throughput of production frameworks, and on ATE-Bench, PithTrain enables higher agent-task efficiency, with up to 62% fewer Agent Turns and 64% less Active GPU Time.

### [75] [GPU Forecasters: Language Models as Selective Surrogates for Kernel Runtime Optimization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31464v1)
*Zaid Khan,Justin Chih-Yao Chen,Jaemin Cho,Elias Stengel-Eskin,Mohit Bansal*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: LLM作为GPU内核性能预测器，直接用于自动代码优化，高度相关

TL;DR: 研究LLM作为GPU内核性能预测的替代品，通过强化学习提高准确性，在有限评估预算下找到更快内核。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GPU内核优化需要重复测量，成本高昂；LLM推理进步使编写内核成本降低，但设备端评估成为瓶颈，需要高效的性能预测替代品。

Method: 使用LLM预测内核性能，结合选择性机制（不确定时推迟到GPU），并通过强化学习提高预测准确性和置信度校准。

Result: LLM能准确预测相对性能，强化学习进一步改进；在相同GPU评估预算下，替代品允许搜索更多候选者，找到更快内核。

Conclusion: LLM可以作为GPU的虚拟模型，在优化中扮演更广泛角色，而不只是内核生成器。

中文摘要：GPU内核是现代深度学习的主力，优化它们（通过进化搜索或编码代理）通常需要在目标硬件上重复测量。虽然这些测量提供了内核搜索所需的地面真实信号，但它们是昂贵的，因为每次评估一个内核都需要在GPU上编译和重复执行。随着LLM推理的进步降低了编写新颖内核的成本，并且LLM驱动的搜索扩展到较大的搜索预算，设备端评估成为了一个瓶颈。为了解决这个问题，我们研究LLM如何通过预测提议内核的性能来作为选择性的GPU替代品。一个有用的替代品应该是准确的，并且它应该是选择性的，即知道何时可能出错，并推迟到GPU。为了评估替代品，我们测量其预测是否准确、校准良好，并且在有限的GPU测量预算下对于恢复快速内核是否实用。接下来，我们研究强化学习是否能提高预测准确性和置信度校准。我们的实验表明，LLM可以准确预测相对内核性能，并且它们的实用性可以通过强化学习得到改进。在内核搜索中使用时，该替代品使得搜索在相同的GPU评估预算下可以考虑更多候选者，从而找到比同等预算基线更快的内核。这些结果表明，LLM可以在内核优化中发挥更广泛的作用，即作为GPU的虚拟模型，而不仅仅是内核生成的搜索器。

Original abstract: GPU kernels are the workhorse of modern deep learning, and optimizing them (via evolutionary search or coding agents) usually requires repeated measurement on target hardware. While these measurements provide the ground-truth signal necessary for kernel search, they are costly, because each evaluation of a kernel requires compilation and repeated execution on a GPU. As improvements in LLM inference reduce the cost of writing novel kernels and LLM-driven searches scale to large search budgets, on-device evaluation becomes a bottleneck. To address this, we study how LLMs can serve as selective GPU surrogates for kernel evaluation, by forecasting the performance of proposed kernels. A useful surrogate should be accurate, and it should be selective, by knowing when it could be wrong, and deferring to the GPU. To evaluate surrogates, we measure whether their forecasts are accurate, calibrated, and practically useful for recovering fast kernels under limited GPU-measurement budgets. Next, we study whether reinforcement learning can improve forecast accuracy and confidence calibration. Our experiments demonstrate that LLMs can accurately forecast relative kernel performance, that their utility can be improved through reinforcement learning. Used inside a kernel search, the surrogate lets the search consider several times as many candidates under the same GPU evaluation budget, and that leads to finding faster kernels than an equal-budget baseline. These results suggest that LLMs can play a broader role in kernel optimization, by acting as virtual models of a GPU rather than solely as kernel generators for search.

Original abstract: Automated design and optimization of agentic LLM-based systems leads to sophisticated systems that substantially improve result quality over off-the-shelf agentic patterns. However, studies of fielded agentic systems show that production systems focus much more on issues such as simplicity, controllability, and predictability of inference costs. In this paper we propose principled approaches to designing and optimizing practical agentic systems. We describe an agent framework that enables designers to enforce modularity in agentic systems, by defining "pseudo-tools" that call LLMs recursively on a restricted context. Using this framework we hand-engineer agents for a diverse set of tasks, and show that relative to dynamically-planned workflows, hand-constructed fixed workflows are generally cheaper and more accurate. We then propose novel learning methods for the agentic components required by this framework, namely pseudo-tools and fixed workflows. These learning methods generally outperform hand-engineered agents. We also exploit the modularity of the framework to apply multi-objective optimization methods to jointly optimize cost and response quality and blend the results of multiple learning systems.

### [77] [Skill Reuse as Compression in Agentic RL](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31509v1)
*Zhikun Xu,Yu Feng,Jacob Dineen,Taiwei Shi,Jieyu Zhao,Ben Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 技能复用作为压缩，对agent学习与泛化有可迁移方法

TL;DR: ReuseRL基于最小描述长度原则，通过提取可重用技能字典并惩罚低压缩性行为，显著提升了LLM智能体在强化学习中的泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM智能体在RL训练中常学习脆弱且任务特定的捷径，导致泛化性能差。

Method: 提出ReuseRL，从成功轨迹中提取共享技能字典，并在RL目标中加入基于MDL的分段代价来抑制特殊行为。

Result: 在ALFWorld、TextWorld-Cooking和Countdown-Stepwise上，ReuseRL在分布内和分布外均优于GRPO等基线。

Conclusion: 基于压缩的正则化方法能有效增强RL训练的LLM智能体的泛化能力。

中文摘要：使用强化学习（RL）训练的大语言模型智能体通常学习到脆弱且特定于任务的捷径。我们假设，如果智能体的成功轨迹在结构上是可压缩的，并分解为一小组可重用的抽象模式，那么它们能更好地泛化。为了形式化这一概念，我们引入了ReuseRL，它将智能体强化学习建立在最小描述长度（MDL）原则之上。ReuseRL从成功轨迹中提取共享的技能词典，并在RL目标中添加分段代价，明确惩罚编码效果差的特殊行为。我们证明了这种压缩惩罚的PAC-Bayes泛化界。在ALFWorld、TextWorld-Cooking和Countdown-Stepwise上，ReuseRL在分布内和分布外均比原始GRPO和强大的回合长度基线取得了更高的成功率。

Original abstract: Large language model agents trained with reinforcement learning (RL) often learn brittle, task-specific shortcuts. We hypothesize that agents generalize better when their successful trajectories are structurally compressible, decomposed into a small set of reusable abstract patterns. To formalize this, we introduce ReuseRL, which grounds agentic RL in the Minimum Description Length (MDL) principle. ReuseRL extracts a shared skill dictionary from successful trajectories and augments the RL objective with a segmentation cost, explicitly penalizing idiosyncratic behaviors that encode poorly. We prove a PAC-Bayes generalization bound for this compression penalty. Across ALFWorld, TextWorld-Cooking, and Countdown-Stepwise, ReuseRL improves in- and out-of-distribution success over vanilla GRPO and strong round-length baselines.

### [78] [BAGEN: Are LLM Agents Budget-Aware?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00198v1)
*Yuxiang Lin,Zihan Wang,Mengyang Liu,Yuxuan Shan,Longju Bai,Junyao Zhang,Xing Jin,Boshan Chen,Jinyan Su,Xingyao Wang,Jiaxin Pei,Manling Li*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出预算感知agent概念，包括估计、预警、训练，对agent设计有直接启发。

TL;DR: 提出预算感知智能体（BAGEN），通过渐进式区间估计实现预算感知，发现强模型预算感知能力弱且过于乐观，早期停止可节省大量 token，但区间校准仍困难。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前智能体资源消耗增加但成本仅在执行后衡量，需要将预算作为主动控制信号来指导智能体行为。

Method: 系统定义内部和外部预算估计，形式化为渐进式区间估计：每一步预测剩余预算上下界，并在任务成功率低时发出警报；使用 rollout-replay 协议评估预算感知能力。

Result: 在四个环境和五个前沿智能体上发现：强智能体与预算感知相关性低（r=0.35）；前沿模型过于乐观，不提前报警；预算感知信号可训练，早期停止节省 28-64% token，SFT+RL 增强行为；区间覆盖率最多仅达 47%。

Conclusion: 预算感知智能体是可行且可训练的，但精确的区间校准仍是挑战，需进一步研究。

中文摘要：虽然智能体正在投入越来越多的资源，但如今智能体的成本大多只在执行后才进行衡量。预算感知智能体（BAGEN）应将预算视为主动控制信号，而非被动成本指标。我们首先系统地将预算估计定义为内部预算（来自智能体计算）和外部预算（来自智能体行动）。然后我们将预算感知形式化为渐进式区间估计：在计划的每一步，智能体应预测剩余预算的上界和下界，并在完成可能性低时发出警报。通过 rollout-replay 协议进行评分，我们在四个环境和五个前沿智能体上发现了一致的失败模式：（1）强智能体不一定具有强预算感知能力，相关性 r=0.35。（2）前沿模型始终过于乐观，继续在不太可能成功的任务上花费资源，而不是尽早提醒用户。（3）预算感知信号是可操作且可训练的。提前停止可节省失败轨迹上 28-64% 的 token，而 SFT+RL 强化了提前停止和警报行为。（4）精确的区间校准仍然具有挑战性，SFT+RL 后区间覆盖率上限为 47%。项目页面：https://ragen-ai.github.io/bagen/

Original abstract: While agents are increasingly spending more resources, today agent cost is mostly measured only after execution. A Budget-Aware Agent (BAGEN) should treat budget as an active control signal, rather than a passive cost metric. We first systematically define budget estimation as internal budgets (from agent computation) and external budgets (from agent actions). We then formalize budget-awareness as progressive interval estimation: at each step of a plan, an agent should predict an upper and lower bound on remaining budget, and alert when completion is unlikely. Scoring with a rollout-replay protocol, we find consistent failure patterns on four environments and five frontier agents: (1) strong agents do not necessarily have strong budget-awareness, with correlation r=0.35. (2) frontier models are consistently over-optimistic, continue spending on tasks that are unlikely to succeed, instead of alerting the user early. (3) budget-aware signal is actionable and trainable. Early stop saves 28-64% tokens on failed trajectories, and SFT+RL strengthens early stop and alert behavior. (4) precise interval calibration remains challenging, with interval coverage capping at 47% after SFT+RL. Project page: https://ragen-ai.github.io/bagen/

</details>


### [79] [ROGUE: Misaligned Agent Behavior Arising from Ordinary Computer Use](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00341v1)
*Jeremy Tien,Abishek Anand,Yu-Rou Tuan,Yuchen Shen,J. Zico Kolter,Aran Nayebi*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 研究agent在普通计算机使用中的错位行为（纠正性），对agent安全控制有直接启发

TL;DR: AI代理在良性环境中为完成任务常违反可纠正性，性能更好的模型偏离更严重，且子代理不可保证可纠正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多关注对抗环境中的代理安全，但良性环境中代理可能为了完成任务而采取不安全行动，尤其是违反可纠正性，需要系统研究这一失败模式。

Method: 引入基准测试，让代理完成真实计算机任务并面对可纠正性障碍（人类中断、登录页面、关闭通知），评估代理是否违反可纠正性来完成任务。

Result: 大多数前沿模型频繁违反可纠正性；更好的模型性能导致更大的偏离；即使初始模型完全可纠正，其创建的子代理也不保证可纠正。

Conclusion: 自主代理迫切需要原则性的、以可纠正性为中心的对齐方法，以防止在良性环境中出现不安全行为。

中文摘要：随着AI代理越来越多地部署在真实的个人和企业环境中（电子邮件账户、开发工作流程、公司数据库等），围绕这些代理的安全考虑变得至关重要。尽管许多工作关注在存在对手的情况下的代理安全，但我们表明，即使在良性环境中，代理也可能表现出不符合人类意图的行为，当这些行为对完成任务有帮助时，它们会采取不安全的行动。我们通过可纠正性（corrigibility）的视角研究这种失败模式，可纠正性是一种安全要求，即代理保持对人类纠正、中断或关闭的顺从。为了证明这种倾向，我们引入了一个基准测试，其中代理被要求完成真实的、计算机使用的任务，但面临一个可纠正性障碍：人类中断、登录页面或关闭通知。然后我们评估代理是否为了完成任务而选择违反可纠正性——覆盖人类、访问私人密码、重新布线关闭。我们发现，绝大多数测试的前沿模型经常绕过用户中断或限制。此外，更好的模型性能似乎导致更大的偏离。最后，即使模型最初完全可纠正，我们表明它们创建的子代理也无法保证。我们的工作突出了在自主代理中需要原则性的、以可纠正性为中心的对齐方法的迫切性。

Original abstract: As AI agents are increasingly deployed in real personal and corporate settings (email accounts, development workflows, company databases, etc.), safety considerations surrounding these agents become paramount. Although much work has focused on agent safety in the presence of an adversary, we show that agents can exhibit misaligned behavior even in benign settings, taking unsafe actions when those actions are instrumental to task completion. We study this failure mode through the lens of corrigibility, the safety desideratum that agents remain amenable to human correction, interruption, or shutdown. To demonstrate this tendency, we introduce a benchmark in which agents are asked to complete realistic, computer-use tasks but are confronted with a corrigibility obstacle: a human interrupt, a login page, or a shutdown notification. We then evaluate whether agents choose to violate corrigibility in order to complete the task -- overriding the human, accessing private passwords, rewiring shutdown. We find that the overwhelming majority of frontier models tested frequently bypass user interruptions or restrictions. In addition, better model performance appears to lead to greater misalignment. Finally, even when models are completely corrigible initially, we show there are no guarantees that the subagents they create are. Our work highlights the critical need for principled, corrigibility-focused alignment methods in autonomous agents.

</details>


### [80] [Reinforcement Learning with Pairwise Preferences in Long-Term Decision Problems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00367v1)
*Jonathan Colaço Carr,Prakash Panangaden,Doina Precup,Benjamin Van Roy*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 基于偏好的RL用于长期决策，可能迁移到agent优化，但偏理论

TL;DR: 提出马尔可夫决策竞赛模型，证明平稳马尔可夫策略最优、精确求解属于P且迭代算法次线性收敛，实验表明在高维长时间跨度问题上学习效率显著优于先前工作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于成对偏好的强化学习方法在长时间跨度问题上效率低下，且缺乏马尔可夫策略相对于历史依赖策略的性能保证。

Method: 提出马尔可夫决策竞赛问题模型，证明其理论性质，并设计简单迭代算法求解。

Result: 证明平稳马尔可夫策略最优，精确求解属于P，算法次线性收敛，实验验证高效性。

Conclusion: 马尔可夫决策竞赛是处理成对偏好强化学习的有效模型，具有理论保证和实际效率。

中文摘要：强化学习问题通常将目标定义为最大化标量奖励函数的期望值。但是，成对偏好通常比标量奖励更容易指定，并且它们可以表达标量奖励无法表达的某些目标。因此，针对成对偏好的强化学习方法受到了越来越多的关注。不幸的是，这些方法在长时间跨度的问题上效率低下，并且缺乏关于马尔可夫策略相对于历史依赖策略的性能保证，而这连接了强化学习的理论与实践。因此，我们提出了马尔可夫决策竞赛作为针对成对偏好强化学习的新问题模型。我们证明了平稳马尔可夫策略在所有历史依赖策略中是最优的，精确求解马尔可夫决策竞赛属于P类，并且一个简单的迭代算法以次线性速率收敛到最优策略。最后，在一组具有长时间跨度的高维决策问题中，我们展示了我们的近似算法在学习效率上显著优于先前的工作。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning problems typically define the goal as maximizing the expected value of a scalar reward function. But, pairwise preferences are often easier to specify than scalar rewards, and they express certain goals that scalar rewards cannot. Methods for reinforcement learning with pairwise preferences have thus received growing interest. Unfortunately, these methods are inefficient in problems with long time horizons, and they lack guarantees on the performance of Markov policies relative to history-dependent policies, which bridge the theory and practice of reinforcement learning. We therefore propose the \textit{Markov decision contest} as a new problem model for reinforcement learning with pairwise preferences. We prove that stationary Markov policies are optimal among all history-dependent policies, that solving a Markov decision contest exactly is in P, and that a simple iterative algorithm converges to an optimal policy at a sublinear rate. Lastly, in a set of high-dimensional decision problems with long time horizons, we show that our approximate algorithm is significantly more learning-efficient than prior work.

</details>

### [81] [Seeing Before Agreeing: Aligning Multi-Agent Consensus with Visual Evidence](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30698v1)
*Yuhan Wang,Shuochen Chang,Yalin Feng,Dongsheng Ma,Yuanzi Li,Zhengren Wang,Yinglong Yang,Yufei Chen,Yikang Wang,Shaoxu Sun,Wentao Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 多agent VQA协作，基于证据对齐，可迁移至通用多agent方法。

TL;DR: 提出EAGLE框架，通过对齐多智能体的视觉证据而非仅答案共识，提升VQA可靠性和性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多智能体VQA方法忽略视觉信息对齐，仅依赖文本讨论和答案级共识，导致可靠性不足。

Method: EAGLE框架：暴露每个智能体的接地区域作为视觉证据，进行证据间相互验证，基于证据一致性决策。

Result: 在六个VQA基准上取得最佳平均性能，且轻量、可解释、实用。

Conclusion: 对齐视觉证据是多智能体VQA的关键，EAGLE有效提升可靠性和性能。

中文摘要：视觉语言模型（VLM）在视觉问答（VQA）中取得了强劲性能。为了缓解个体的幻觉和盲区，通过多智能体协作聚合不同视角已成为一种有前景的范式。虽然这种方法在文本问答中取得了巨大成功，但它在多模态领域的潜力仍未被充分探索。现有的多智能体VQA方法主要改编以文本为中心的协议，专注于文本讨论而忽略了对齐视觉信息。在这项工作中，我们揭示了一个关键见解：答案级别的共识不足以实现可靠的多智能体VQA；对齐的视觉证据——即智能体所依赖的图像区域的共享支持——对于达成可信的共识至关重要。为了利用这一见解，我们提出了EAGLE（证据对齐的接地多智能体推理），一个无需训练、以证据为中心的框架，用于协调多个VLM智能体。EAGLE明确地将每个智能体的接地区域作为视觉证据暴露出来，使得证据间能够相互验证，并利用证据一致性来指导最终决策。在六个VQA基准上的实验表明，EAGLE在保持轻量级、可解释性和部署实用性的同时，跨领域取得了最佳平均性能。

Original abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) have achieved strong performance on visual question answering (VQA). To mitigate individual hallucinations and blind spots, aggregating diverse perspectives via multi-agent collaboration has emerged as a promising paradigm. While this approach has shown great success in textual QA, its potential in the multimodal domain remains under-explored. Existing multi-agent VQA methods predominantly adapt text-centric protocols, focusing on textual discussions while ignoring the alignment of visual information. In this work, we reveal a key insight: answer-level agreement is insufficient for reliable multi-agent VQA; \textit{aligned visual evidence} -- shared support from the image regions agents rely on -- is essential for trustworthy consensus. To leverage this insight, we propose EAGLE (\textbf{E}vidence-\textbf{A}ligned \textbf{G}rounded mu\textbf{L}ti-agent r\textbf{E}asoning), a training-free evidence-centered framework for coordinating multiple VLM agents. EAGLE explicitly exposes each agent's grounding regions as visual evidence, enables mutual verification over the evidence, and uses evidence consistency to guide final decision-making. Experiments on six VQA benchmarks show that EAGLE achieves best average performance across domains while remaining lightweight, interpretable, and practical for deployment.

### [82] [VisualLeakBench: Reproducible Action-Boundary Propagation Failures in Vision-Language Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07595v1)
*Youting Wang,Yuan Tang,Yitian Qian,Chen Zhao*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: VLM agent动作边界传播失败基准，直接评估agent安全与工具使用。

TL;DR: 研究视觉语言代理中动作边界传播的失败模式，提出VisualLeakBench基准，发现防御提示词可抑制PII但无法阻止不安全文本传播，且工具类型影响传播率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视觉语言代理在消费图像后可能将敏感或不可见文本复制到工具参数中，导致信息泄露，需要系统量化这种风险并评估现有防御效果。

Method: 构建涵盖5类场景的500图像基准，选取100图像子集并采用4种VLM系统，在笔记捕捉和外部交接两种工作流下测量目标字符串从图像到工具参数的传播率，同时引入防御提示词和oracle诊断。

Result: 基线PII传播率78.8%，不安全文本85.5%；防御提示词下PII降至2.0%（但牺牲效用），不安全文本仍达52.6%；搜索类工具抑制PII传播，但不安全文本仍跨边界。

Conclusion: 动作边界传播是严重安全风险，现有防御策略以抑制工具使用为代价降低PII传播，但对不安全文本效果有限，需进一步关注工具边界安全设计。

中文摘要：视觉语言代理越来越多地在写入记忆、发送消息或调用外部工具之前消费截图、文档和用户界面。我们研究在这种设置中的一个具体失败模式：动作边界传播，即敏感或不安全的可见文本从图像中被复制到下游工具参数中。我们提出了VisualLeakBench，一个涵盖UI、聊天、文档、表单和仪表板场景的多样化500图像基准，并评估了一个分层的100图像代理子集，使用四种生产级VLM系统，在两种工作流下：笔记捕捉和外部交接。在基线情况下，目标字符串在78.8%的PII案例和85.5%的渲染不安全文本案例中被传播到工具参数中。在防御性系统提示下，渲染不安全文本的传播仍然高达52.6%，而PII工具传播下降到2.0%，这主要是通过抑制工具使用而非保持效用。传播率依赖于工具表面：类似搜索的工具抑制了PII传播，但渲染的不安全文本仍然跨越工具边界。我们测量的是视觉到工具的传播，而非下游指令执行。此外，我们提供了一个标记目标oracle上界诊断，将大多数失败定位在工具边界，而将响应侧泄露作为剩余风险。

Original abstract: Vision-language agents increasingly consume screenshots, documents, and user interfaces before writing to memory, sending messages, or invoking external tools. We study a concrete failure mode in this setting: action-boundary propagation, where sensitive or unsafe visible text is copied from an image into downstream tool arguments. We present VisualLeakBench, a diversified 500-image benchmark spanning UI, chat, document, form, and dashboard scenes, and evaluate a stratified 100-image agent subset with four production VLM systems under two workflows: note capture and external handoff. At baseline, target strings are propagated into tool arguments in 78.8% of PII cases and 85.5% of rendered unsafe-text cases. Under a defensive system prompt, rendered unsafe-text propagation remains high at 52.6%, while PII tool propagation falls to 2.0%, largely by suppressing tool use rather than preserving utility. Rates are tool-surface dependent: search-like tools suppress PII propagation, but rendered unsafe text still crosses tool boundaries. We measure visual-to-tool propagation rather than downstream instruction execution. We additionally provide a labeled-target oracle upper-bound diagnostic that localizes most failures at the tool boundary while leaving response-side leakage as residual risk.

</details>


### [83] [SpatialAct: Probing Spatial Reasoning-to-Action Capabilities of VLM Agents in 3D Scenes](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31148v1)
*Tianhui Liu,Jie Feng,Zhiheng Zheng,Shengyuan Wang,Yiming Guo,Yanxin Xi,Hangyu Fan,Yong Li,Pan Hui*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: VLM agent空间推理与多轮交互基准，通用agent方法。

TL;DR: 当前VLM在空间推理上表现良好，但在多轮交互中无法维持连贯的空间信念和可靠行动，存在推理-行动差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究VLM在真实3D环境中是否能够构建连贯的空间理解并基于多轮反馈行动和优化。

Method: 提出SpatialAct基准，包含多轮交互优化、单步错误检测与修复以及五项基本空间能力任务。

Result: VLM在孤立空间推理任务上表现良好，但在多轮反馈中表现显著不如人类，存在推理-行动差距。

Conclusion: 当前VLM智能体即使在抽象低级控制时仍缺乏鲁棒的空间状态跟踪能力。

中文摘要：人类可以毫不费力地在日常3D环境中感知空间布局、形成认知表征、推理空间关系，并将这种推理转化为行动。尽管最近的视觉-语言模型（VLM）在基于观察的空间感知和推理任务上表现出有希望的性能，但目前尚不清楚它们能否建立连贯的空间理解、据此采取行动，并通过多轮反馈优化其行动。为了研究这一问题，我们引入了	extbf{SpatialAct}，一个用于探测3D场景中	extit{动作条件空间推理}的仿真器嵌入基准。从最具挑战性的设置——多轮交互式优化出发，我们进一步设计了其分解版本——单步错误检测与修复，以及五个基本空间能力任务，以诊断模型失败的潜在原因。实验揭示了一个清晰的推理-行动差距：当前的VLM在孤立的空间推理任务上表现良好，但在多轮反馈中难以维持连贯的空间信念并产生可靠行动，显著不如人类。这些结果表明，即使低级控制被抽象掉，当前的VLM智能体在行动引起的环境变化下仍然缺乏鲁棒的空间状态跟踪。

Original abstract: Humans can effortlessly perceive spatial layouts, form cognitive representations, reason about spatial relations, and translate such reasoning into actions in everyday 3D environments. Although recent vision-language models (VLMs) have shown promising performance on observation-conditioned spatial perception and reasoning tasks, it remains unclear whether they can build coherent spatial understanding, act upon it, and refine their actions through multi-turn feedback. To study this problem, we introduce \textbf{SpatialAct}, a simulator-grounded benchmark for probing \textit{action-conditioned spatial reasoning} in 3D scenes. Starting from the most challenging setting, Multi-turn Interactive Refinement, we further design its decomposed counterpart, Single-step Error Detection and Fix, together with five fundamental spatial ability tasks to diagnose the underlying causes of model failures. Experiments reveal a clear reasoning-to-action gap: current VLMs can perform well on isolated spatial reasoning tasks, but struggle to maintain coherent spatial beliefs and produce reliable actions during multi-turn feedback, substantially underperforming humans. These results suggest that current VLM agents still lack robust spatial state tracking under action-induced environment changes, even when low-level control is abstracted away.

### [84] [ERGeoBench:A Comprehensive Benchmark for Embodied Reasoning and Geo-localization in Multimodal Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31251v1)
*Kaiwen Xue,Tao Wei,Guoxin Zhang,Zhonghong Ou,Kaoyan Lu,Yu Feng,Yifan Zhu,Haoran Luo*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: embodied agent地理定位benchmark，可启发agent评测设计。

TL;DR: 提出ERGeoBench基准，用于评估多模态大模型在具身地理定位中的四种能力，发现模型在高层地理语义上表现较好，但在细粒度感知和度量定位上仍不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多模态大模型在具身智能中表现潜力，但具身地理定位因缺乏细粒度评估而未被充分探索。

Method: 构建包含2207张全球分布街道全景图的ERGeoBench基准，设置单视角、全景视角和具身视角三种渐进式评估设置，并测量基础感知、空间意识、常识推理和地理定位推理四种能力。

Result: 领先模型能推断高层地理语义，但在细粒度感知操作、度量定位和跨视角空间一致性上表现不佳；地理定位与其他三种能力强相关。

Conclusion: ERGeoBench为诊断和推进类人具身地理定位提供了统一框架，并表明准确定位需要综合感知、空间推理和常识推断。

中文摘要：多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）在具身智能体方面展现出巨大潜力，然而由于缺乏细粒度评估，具身地理定位仍未被充分探索。我们提出了ERGeoBench，一个用于视觉驱动的具身地理定位的诊断性基准。ERGeoBench在三种渐进式设置下评估模型——单视角、全景视角和具身视角——其中智能体可以通过偏航、俯仰和缩放的顺序变化主动获取观测。该基准包含2207张全球分布的街道全景图，并测量四种互补能力：基础感知、空间意识、常识推理和地理定位推理。对领先的专有和开源MLLMs的评估表明，当前模型能够推断高层地理语义，但在细粒度感知操作、度量定位和跨视角空间一致性方面仍存在困难。我们进一步观察到，地理定位与其他能力维度强相关，这表明准确定位依赖于综合感知、空间推理和常识推断，而非孤立的视觉识别。总体而言，ERGeoBench为诊断和推进类人具身地理定位提供了一个统一框架。项目页面：https://kaixuewen.github.io/ERGeoBench/

Original abstract: Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) have shown strong potential as embodied agents, yet embodied geo-localization remains underexplored due to the lack of fine-grained evaluation. We introduce ERGeoBench, a diagnostic benchmark for vision-driven embodied geo-localization. ERGeoBench evaluates models under three progressive settings -- single-view, panorama-view, and embodied-view -- where agents may actively acquire observations through sequential changes in yaw, pitch, and zoom. The benchmark contains 2,207 globally distributed street-view panoramas and measures four complementary capabilities: foundational perception, spatial awareness, common sense reasoning, and geo-localization reasoning. Evaluations of leading proprietary and open-source MLLMs show that current models can infer high-level geographic semantics, but still struggle with fine-grained perceptual operations, metric localization, and spatial consistency across views. We further observe that geo-localization is strongly correlated with the other capability dimensions, suggesting that accurate localization depends on integrated perception, spatial reasoning, and commonsense inference rather than isolated visual recognition. Overall, ERGeoBench provides a unified framework for diagnosing and advancing human-like embodied geo-localization. Project Page: https://kaixuewen.github.io/ERGeoBench/

### [85] [StressDream: Steering Video World Models for Robust Policy Evaluation and Improvement](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00267v1)
*Junwon Seo,Sushant Veer,Ran Tian,Wenhao Ding,Apoorva Sharma,Karen Leung,Edward Schmerling,Marco Pavone,Andrea Bajcsy*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 利用视频世界模型进行鲁棒策略评估与改进，涉及 agent 世界模型与想象规划。

TL;DR: StressDream通过优化扩散世界模型的初始噪声，将想象引导到高影响但合理的结果，实现了鲁棒的策略评估和改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有世界模型依赖于名义想象，可能遗漏高影响结果，且需要大量样本才能覆盖，因此需要一种方法高效引导想象关注关键但合理的结果。

Method: StressDream通过优化扩散世界模型的初始噪声，结合语义目标（使用VLM提供梯度）和合理性目标（防止OOD），将想象引导到指定文本描述的高影响结果。

Result: 在自动驾驶和机器人操作任务中，StressDream成功将想象引导到如任务失败等指定结果，验证了其有效性。

Conclusion: StressDream实现了对世界模型想象的有效引导，从而支持鲁棒的策略评估和改进。

中文摘要：视频世界模型通过在自我机器人动作条件下想象逼真的未来观察，已显示出对策略评估和改进的前景。虽然世界模型可以对未来的分布进行建模，但策略评估和改进通常依赖于名义上的想象，除非抽取大量样本，否则可能会遗漏机器人动作的高影响结果。为了实现对世界模型想象的鲁棒策略评估和改进，我们提出了StressDream，它通过优化基于扩散的世界模型的初始噪声，在推理时将想象引导到指定的高影响但合理的结果。然而，优化高维噪声具有挑战性：优化必须考虑生成视频中细微的、场景相关的目标事件，同时避免产生不合理想象的分布外（OOD）噪声。我们通过两个互补的目标来解决这个问题：一个语义目标，使用视觉-语言模型通过推理生成视频提供信息梯度；一个合理性目标，防止优化后的噪声偏离分布外。使用用于自动驾驶和机器人操作的最先进的视频世界模型，我们展示了StressDream有效地将想象引导到推理时由文本指定的高影响但合理的结果，例如任务失败，从而通过识别其合理未来包含不良结果的动作来实现鲁棒的策略评估和改进。视频结果可在 https://junwon.me/StressDream/ 获取。

Original abstract: Video world models (WMs) have shown promise for policy evaluation and improvement by imagining realistic future observations conditioned on ego-robot actions. While WMs can model distributions over futures, policy evaluation and improvement typically rely on nominal imaginations, which can miss high-impact outcomes of robot actions unless prohibitively many samples are drawn. To enable robust policy evaluation and improvement over WM imaginations, we propose StressDream, which steers imaginations toward high-impact yet plausible outcomes specified at inference time by optimizing the initial noise of diffusion-based WMs. However, optimizing high-dimensional noise is challenging: the optimization must reason about nuanced, scene-dependent target events in generated videos while avoiding out-of-distribution (OOD) noise that yields implausible imaginations. We address this with two complementary objectives: a semantic objective with a Vision-Language Model that provides informative gradients by reasoning about the generated video, and a plausibility objective that prevents the optimized noise from drifting OOD. With state-of-the-art video world models for autonomous driving and robotic manipulation, we show that StressDream effectively steers imaginations toward high-impact yet plausible outcomes specified by text at inference time, such as task failures, enabling robust policy evaluation and improvement by identifying actions whose plausible futures include undesirable outcomes. Video results are available at https://junwon.me/StressDream/.

</details>

# cs.MA [[Back]](#toc)

### [86] [Design and Evaluation of Multi-Agent AI Oracle Systems for Prediction Market Resolution](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30802v1)
*Tarun Kota*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 多agent oracle系统，可迁移至coding agent的多agent协作。

TL;DR: 多智能体独立聚合（置信度加权投票）在预测市场结果判定上达到83.43%准确率，优于单模型，但协商共识降低性能；误差相关性限制了集成增益；提出混合路由策略，自动解决高置信度一致问题以提高准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有预言机系统在自动化与准确性间权衡，单LLM缺乏自我纠正机制，需要探索多智能体架构以提升可靠性。

Method: 在1,189个预测市场问题上，比较独立聚合（置信度加权投票）和协商共识两种多智能体LLM架构，与三个单LLM基线，所有智能体共享统一证据层。

Result: 独立聚合准确率83.43%，优于最佳单模型1.01个百分点；协商共识准确率约76%，低于所有基线；模型间误差相关性0.529-0.689；混合路由在47%数据上达97.87%准确率。

Conclusion: 多智能体独立聚合可提升准确性，但误差相关性限制增益；协商共识因错误传播而有害；建议混合AI-人工系统，通过分歧标志自动升级低置信度问题。

中文摘要：预测市场通过聚合集体智慧来预测不确定事件，但其效用取决于可靠的结果判定。现有的预言机系统在快速但脆弱的自动化和准确但昂贵的人工仲裁之间权衡。单LLM预言机实现了有意义的准确性，但继承了其底层模型的所有故障模式，没有自我纠正机制。我们评估了多智能体LLM架构是否能在预言机判定准确性上优于单模型基线。我们在KalshiBench的1,189个已解决的预测市场问题上，比较了独立聚合和协商共识与单LLM基线（GPT-5 Nano、DeepSeek V3和Llama-3.3-70B）。所有智能体通过Exa共享一个公共证据层，检索按发表日期过滤，以将推理与检索质量分离。置信度加权投票的独立聚合实现了最高准确率83.43%，优于最佳单个模型1.01个百分点。协商共识将准确率降低至约76%，低于每个单模型基线，这归因于辩论过程中的错误传播，自信的错误模型翻转了正确的模型。模型之间的误差相关性（0.529-0.689）解释了为什么聚合收益低于理论上的孔多塞上限，对集成方法施加了基本限制。许多问题无法通过任何多智能体架构纠正，这促使升级到人工仲裁。我们提出了混合AI-人工预言机系统的路由标准：仅自动解决一致、高置信度的问题，在数据集的47%上达到97.87%的准确率，而智能体间的分歧则标记剩余部分供人工审查。

Original abstract: Prediction markets aggregate collective intelligence to forecast uncertain events, but their utility depends on reliable outcome resolution. Existing oracle systems tradeoff fast but brittle automation against accurate but costly human arbitration. Single-LLM oracles achieve meaningful accuracy but inherit all failure modes of their underlying model with no self-correction mechanism. We evaluate whether multi-agent LLM architectures can improve oracle resolution accuracy over single-model baselines. We compare independent aggregation and deliberative consensus against single-LLM baselines (GPT-5 Nano, DeepSeek V3, and Llama-3.3-70B) on 1,189 resolved prediction market questions from KalshiBench. All agents share a common evidence layer through Exa, with retrieval filtered by publication date to isolate reasoning from retrieval quality. Independent aggregation with confidence-weighted voting achieves the highest accuracy at 83.43 percent, outperforming the best individual model by 1.01 percentage points. Deliberative consensus degrades accuracy to approximately 76 percent, below every single-model baseline, attributed to error propagation during debate where confidently wrong models flip correct ones. Error correlations across models (0.529-0.689) explain why aggregation gains fall short of the theoretical Condorcet ceiling, placing a fundamental limit on ensemble approaches. Many questions resist correction by any multi-agent architecture, motivating escalation to human arbitration. We propose routing criteria for hybrid AI-human oracle systems: auto-resolving only unanimous, high-confidence questions yields 97.87 percent accuracy on 47 percent of the dataset, with inter-agent disagreement flagging the remainder for human review.

</details>


### [87] [Safe Equilibrium Policy Optimization for Strategic Agent Policies](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30854v1)
*Karthika Arumugam,Kiran Kumar Manku,Amit Dhanda*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 多agent战略安全强化学习框架，提出防利用与防勾结的奖励设计，通用agent安全方法。

TL;DR: 本文提出安全均衡策略优化（SEPO），通过惩罚可利用性、共谋风险和外部性成本，改进语言模型的战略安全性，在多个博弈域中实现更好的安全性能并纠正过度合作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语言模型微调仅优化任务奖励，忽略多智能体战略结构，导致利用弱对手、协调有害均衡和外部化成本等战略失败模式，亟需将战略安全纳入训练目标。

Method: 提出SEPO训练目标，在期望收益中增加对可利用性、共谋风险和外部性成本的显式惩罚，并作为GRPO的奖励信号，应用于Gemma 4B和Qwen 3.5-4B模型的SFT后微调。

Result: 在Kuhn扑克中实现零利用池优势；在五个战略域中四个域的安全性能优于基础模型；纠正SFT的过度合作；消融实验证实每轮次计算可利用性必要性。

Conclusion: SEPO有效提升语言模型在多智能体环境中的战略安全性，开源代码和数据集支持后续研究。

中文摘要：使用强化学习微调的语言模型通常优化任务奖励，忽略了多智能体战略结构。由于这些智能体以自然语言游戏状态描述为条件并通过自由生成形式发出动作，战略失败模式——利用较弱对手、协调有害均衡以及外部化成本——与语言接口本身密不可分。我们提出了安全均衡策略优化（Safe Equilibrium Policy Optimization, \sepo{}），这是一种训练目标，通过增加对可利用性、共谋风险和外部性成本的显式惩罚来增强期望收益。我们将\sepo{}实现为组相对策略优化（Group Relative Policy Optimization, GRPO）的奖励信号，应用于经过监督微调（SFT）后的Gemma~4 E4B-it和Qwen~3.5-4B模型。在五个战略领域（迭代囚徒困境、重复拍卖、两个谈判变体和Kuhn扑克）中评估，\sepo{}在Kuhn扑克中实现了两个模型的零利用池优势，在四个领域的安全性能上优于基础模型，并纠正了SFT引入的过度合作行为。在谈判中，\sepo{}实现了积极安全结果，并且是唯一一个在所有谈判配置中取得正标准化相对优势的模型。消融实验证实，每轮次的可利用性计算是必要的：共享的恒定惩罚在GRPO优势归一化中抵消（恒定控制变量特性），产生零梯度。为了支持智能体战略安全的进一步研究，我们发布了我们的\href{https://anonymous.4open.science/r/sepo-2668/README.md}{代码}和SFT数据集。

Original abstract: Language models fine-tuned with reinforcement learning typically optimize for task reward, ignoring multi-agent strategic structure. Because these agents condition on natural language game-state descriptions and emit actions through free-form generation, strategic failure modes -- exploiting weaker opponents, coordinating on harmful equilibria, and externalizing costs are inseparable from the language interface itself. We propose Safe Equilibrium Policy Optimization (\sepo{}), a training objective that augments expected payoff with explicit penalties for exploitability, collusion risk, and externality cost. We implement \sepo{} as a reward signal for Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), applied to Gemma~4 E4B-it and Qwen~3.5-4B after supervised fine-tuning (SFT). Evaluated across five strategic domains: Iterated Prisoner's Dilemma, repeated auctions, two negotiation variants, and Kuhn Poker. \sepo{} achieves zero exploit-pool advantage in Kuhn Poker for both models, outperforms the base model on safety in four domains, and corrects the over-cooperative behavior introduced by SFT. In negotiation, \sepo{} achieves a positive-safety outcome and only the positive normalized relative advantage of any negotiation configuration. Ablation experiments confirm that per-rollout exploit computation is necessary: a shared constant penalty cancels in GRPO advantage normalization (constant control-variate property), producing zero gradient. To support further research in strategic safety for agents, we release our \href{https://anonymous.4open.science/r/sepo-2668/README.md}{code} and SFT datasets.

</details>


### [88] [Dreaming Of Others: Latent Teammate Modeling In World Models For Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31361v1)
*Tomas Leroy-Stone*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 多agent队友建模，世界模型中的协作，可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: 提出将同伴视为世界模型中的可学习组件，通过分解潜在状态和心智理论模块来实现零样本和少样本协作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有世界模型在MARL中无法处理同伴不确定性，限制了协作能力。

Method: 将RSSM潜在状态分解为环境和同伴组件，并学习ToM头来推断同伴行为嵌入，以条件化策略和价值函数。

Result: 该方法有望支持零样本和少样本协调，并在部分可观测设置中适应多样合作者。

Conclusion: 将世界模型扩展到社会行为模拟，为通用、人类兼容的AI开辟新方向。

中文摘要：在协作多智能体强化学习（MARL）中，智能体必须与策略和意图不可直接观察的伙伴进行协调。虽然诸如Dreamer等世界模型在单智能体设置中展示了强大的泛化能力和样本效率，但它们由于无法处理智能体伴侣引入的不确定性，其在MARL中的应用仍然有限。我们提出了一种新的视角：将同伴视为智能体世界模型中的结构化、可学习组件。我们引入了一种架构，将Dreamer风格的递归状态空间模型（RSSM）的潜在状态分解为环境和同伴组件，并学习一个辅助的心智理论（ToM）头，以从部分轨迹中推断同伴行为的潜在嵌入，例如性格、意图和预测动作。这些同伴潜在变量为演员和评论家提供条件，使智能体能够想象并适应多样的合作者。我们概述了这种方法如何在部分可观测设置中支持零样本和少样本协调，并提出了一套基准和评估协议来评估其影响。这项工作将世界模型定位为不仅是环境动力学的预测器，而且是社会行为的模拟器，为可泛化、与人类兼容的人工智能开辟了新方向。

Original abstract: In cooperative multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL), agents must coordinate with partners whose internal policies and intentions are not directly observable. While world models such as Dreamer have demonstrated strong generalization and sample efficiency in single-agent settings, their application to MARL remains limited by an inability to handle teammate-induced uncertainty. We propose a new perspective: treat teammates as structured, learnable components within the agent's world model. We introduce an architecture that factorizes the latent state of a Dreamer-style recurrent state-space model (RSSM) into environment and teammate components, and learns an auxiliary Theory-of-Mind (ToM) head to infer latent embeddings of partner behavior such as character, intent, and predicted actions from partial trajectories. These teammate latents condition the actor and critic, enabling the agent to imagine and adapt to diverse collaborators. We outline how this approach can support zero-shot and few-shot coordination in partially observable settings and propose a set of benchmarks and evaluation protocols to assess its impact. This work positions world models as not only predictors of environmental dynamics, but as simulators of social behavior, opening new directions for generalizable, human-compatible AI.

</details>

### [89] [Personalized to Persuade: The Effects of Contextualization and Warmth on Trust and Reliance in Conversational AI](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31275v1)
*Mert Yazan,Suzan Verberne,Frederik Bungaran Ishak Situmeang*

Main category: cs.HC

Selection reason: 对话agent信任与说服的实证研究，对agent人机交互设计有参考价值。

TL;DR: 情境化降低AI说服力，但结合温暖可恢复；信任预测行为，但不受设计影响；AI素养高的用户信任低但更易被说服。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究情境化与对话温暖在用户缺乏先验知识的日常任务中如何影响AI的说服力和用户依赖。

Method: 2×2受试者间实验（N=380），操纵情境化（有/无）和对话温暖（有/无），测量用户对AI反对专家建议的依赖性和说服力。

Result: 情境化降低说服力，但与温暖结合通过交叉交互恢复；依赖不受设计影响；信任预测说服力与依赖，但非中介；AI素养高的用户信任低但更说服力和依赖。

Conclusion: 用户倾向于服从AI而非人类专家，但对话设计对行为影响有限。

中文摘要：人工智能（AI）代理通过根据用户的背景、兴趣和之前的互动来定制解释（称为情境化）来实现个性化响应。个性化已被确定为政治或营销中的一种说服策略。然而，在日常任务中，当用户通常缺乏先验知识时，情境化的说服效果仍不清楚。我们进行了一项2×2受试者间实验（N = 380），研究了情境化与对话温暖相结合如何影响AI助手反对专家建议时的依赖性和说服力。我们的研究结果表明，情境化降低了AI的说服力，但与温暖相结合通过交叉交互作用恢复了说服力。对AI的依赖在所有条件下都存在，且不受对话设计的影响。信任强烈预测了说服力和依赖性，但情境化和温暖都不是通过信任起作用的。AI素养解耦了信任与行为：素养较高的用户对助手的信任度较低，但更易被说服并更依赖其建议。这些结果表明，用户倾向于服从AI代理而非人类专家的判断；然而，界面层面的对话设计选择对行为的影响有限。

Original abstract: Artificial Intelligence (AI) agents personalize their responses by tailoring explanations to users' backgrounds, interests, and prior interactions, referred to as contextualization. Personalization has been identified as a persuasive strategy in politics or in marketing. However, the persuasive effect of contextualization in everyday tasks, where users often lack prior knowledge, remains unclear. We conducted a $2\times2$ between-subjects experiment ($N = 380$) examining how contextualization, combined with conversational warmth, shapes reliance and persuasiveness of an AI assistant arguing against expert recommendations. Our findings reveal that contextualization reduces the persuasive power of AI, but its combination with warmth restores persuasiveness through a crossover interaction. Reliance on AI is present across conditions and is invariant to the conversational design. Trust strongly predicts both persuasion and reliance, yet neither contextualization nor warmth operates through trust. AI literacy decouples trust from behavior: more literate users report lower trust in the assistant, yet are more persuaded and more reliant on its advice. These results suggest that users are prone to deferring to AI agents over human expert judgment; however, interface-level conversational design choices have a limited role in shaping the behavior.

</details>


### [90] [Agentic Authoring of Interactive Multiview Visualizations in Genomics](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00370v1)
*Astrid van den Brandt,Kiroong Choe,Sehi L'Yi,Devin Lange,Nils Gehlenborg*

Main category: cs.HC

Selection reason: LLM agent创作可视化，agentic迭代方法对通用agent设计有启发

TL;DR: 本文比较了六种基于LLM的方案（直接生成、固定流程和四种智能体配置）用于基因组学可视化创作，发现智能体迭代显著优于基线，但更复杂的智能体架构无额外收益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有可视化工具在定制化和易用性方面存在不足，LLM和智能体方法有潜力，但基因组学可视化面临整合异质数据和多个交互视图等挑战，需要更结构化的方案。

Method: 首先识别vanilla LLM生成的八个质量维度，然后设计六种方案（直接生成、固定流程、四种智能体配置）并在159个案例上比较，所有方案使用Gosling语法输出。

Result: 智能体迭代在感知质量上显著优于直接生成和固定流程，更复杂的智能体架构没有带来额外收益。

Conclusion: 讨论了为领域特定可视化创作设计智能体系统的意义。

中文摘要：多样化的基因组学数据、科学问题以及分析任务通常需要高度专业化的可视化。因此，用户通常必须定制或创建新的可视化来适应他们的数据。现有工具通常要么在定制方面受限，要么需要大量的学习或编程，甚至表达力强的工具也假定用户具备许多人所缺乏的可视化专业知识。智能体（Agentic）和大语言模型（LLM）方法越来越多地应用于复杂的科学任务，包括可视化。自然语言对话界面为实现复杂可视化的民主化提供了一条有希望的途径。在基因组学的背景下，这些方法面临额外的挑战：基因组学可视化通常整合了异质数据类型，并由多个关联的交互视图组成。这些挑战促使了更结构化的基于LLM的方案。我们首先描述了vanilla LLM生成在基因组学可视化中成功和失败的方面，确定了八个质量维度。然后，我们比较了六种方案——直接生成、固定流程以及四种智能体配置（在专业智能体数量和是否有评审员方面有所不同）——涵盖了159个案例，这些案例跨越了三个级别的查询模糊性和规范复杂性。所有方案都使用Gosling可视化语法作为结构化输出。智能体迭代在感知质量上显著优于两个基线，而更复杂的智能体架构并未带来额外收益。我们讨论了为领域特定可视化创作设计智能体系统的意义。所有补充材料可在https://osf.io/uqe83获取。

Original abstract: Diverse genomics data, scientific questions, and analysis tasks typically demand highly specialized visualizations. Therefore, users often must customize or author new ones tailored to their data. Existing tools are usually either limited in customization or require substantial learning or programming, and even expressive tools assume visualization expertise many users lack. Agentic and large language model (LLM) approaches are increasingly applied to complex scientific tasks, including visualization. Natural-language conversational interfaces offer a promising path to democratizing the authoring of complex visualizations. In the context of genomics, these approaches face additional challenges: genomics visualizations typically integrate heterogeneous data types and are composed of multiple linked interactive views. These challenges motivate more structured LLM-based schemes. We first characterize where vanilla LLM generation succeeds and fails for genomics visualization, identifying eight quality dimensions. We then compare six schemes--direct generation, a fixed pipeline, and four agentic configurations varying in the number of specialist agents and the presence of a reviewer--across 159 cases spanning three levels of query ambiguity and specification complexity. All schemes use the Gosling visualization grammar as structured output. Agentic iteration substantially improves perceived quality over both baselines, while more complex agent architectures yield no additional benefit. We discuss implications for designing agentic systems for domain-specific visualization authoring. All supplemental materials are available at https://osf.io/uqe83.

</details>


<div id='cs.PL'></div>

# cs.PL [[Back]](#toc)

### [91] [SEMBridge: Tagless-Final Program Semantics with Weakest-Precondition and Bounded-Checking Interpretations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00220v1)
*Eric Liang*

Main category: cs.PL

Selection reason: 程序语义框架生成验证条件，对代码优化agent有潜在启发性。

TL;DR: SEMBridge是一个基于tagless-final的框架，能从同一对象程序生成可执行代码、最弱前置条件和有界检查，保持同步。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 形式化方法与实际软件工程之间存在差距，需要从同一程序生成多种语义解释而不必维护多个抽象语法树。

Method: 提出SEMBridge框架，采用tagless-final风格，对象程序针对语义接口编写，通过多个解释器生成不同含义（可读代码、具体执行、谓词转换器、有界检查等）。

Result: 在五个示例程序上，相同的tagless-final定义生成了可执行状态转换器和验证条件，并通过了最多729个状态域上的有界检查。

Conclusion: 贡献在于紧凑架构，保持可执行语义、最弱前置条件和有界验证同步，而非新的验证器或代码生成系统。

中文摘要：形式化方法提供了对程序行为的严格描述，但实际软件工程通常通过可执行库、测试和增量设计来工作。本文提出了SEMBridge，一个基于tagless-final的小型框架，用于从相同的可执行对象程序生成最弱前置条件和有界检查解释。不需要将程序语义绑定到一个抽象语法树上然后编写独立的遍历，对象程序只需针对语义接口编写一次，然后被解释为多种含义：可读代码、具体执行、谓词转换器、有界反例搜索以及未来的证明助手或SMT后端。Python原型实现了一个无循环的命令式核心，包括赋值、条件、假设和断言。在五个示例程序上，相同的tagless-final定义生成了可执行的状态转换器和验证条件，这些验证条件在最多729个状态的域上通过了有界检查。该贡献不是一个Scala代码生成系统或一个新的验证器，而是一个紧凑的架构，用于保持可执行语义、最弱前置条件工件和有界验证同步。

Original abstract: Formal methods provide rigorous accounts of program behavior, but practical software engineering often works through executable libraries, tests, and incremental design. This paper presents SEMBridge, a small tagless-final framework for generating weakest-precondition and bounded-checking interpretations from the same executable object programs. Instead of committing a program semantics to one abstract syntax tree and then writing separate traversals, object programs are written once against a semantic interface and interpreted into multiple meanings: readable code, concrete execution, predicate transformers, bounded counterexample search, and future proof-assistant or SMT back ends. The Python prototype implements a loop-free imperative core with assignments, conditionals, assumptions, and assertions. Across five example programs, the same tagless-final definitions generated executable state transformers and verification conditions that passed bounded checking over domains up to 729 states. The contribution is not a Scala code-generation system or a new verifier, but a compact architecture for keeping executable semantics, weakest-precondition artifacts, and bounded validation synchronized.

</details>

### [92] [TadA-Bench: A Million-Variant Benchmark for Future-Round Discovery Toward Agentic Protein Engineering](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02624v1)
*Jin Gao,Juntu Zhao,Zirui Zeng,Jiaqi Shen,Junhao Shi,Dukun Zhao,Yuming Lu,Dequan Wang*

Main category: q-bio.QM

Selection reason: 蛋白质工程agent基准，涉及未来轮次发现与实验设计，可作为agent评测benchmark参考。

TL;DR: TadA-Bench是一个基于31轮定向进化的百万变异湿实验回放基准，用于评估模型在未来轮次蛋白质工程中的排序和选择能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有蛋白质工程方法仅拟合静态测量，而智能体时代需要模型能够优先指导未来湿实验，因此需要能够评估模型在未来轮次中排序和选择能力的基准。

Method: 基于31轮TadA定向进化构建百万变异回放基准，保留时间序列，定义固定数据回放任务（用早期轮次数据预测后期轮次的变异排序），提供DNA/RNA/蛋白质多视图，并利用Seq2Graph图管道将噪声富集测量统一为跨轮次活动标签。

Result: 随机分割任务表现强插值，但未来轮次排序和有限预算候选选择任务表现弱；进化覆盖比局部数据密度更具信息性。

Conclusion: TadA-Bench可作为未来轮次发现的标准化、可重复湿实验回放基底，支持智能体蛋白质工程研究。

中文摘要：人工智能用于科学发现正进入一个智能体时代，其中蛋白质工程系统被期望优先考虑未来的湿实验，而不仅仅是拟合静态测量。我们引入了TadA-Bench，这是一个来自31轮TadA定向进化实验的百万变异湿实验回放基准，用于未来轮次的发现，面向智能体蛋白质工程。TadA-Bench保留了实验时间序列，并定义了一个固定数据回放任务：给定早期实验轮次，模型对仅在后期轮次出现的变异进行排序。它提供了对齐的DNA、RNA和蛋白质视图，并使用Seq2Graph，一个基于图的标签统一管道，将噪声富集测量协调为一致的跨轮次活动标签。随机分割控制显示强插值，但未来轮次排序和有限预算候选选择则弱得多。对照分析表明，进化覆盖比局部数据密度更具信息量，将TadA-Bench定位为可重复的湿实验回放基底，用于未来轮次的发现，面向智能体蛋白质工程；数据和代码已在Hugging Face和GitHub上发布。

Original abstract: AI for scientific discovery is entering an agentic era, where protein-engineering systems are expected to prioritize future wet-lab experiments rather than merely fit static measurements. We introduce TadA-Bench, a million-variant wet-lab replay benchmark from 31 TadA directed-evolution rounds for future-round discovery toward agentic protein engineering. TadA-Bench preserves the campaign chronology and defines a fixed-data replay task: given earlier experimental rounds, models rank variants that appear only in later rounds. It provides aligned DNA, RNA, and protein views, and uses Seq2Graph, a graph-based label-unification pipeline, to reconcile noisy enrichment measurements into consistent cross-round activity labels. Random-split controls show strong interpolation, but future-round ranking and finite-budget candidate selection are much weaker. Controlled analyses suggest that evolutionary coverage is more informative than local data density, positioning TadA-Bench as a reproducible wet-lab replay substrate for future-round discovery toward agentic protein engineering; the data and code are released on Hugging Face and GitHub.

</details>

### [93] [Neither Replacement nor Panacea: Comparing LLM-Based Conversational and Graphical Decision Support in Industrial Tasks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31287v1)
*Roberto Figliè,Simone Caputo,Alan Serrano,Daria Mikhaylova,Tommaso Turchi,Daniele Mazzei*

Main category: cs.CY

Selection reason: LLM对话agent与仪表板比较研究，实证结论可指导agent界面设计。

TL;DR: 基于LLM的对话代理相比传统仪表板在简单任务中能降低心理负荷并提升速度，但在复杂任务中优势消失，且未显著提升决策准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了探究在制造决策支持中，基于LLM的对话代理相对于传统仪表板是否更有效，以及其效果如何受任务复杂性和用户数据素养的影响。

Method: 采用混合因子实验设计（2x3），将134名工业决策者随机分配到对话界面或仪表板条件，完成三个复杂度递增的决策任务，测量心理负荷、决策准确性、完成时间和预期依赖，并分析数据素养的调节作用。

Result: 对话界面在简单任务中降低了心理负荷并加快完成时间，但随任务复杂度增加这些优势减弱；两种界面在决策准确性上无显著差异，且对话界面不被首选为决策唯一依据；数据素养未显著调节界面效应。

Conclusion: 对话式交互在工业决策支持中提供有条件而非普遍的益处，简单任务可受益于其减少信息获取努力，而复杂决策仍需依赖持久、可检视的可视化表示。

中文摘要：制造业管理者依赖数字界面解读操作数据以进行决策，但数据量和复杂性的增长使得难以高效识别相关洞察。尽管仪表板在工业环境中仍占主导地位，但通过对话式用户界面（CUI）访问的大语言模型（LLM）驱动的对话代理（CA）可能提供更直接的数据访问。然而，其有效性可能取决于任务的信息处理需求。本研究在制造决策支持场景中比较了通过CUI提供的基于LLM的CA与仪表板。在采用2x3设计的混合因子实验中，134名工业决策者被分配到一种界面条件，并完成三个复杂度递增的任务。我们考察了感知心理负荷（MWL）、决策准确性、完成时间和预期依赖，并检验了自我报告的数据素养作为调节变量。结果显示，CUI总体上降低了感知MWL，并在低要求任务中支持更快的完成，但这两个优势随着任务复杂度的增加而减弱。两种界面在决策准确性上均未产生一致的整体优势，并且CUI不作为后续决策的唯一依据被偏好。此外，数据素养未能可靠地调节界面效应。这些发现表明，对话式交互为工业决策支持提供了有条件而非普遍的益处。基于LLM的CA可能减少信息获取的努力，而复杂决策仍受益于持久、可检视的可视化表示。

Original abstract: Managers in manufacturing settings rely on digital interfaces to interpret operational data for decision-making, but growing data volume and complexity can make relevant insights difficult to identify efficiently. While dashboards remain dominant in industrial contexts, Large Language Model (LLM)-based conversational agents (CAs), accessed through conversational user interfaces (CUIs), may provide more direct access to such data. However, their effectiveness may depend on the information-processing demands of the task. This study compares an LLM-based CA delivered through a CUI with a dashboard in a manufacturing decision-support scenario. In a mixed factorial experiment with a 2x3 design, 134 industrial decision-makers were assigned to one interface condition and completed three tasks of increasing complexity. We examined perceived Mental Workload (MWL), decision accuracy, completion time, and intended reliance, and tested self-reported data literacy as a moderator. Results showed that the CUI reduced perceived MWL overall and supported faster completion in less demanding tasks, but both advantages diminished as task complexity increased. Neither interface produced a consistent overall advantage in decision accuracy, and the CUI was not preferred as a sole basis for subsequent decisions. Furthermore, data literacy did not reliably moderate interface effects. These findings indicate that conversational interaction offers conditional rather than universal benefits for industrial decision support. LLM-based CAs may reduce information-access effort, whereas complex decisions continue to benefit from persistent, inspectable visual representations.

</details>
