### [94] [Sophrosyne: Agentic Exploration of Relational Data Systems Needs Moderation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30862v1)
*Madhav Jivrajani,Ramnatthan Alagappan,Aishwarya Ganesan*

Main category: cs.DB

Selection reason: Text2SQL agent过度探索问题，提出引导指令减少无效探索，直接关系到coding agent工具使用。

TL;DR: 本文研究Text2SQL代理在数据系统API表面上的探索效率与准确性权衡，发现细粒度API导致过度探索和准确率下降，提出Sophrosyne系统通过指令引导探索，显著减少过度探索并提升准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Text2SQL代理在使用细粒度API时过度探索不相关模式元素，导致SQL生成不准确，需要一种方法在保证探索效率的同时提升准确性。

Method: 提出Sophrosyne数据系统环境，通过在API响应中增强指令来引导代理的探索过程，抑制过度探索。

Result: 初步实验显示，指令使过度探索减少4.6倍，准确率提升高达12.4%（约4个百分点）。

Conclusion: 抑制过度探索是有效利用API表面的关键，Sophrosyne通过指令引导能够兼顾探索成本与SQL生成准确性。

中文摘要：由LLM驱动的Text2SQL代理通过工具调用探索数据系统来制定查询，从而将自然语言意图转化为SQL。然而，为了确保安全和范围访问，数据系统构建具有明确API表面的环境。我们研究并将当今暴露的这些API分类为粗粒度或细粒度，并指出在两者之间选择存在成本效益的探索和准确的SQL生成之间的根本权衡。大多数数据系统暴露细粒度API，但这却无意中使代理处于不利地位：它们过度探索，将不相关的模式元素纳入查询制定中，并产生不准确的结果。我们认为抑制过度探索是有效利用这些API表面的关键，并提出了Sophrosyne，一种数据系统环境，通过指令来增强API响应，指导代理的探索过程。初步结果显示，指令将过度探索减少了4.6倍，并将准确率提高了高达12.4%（约4个百分点）。

Original abstract: Text2SQL agents powered by LLMs translate natural language intent into SQL by exploring the data system through tool calls before formulating the query. However, to ensure secure and scoped access, data systems construct environments with explicit API surfaces. We study and categorize these APIs exposed today as either coarse-grained or fine-grained and posit that choosing between them presents a fundamental tradeoff between cost-efficient exploration and accurate SQL generation. Most data systems expose fine-grained APIs, but this inadvertently disadvantages agents: they over-explore, incorporating irrelevant schema elements into their query formulation and produce inaccurate results. We argue that curbing over-exploration is key to the effective use of these API surfaces, and propose Sophrosyne, a data system environment that augments API responses with directives that guide the agent's exploration process. Initial results show that directives reduce over-exploration by 4.6x and boost accuracy by up to 12.4% (approx. 4 percentage points).

</details>


### [95] [SpecDB: LLM-Generated Customized Databases via Feature-Oriented Decomposition](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31097v1)
*Yunkai Lou,Longbin Lai,Shunyang Li,Zhengping Qian,Ying Zhang*

Main category: cs.DB

Selection reason: 使用LLM agent生成定制数据库，多agent协作，直接相关coding agent。

TL;DR: SpecDB利用LLM根据工作负载描述自动合成定制关系型数据库，生成的数据库在TPC-C上性能与PostgreSQL和MySQL相当，但代码量仅为它们的3%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 主流数据库提供统一功能集，但工作负载只用部分功能，造成冗余和低效；能否根据工作负载按需生成定制数据库？

Method: 提出SpecDB，用FODA模型扩展合作边形成依赖图DBGraph，分层模块构建管道，子代理（主、测试、架构）生成和验证模块，精炼代理迭代修复，选择组件将自然语言描述转为实现变体。

Result: 生成的Rust数据库（23,779行）在TPC-C 10仓库下tpmC=130（PostgreSQL 128，MySQL 127），零错误，延迟相当，代码大小约3%。

Conclusion: LLM可有效合成定制数据库，成本下降使该方案可行，能跨系统组合技术。

中文摘要：主流关系型数据库在部署中提供统一的功能集，尽管单个工作负载仅使用可用子系统的一小部分。我们研究是否可以根据需求生成一个数据库，其功能集与目标工作负载匹配。我们提出SpecDB，一个使用大型语言模型（LLM）来合成定制关系型数据库的系统。我们调查了9个生产系统，并将它们分解为10个功能模块，每个模块进一步分为实现变体。为了捕获跨模块依赖性，包括在不相交子树中的实现必须协同设计的情况，我们采用FODA特征模型并扩展了合作边，得到依赖图DBGraph。SpecDB通过一个分层模块构建管道来操作化DBGraph，其中每个模块由专门的子代理（由三个内部代理驱动：主代理、测试代理、架构代理）生成、验证和集成，还有一个精炼代理，它针对用户提供的精炼工具有迭代地修复和调整组装好的数据库，该工具对现有数据库源代码具有只读访问权限。一个配套的选择组件将自然语言工作负载描述翻译成一组实现变体，提供了从工作负载描述到可部署数据库的端到端管道。我们在TPC-C上使用BenchmarkSQL评估SpecDB。生成的数据库（23,779行Rust代码）在1个和10个仓库上完成了60分钟的TPC-C，零错误。在10个仓库时，它达到了tpmC=130，而PostgreSQL为128，MySQL为127，延迟相当，代码大小约为它们的3%。由于代理在模块规范级别而非产品源代码级别操作，它原则上可以跨系统边界组合技术。随着LLM成本下降，为目标工作负载生成专用数据库正变得简单。

Original abstract: Mainstream relational databases ship a uniform feature set across deployments, although individual workloads exercise only a fraction of the available subsystems. We investigate whether a database can instead be generated on demand with a feature set matched to the target workload. We present SpecDB, a system that uses large language models (LLMs) to synthesize customized relational databases. We survey 9 production systems and decompose them into 10 functional modules, each further divided into implementation variants. To capture cross-module dependencies, including cases where implementations in disjoint subtrees must be co-designed, we adopt the FODA feature model and extend it with a cooperate edge, yielding a dependency graph DBGraph. SpecDB operationalizes DBGraph through a layered module-construction pipeline in which each module is generated, validated, and integrated by a dedicated subagent (driven by three inner agents: Main, Tester, Architect), and a Refining Agent that iteratively repairs and tunes the assembled database against a user-supplied refining harness with read-only access to existing database source code. A companion selection component translates a natural-language workload description into a set of implementation variants, providing an end-to-end pipeline from workload description to deployable database. We evaluate SpecDB on TPC-C with BenchmarkSQL. The generated database (23,779 lines of Rust) completes 60-minute TPC-C at 1 and 10 warehouses with zero errors. At 10 warehouses it reaches tpmC=130, compared to 128 for PostgreSQL and 127 for MySQL, with comparable latency at ~3% of their code size. Because the agent operates at module-specification level rather than product source, it can in principle combine techniques across system boundaries. Paired with falling LLM costs, generating a purpose-built database for a target workload is becoming straightforward.

</details>


<div id='cs.RO'></div>

# cs.RO [[Back]](#toc)

### [96] [GSAM: A Generalizable and Safe Robotic Framework for Articulated Object Manipulation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30740v1)
*Beichen Shao,Mengying Xie,Heng Su,Wanyi Zhang,Mingyan Li,Yan Ding,Fausto Giunchiglia,Chao Chen*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 机器人操作中LLM规划与约束推理，可迁移agent规划方法。

TL;DR: 提出GSAM框架，通过视觉感知、VLM常识推理和LLM约束规划，实现通用且安全的关节物体操作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法忽视关节物体多样性和交互复杂性，导致泛化差和碰撞问题。

Method: 包含视觉感知器生成运动学参数、VLM优化器利用COT推理优化感知、交互约束函数生成器集成物体-姿态-避障知识、LLM函数化约束并规划轨迹与姿态、运动学操作规划器验证可达性。

Result: 在50个铰链任务中，标准差降低3.1%，操作成功率提高36.0%。

Conclusion: GSAM在物体泛化能力和交互安全性上显著优于基线，适用于实际场景。

中文摘要：关节物体操作是服务机器人面临的一个独特挑战。现有方法采用端到端策略学习、视觉-运动规划以及大语言/视觉语言模型（LLM/VLM），但往往忽略了关节物体的多样性和末端执行器与把手之间交互的复杂性，导致泛化能力有限和破坏性碰撞。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了GSAM，一个通用且安全的机器人关节物体操作框架。具体来说，一个基于视觉的感知器生成运动学参数。考虑到感知器中预训练标记产生的原始估计可能偏离常识，我们提出了一个微调的基于VLM的优化器，使用思维链（COT）常识推理来优化感知。为了防止破坏性碰撞，我们设计了一个交互约束函数生成器，将关节物体、交互姿态和避障知识集成到一个基础中。然后LLM将这些约束函数化并应用于轨迹和姿态规划。一个运动学感知的操作规划器验证轨迹和姿态的可达性。在5个物体类别的50个铰链任务和50个随机初始化的末端执行器-把手配置上的实验表明，与最佳基线相比，GSAM将标准差降低了3.1%，并将操作成功率提高了36.0%，分别证明了GSAM在实际场景中的优越物体泛化能力和交互安全性。

Original abstract: Articulated object manipulation is a unique challenge for service robots. Existing methods employ end-to-end policy learning, visionmotion planning, and large-language/visual-language model (LLM/VLM), but often overlook the diversity of articulated objects and the complexity of interactions between end-effector and handle, leading to limited generalization and destructive collisions. To address this, we propose GSAM, a generalizable and safe robotic framework for articulated object manipulation. Specifically, a vision-based perceiver generates the kinematic parameters. Considering that pre-trained markers in perceiver yield raw estimations that may deviate from commonsense, we present a f ine-tuned VLM-based refiner, using chain-of-thought (COT) commonsense reasoning to refine perception. To prevent destructive collisions, we design an interaction constraint function generator, integrating articulated object, interaction pose, and obstacle avoidance knowledge into a base. LLM then functionalize these constraints and apply them to trajectory and posture planning. A kinematic-aware manipulation planner verifies reachability for trajectory and posture. Experiments on 50 hinge tasks across 5 object categories and 50 randomly initialized end-effectorhandle configurations show that GSAM reduces standard deviation by 3.1% and improves manipulation success rate by 36.0% compared to the best baseline, respectively demonstrating the superior object generalization and interaction safety of GSAM in practical scenarios.

</details>


### [97] [Completion at the Boundary (CaB): Deployable Switching with Completion-Aware Control under Limited Calibration](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00145v1)
*Yusuke Sano,Takeshi Itoga*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 提出CaB完成检测与切换机制，可迁移至agent长程任务控制。

TL;DR: CaB通过边界阶段令牌（Before/Hit/After）保留双边边界证据，并利用CaB-When和CaB-How分别实现切换决策和动作生成，从而在低校准VLA场景中提高组合指令完成和交接质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLA系统缺乏决定指令何时完成的接口，尤其在短组合指令中交接时机不当导致失败。在低校准约束下，将不对称边界证据压缩为单标量脆弱。

Method: 提出CaB，预测边界阶段令牌（Before/Hit/After）作为事件局部的完成对象，保留双边证据。CaB-When用于切换决策，CaB-How用于动作生成。

Result: 在Minecraft VLA基准上，CaB提高组合执行和交接质量。

Conclusion: CaB在低校准约束下有效改进VLA组合指令完成。

中文摘要：视觉-语言-动作（VLA）智能体可以执行自然语言指令，但已部署的系统仍然缺乏一个操作接口：决定何时指令完成。这一差距在短组合指令（如“做A，然后做B”）中尤为突出，因为时机不当的交接会导致下游故障的级联。完成本质上是闭环的，因为切换是一种干预，会改变指令上下文，从而影响未来的动作和观察。我们在一个可部署的低校准机制下研究完成问题，该机制受开放式指令空间的启发，强制要求无测试时重新学习，并且只选择一个在开发集上确定并在测试集上原样复用的全局校准切换规则。在这种约束下，将不对称的边界证据压缩成单个标量在跨任务极性变化时可能会变得脆弱。我们提出了边界完成（Completion at the Boundary, CaB），它预测一个事件局部的完成对象，形式为边界阶段令牌（之前/命中/之后），在这种规则下保留双边边界证据。CaB-When将这个完成对象转换为一个最小、可审计的切换决策（何时），而CaB-How则重用相同的完成对象来调节动作生成，以实现通过交接的边界稳定控制（如何）。使用一个干预感知的E1/E2协议，我们展示了CaB在匹配容量和可部署性约束下，在第一人称Minecraft VLA基准测试上提高了组合执行和交接质量。

Original abstract: Vision-language-action (VLA) agents can execute natural-language instructions, yet deployed systems still lack an operational interface: deciding when the instruction is complete. This gap is acute in short composites ("do A, then B"), where mistimed handoffs cascade into downstream failures. Completion is inherently closed-loop because switching is an intervention that changes the instruction context and thus future actions and observations. We study completion under a deployable low-calibration regime motivated by open-ended instruction spaces, enforcing no test-time relearning and a single globally calibrated switching rule selected once on development set and reused unchanged on test set. Under this constraint, collapsing asymmetric boundary evidence into a single scalar can be brittle under polarity shifts across tasks. We propose Completion at the Boundary (CaB), which predicts an event-local completion object in the form of Boundary-Phase Tokens (Before/Hit/After), retaining two-sided boundary evidence under this discipline. CaB-When converts this completion object into a minimal, auditable switching decision (when), while CaB-How reuses the same completion object to condition action generation for boundary-stable control through handoffs (how). Using an intervention-aware E1/E2 protocol, we show that CaB improves composite execution and handoff quality on a first-person Minecraft VLA benchmark under matched capacity and deployability constraints.

### [98] [Hide-and-Seek in Trajectories: Discovering Failure Signals for VLA Runtime Monitoring](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30834v1)
*Seongheon Park,Wendi Li,Changdae Oh,Samuel Yeh,Zsolt Kira,Michael Hagenow,Sharon Li*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: VLA失败检测框架，对比学习与轨迹级监督，可迁移至agent运行时监控与自我改进。

TL;DR: 提出Hide-and-Seek框架，将VLA失败检测转化为粗监督学习，通过轨迹级对比学习定位失败动作，无需步骤级标注，实现SOTA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VLA模型执行失败检测对可靠部署至关重要，现有方法要么昂贵要么掩盖局部失败信号。

Method: 提出Hide-and-Seek框架，结合轨迹间和轨迹内对比目标，从轨迹级监督中学习时间结构化的失败信号。

Result: 在LIBERO、VLABench和真实平台上，对三种VLA策略实现SOTA多任务失败检测性能，具有实用准确性-及时性权衡。

Conclusion: Hide-and-Seek有效检测VLA执行失败，无需步骤级标注，泛化良好。

中文摘要：Vision-Language-Action (VLA) 模型使机器人能够遵循自然语言指令并在不同任务间泛化，但在实际部署中仍然容易受到执行失败的影响，从而影响可靠性。因此，在执行过程中检测此类失败对于鲁棒部署具身系统至关重要。现有的失败检测方法要么依赖昂贵的动作重采样或外部模型，要么将轨迹级标签均匀传播到每个时间步，从而掩盖了局部失败信号。在本文中，我们提出了 Hide-and-Seek，一个将VLA失败检测公式化为粗监督学习问题的框架。通过结合轨迹间和轨迹内对比目标，Hide-and-Seek 能够定位指示失败的动作，并仅从轨迹级监督中诱导出时间结构的失败信号，无需任何步骤级标注。我们在 LIBERO、VLABench 和真实机器人平台上对三种代表性VLA策略（OpenVLA、π₀ 和 π₀.₅）评估了 Hide-and-Seek。我们的方法在保形预测下实现了具有实用准确性-及时性权衡的最先进的多任务失败检测性能，并且对见过的和未见的任务都能很好地泛化。

Original abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models enable robots to follow natural language instructions and generalize across diverse tasks, but they remain vulnerable to execution failures that compromise reliability in real-world deployment. Detecting such failures during execution is therefore critical for the robust deployment of embodied systems. Existing failure detection methods either rely on expensive action resampling or external models, while alternatives propagate trajectory-level labels uniformly across every timestep, obscuring localized failure signals. In this paper, we propose \textbf{Hide-and-Seek}, a framework that formulates VLA failure detection as a coarsely supervised learning problem. By combining inter-trajectory and intra-trajectory contrastive objectives, Hide-and-Seek localizes failure-indicative actions and induces temporally structured failure signals from trajectory-level supervision alone, without any step-level annotation. We evaluate Hide-and-Seek on LIBERO, VLABench, and a real-world robotic platform across three representative VLA policies: OpenVLA, $π_0$, and $π_{0.5}$.Our method achieves state-of-the-art multi-task failure detection performance with a practical accuracy--timeliness trade-off under conformal prediction, and generalizes well to both seen and unseen tasks.

</details>


### [99] [TARIC: Memory-Augmented Traversability-Aware Outdoor VLN under Interrupted Semantic Cues](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31121v1)
*Tianle Zeng,Hanjing Ye,Jianwei Peng,Jingwen Yu,Hanxuan Chen,Hong Zhang*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 户外VLN agent，含记忆与规划，可迁移至coding agent的导航启发。

TL;DR: 提出一种统一室外VLN框架，通过可通行性一致的引导和3D线索记忆，在长时间无线索阶段保持目标导向，在模拟和真实环境中显著提升成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 室外VLN中语义线索中断导致智能体退化为回溯或探索，现有记忆方法在可通行性驱动的绕行中失败，需要可通行性作为维持目标引导的稳定性条件。

Method: 提取可见性门控线索的语义方位，利用实时近场可通行性剖面落实为可执行朝向；将间歇2D证据提升为世界对齐3D线索记忆，使用不确定性感知读取机制。

Result: 在四足和轮式平台上，模拟成功率提升超10个百分点，真实世界成功率40%（基线17.5%），长时间无线索间隔鲁棒性显著提高。

Conclusion: 所提框架有效应对语义线索中断，通过可通行性一致的引导和3D记忆显著提升室外VLN性能。

中文摘要：在长距离、开放世界环境中的室外视觉-语言导航（VLN）经常受到语义线索中断的干扰，即信息丰富的目标线索变得稀疏、被遮挡或离开视野。一旦这类线索消失，智能体进入无线索阶段，常常退化为回溯、振荡性朝向或漫无目的的探索。虽然基于记忆的方法试图弥合这些间隙，但它们通常在受可通行性驱动的绕行中失败：记忆中的线索方向可能不可行，迫使绕行延长无线索阶段，并逐渐使机器人中心的线索过时且隐式历史模糊。这使得可通行性成为维持目标导向引导的稳定性条件，而不仅仅是局部的安全问题。我们提出一个统一的室外VLN框架，通过在整个长时间无线索阶段维持可通行性一致的可执行引导，从而在语义线索中断中存活。具体来说，我们的方法从可见性门控的目标或探索线索中提取语义方位，并使用实时近场可通行性剖面将其落实为可执行的朝向，提供目标一致且可行的引导，超越仅拒绝的安全过滤。为防止绕行期间引导退化，我们将间歇性的2D证据提升为世界对齐的3D线索记忆，并配备不确定性感知的读取机制，确保引导在机器人移动时持续可达且稳定。我们在四足和轮式平台上评估该框架，路线长度为600-1000米。我们的方法在模拟中比最强基线提高了超过10个百分点的成功率，并在真实世界中达到了40%的成功率，而最强基线为17.5%，在长时间无线索间隔期间具有显著更高的鲁棒性。

Original abstract: Outdoor vision-language navigation (VLN) in long-range, open-world environments is frequently disrupted by semantic-cue interruptions, where informative goal cues become sparse, occluded, or leave the field of view. Once such cues disappear, agents enter a cue-free phase and often degrade into backtracking, oscillatory headings, or aimless exploration. While memory-based methods attempt to bridge these gaps, they often fail under traversability-driven detours: the remembered cue direction may be infeasible, forcing detours that prolong cue-free phases and gradually render robot-centric cues stale and implicit histories blurred. This makes traversability a stability condition for maintaining goal-directed guidance, rather than merely a local safety concern.
  We propose a unified outdoor VLN framework that survives semantic-cue interruptions by maintaining traversability-consistent executable guidance throughout prolonged cue-free phases. Specifically, our method extracts semantic bearings from visibility-gated goal or exploration cues and grounds them into executable headings using a real-time near-field traversability profile, providing goal-consistent feasible guidance beyond reject-only safety filtering. To prevent guidance degradation during detours, we lift intermittent 2D evidence into a world-aligned 3D cue memory with an uncertainty-aware readout mechanism, ensuring guidance remains continuously reachable and stable as the robot moves.
  We evaluate the framework on quadrupedal and wheeled platforms over 600--1000 m routes. Our method improves simulation success rate by over 10 percentage points over the strongest baseline and achieves a real-world success rate of 40%, compared to 17.5% for the strongest baseline, with substantially higher robustness during prolonged cue-free intervals.

</details>


### [100] [Continuous Reasoning for Vision-Language-Action](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00229v2)
*Yueh-Hua Wu,Tatsuya Matsushima,Kei Ota*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: VLA agent的连续推理介质，可迁移到agent推理设计。

TL;DR: 提出连续推理方法，通过可共享、可验证的连续思维改善视觉-语言-动作模型的行动控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自然语言与连续控制的粒度不匹配，现有VLA方法中语言推理与细粒度动作选择弱耦合，需要一个可共享、可验证且对齐时间扩展控制结构的推理媒介。

Method: 提出连续推理模型，先预测一组结构化连续思维作为高斯潜在变量，再将其作为共享上下文生成分块动作。通过自验证目标训练，使用指数移动平均教师网络消费学生推理来预测目标动作。

Result: 在LIBERO-PRO上提升鲁棒性，在真实机器人实验中，TX-G2上平均子任务成功率较π0.5提升40.4%，HSR上提升26.3%。

Conclusion: VLA中的推理关键在于可共享、可验证的内部动作语言，而非增加额外令牌。

中文摘要：自然语言是语言和视觉-语言模型的一种强大推理媒介，但它与连续控制的粒度不匹配。文本和显式子目标在任务级粒度上操作，而视觉-语言-动作（VLA）策略必须在更精细的时间尺度上选择动作；因此，单个推理步骤可能跨越多个动作块，同时与当前所需的动作保持弱耦合。这为VLA提出了一个不同的问题：什么应该扮演语言的角色？我们认为，有用的VLA推理媒介必须能够在模型实例之间共享，通过下游动作改进进行验证，并与时间上扩展的控制结构对齐。基于这一观点，我们提出了用于视觉-语言-动作的连续推理。我们的模型首先以结构化连续思维集合的形式预测连续推理，然后将其作为共享上下文用于分块动作生成。仅凭更好的动作预测并不能证明推理良好：如果相同的内部媒介不能在模型实例之间共享，并且不能通过改进的下游控制独立验证，那么添加的潜在变量可能只是模型私有的捷径，有助于在已见行为上表现，但不支持可泛化的控制。因此，我们将连续推理实例化为共享的高斯潜在接口，并使用自验证目标进行训练，其中指数移动平均教师必须在预测目标动作时成功消耗学生的推理。实验上，连续推理提高了LIBERO-PRO的鲁棒性，并在真实机器人上表现强劲，在TX-G2（与AgiBot G2兼容的变体）上将平均子任务成功率相较于π0.5提高了40.4%，在HSR上提高了26.3%。这表明VLA中的推理更多关乎可共享、可验证的内部动作语言，而非额外的令牌。

Original abstract: Natural language is a powerful reasoning medium for language and vision-language models, but it is mismatched to the granularity of continuous control. Text and explicit subgoals operate at task-level granularity, whereas vision-language-action (VLA) policies must choose actions at a much finer temporal scale; a single reasoning step can therefore span many action chunks while remaining only weakly coupled to the action needed now. This suggests a different question for VLA: what should play the role of language? We argue that a useful VLA reasoning medium must be shareable across model instances, verifiable through downstream action improvement, and aligned with temporally extended control structure.
  Based on this view, we propose Continuous Reasoning for Vision-Language-Action. Our model first predicts continuous reasoning in the form of a structured set of continuous thoughts, then reuses them as shared context for chunk-structured action generation. Better action prediction alone does not certify good reasoning: if the same internal medium cannot be shared across model instances and independently verified through improved downstream control, the added latent may simply become a model-private shortcut that helps on seen behaviors without supporting generalizable control. We therefore instantiate continuous reasoning as a shared Gaussian latent interface and train it with a self-verification objective in which an exponential-moving-average teacher must successfully consume the student's reasoning when predicting target actions.
  Empirically, Continuous Reasoning improves LIBERO-PRO robustness and performs strongly on real robots, raising mean subtask success over π0.5 by 40.4% on TX-G2, an AgiBot G2-compatible variant, and 26.3% on HSR. This suggests that reasoning in VLA is less about extra tokens than about a shareable, verifiable internal language for action.

</details>


### [101] [Physical Atari: A Robust and Accessible Platform for Real-time Reinforcement Learning on Robots](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19357v1)
*Khurram Javed,Joseph Modayil,Gloria Kennickell,Richard S. Sutton,John Carmack*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 构建物理 Atari 平台验证强化学习算法，对 agent 在物理世界部署与自适应有启发。

TL;DR: Physical Atari是一个低成本、鲁棒的物理强化学习平台，验证了算法可直接在机器人上学习，且分布偏移会显著降低性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 需要一个鲁棒且可访问的物理世界平台来研究强化学习算法。

Method: 构建Robotroller（通过轴承减少磨损）和Atari Devbox，使用现成摄像头和电脑，高频监控伺服电机并干预，采用低成本组件和3D打印零件。

Result: 系统成本低于$1000，可连续数周无故障运行；验证了算法可直接学习，但分布偏移显著降低性能。

Conclusion: 设备上自适应对于机器人策略性能至关重要。

中文摘要：我们构建了一个名为Robotroller的机器人，它可以驱动Atari CX40+控制器，以及一个名为Atari Devbox的设备，该设备在屏幕上渲染来自Arcade Learning Environment的游戏画面和奖励信号。Robotroller和Atari Devbox，加上一个现成的摄像头和一台台式计算机，构成一个可用于在物理世界中研究强化学习算法的系统。我们将整个系统称为Physical Atari。在本文中，我们详细介绍了使Physical Atari成为一个鲁棒且可访问平台的关键决策。为了增强系统的鲁棒性，我们设计了Robotroller，使其所有运动通过轴承实现，从而减少磨损。此外，我们编写了软件，高频监控伺服电机状态并在必要时进行干预以限制应力。为了使其易于获取，我们使用了价格合理的现成组件和可通过消费级3D打印机打印的零件。Physical Atari的建造成本低于1000美元，并已用于连续数周的强化学习实验而没有任何机械故障。我们利用它验证了强化学习算法可以直接在机器人上学习，并表明即使学习和部署之间的微小分布偏移也会显著降低策略的性能。我们的结果强调了设备上自适应对于在机器人上获得强性能的重要性。

Original abstract: We built a robot called the Robotroller that actuates an Atari CX40+ controller and a device called the Atari Devbox that renders the game frame and the reward signal from the Arcade Learning Environment on a screen. The Robotroller and the Atari Devbox, together with an off-the-shelf camera and a desktop computer, constitute a system that can be used to study reinforcement learning algorithms in the physical world. We call the full system Physical Atari. In this paper, we detail the key decisions that make Physical Atari a robust and accessible platform. To make the system robust, we designed the Robotroller so that all movement is done through bearings, which reduces wear. Additionally, we wrote software that monitors the state of the servos at a high frequency and intervenes to limit stress. To make the system accessible, we used affordable off-the-shelf components and parts that can be manufactured using consumer 3D printers. Physical Atari can be built for under $1,000 and has been used for weeks of non-stop reinforcement learning experiments without any mechanical failures. We used it to validate that reinforcement learning algorithms can learn directly on robots and show that even small distribution shifts between learning and deployment can significantly degrade the performance of policies. Our results underscore the importance of on-device adaptation for strong performance on robots.

</details>
